Ibihugu bya Afurika buri gihe usanga bigarukwaho mu itangazamakuru ry'abo """" bavuga ko bageze kuri demokarasi """" bigaragazwa nk'ahari kubera ihonyorwa ry'uburenganzira bwa muntu , intambara , indiri y'imitwe y'iterabwoba , ibyorezo n'inzara ; ukagira ngo ni nk'imbabare itabarizwa .
Nko mu Bufaransa by'umwihariko , isura y'u Rwanda mu mboni zabwo ntiyakunze kuba nziza bitewe ahanini n'uruhare abari abayobozi babwo bashinjwa kugira muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 , nyuma bakajya no mu murongo wo kuyihakana no kutavuga ukuri kuri yo .
Ibyo byatumye n'abanyamakuru baho bagendera muri uwo mujyo , kuvuga ibyiza by'u Rwanda bigasa n'ibitabaho .
Buri wese wumvise ko itangazamakuru ry'Abafaransa ryavuze ibyiza by'u Rwanda ntiyabura kugwa mu kantu .
Ibyo ariko birashoboka kuko mu nshuro nke bibaho n'iy'uyu munsi irazamo .
Ikiganiro Echappées Belles gica kuri Televiziyo ya France 5 buri wa Gatandatu kuva ku wa 30 Ukuboza mu 2006 , kiraza kwerekana ibyiza u Rwanda rumaze kugeraho mu rugendo rw'imyaka 27 rwiyubaka .
Kiraba Saa 20 : 50 z'i Paris , saa 21 : 50 z'i Kigali .
Ni ikiganiro gisanzwe kigaragaza agace , igihugu cyangwa akarere runaka n'icyerekezo cyaho .
Gikorwa n'abanyamakuru b'Abafaransa barimo Sophie Jovillard wanagitangije , akagikorana na Tiga ukomoka muri Bénin , Ismaël Khelifa na Jérôme Pitorin .
Mu itegurwa ryacyo , abo banyamakuru bakora urugendo bakajya gusura agace kadakunze kuvugwaho ibyiza ( akenshi basura agace kari kure y'u Bufaransa ) , bakareba icyerekezo cyako n'ibihari byihariye bidakunze kuboneka ahandi , maze bakabyereka abagikurikira .
Mu minota 60 yacyo yo kuri uyu wa Gatandatu tariki 6 Werurwe 2021 , Jovillard arerekana u Rwanda n'iterambere rumaze kugeraho n'ubwiza rufite mu myaka 27 rumaze rushegeshwe na Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 , aho yibanda ku guteza imbere abagore banagaragara cyane mu nzego nkuru z'igihugu .
Arabyerekanira mu mashusho arimo ayafatiwe mu Majyaruguru y'u Rwanda muri Pariki y'Ibirunga , Jovillard atemberana na Nyirakaragire Natalie wabaye umuganga wa mbere w'inyamaswa zo muri iyo pariki .
Haragaragaramo uko Abanyarwandakazi bari mu rwego rw'abikorera bageze kuri 40 % , intambwe ikomeye itaraterwa n'ibindi bihugu byitwa ko bikomeye nk'u Bufaransa kuko bwo bufite 27 % .
Muri Echappées Belles y'uyu munsi kandi haragaragarizwamo uko u Rwanda ruri kubaka ubukungu bushingiye ku ikoranabuhanga hahangwa imishinga myinshi izana udushya muri urwo rwego , ari nako rwongera ingamba zo kurengera ibidukikije .
Intambwe yo kuba rwaraciye umuco wo gupfunyika mu mashashi hakifashishwa ibindi bikoresho ni hake yatewe , naho ikoranabuhanga ryo gutwara amaraso ku bitaro bitandukanye hifashishijwe Drones ni ibigwi .
Mu mashusho y'umunota umwe yashyizwe kuri YouTube na Facebook bya Echappées Belles , Sophie Jovillard yakumbuje abantu icyo kiganiro abararikira kudacikanwa kuko cyerekana ibyiza nyaburanga by'u Rwanda birimo ikiyaga cya Kivu n'inyamaswa zo muri Pariki ya Akagera .
Ati """" Mwaramutse nshuti !
Mwitegure tujyane mu rugendo rudasanzwe , mwese muhawe ikaze mu Rwanda , ahari ubwiza bushya butuma bamwe barubonamo Singapore ya Afurika , naho abandi bakarwita u Busuwisi bwo muri Afurika . """"
Yavuze ko u Rwanda ari ruto mu ngano ariko rukaba """" rugari bitewe n'ubwiza """" bwarwo , ashimangira ko nyuma y'ihungabana rwasigiwe n'amateka mabi """" ubu abarutuye babanye mu mahoro . """"
Yakomeje ati """" Ruriya ni urugero rw'abantu bakize ibikomere , mu by'ukuri ndumva nshaka kuhatemberana namwe .
Nsubiyemo nti """" ikaze kuri mwese . """"
Murakaza neza mu Rwanda . """"
Abashaka gutembera no kumenya Umujyi wa Kigali bashyizwe igorora .
Uwageze muri uyu mujyi ntiyifuza gutaha kubera ibyiza byinshi birimo imiturirwa myiza , amahoteli yo ku rwego rwo hejuru , ubusitani burimo ibiti bitanga umwuka mwiza n'ibindi byinshi binogera ijisho ry'abawugezemo .
Abawugenda bakoresha uburyo butandukanye butuma babasha kwirebera ibyiza biwugize , hari abagenda n'amaguru cyangwa abakoresha imodoka zabo biterwa n'icyo bashimye .
Mu gukomeza korohereza abatembera uyu Mujyi , Kigali City Tour yazanye imodoka nini zifasha abantu kureba no kumenya neza Umujyi wa Kigali batavunitse .
Iyi modoka nini ikoze mu buryo bugeretse ku buryo ushaka kurebera Kigali ahirengeye ayibona ndetse no hasi akayibona , ikaba ikora ingendo zitandukanye buri munsi mu Mujyi wa Kigali .
Iyi modoka ihagurukira kuri Kigali Arena ikazenguruka hirya no hino mu duce two muri Kigali nka Kimironko , Kibagabaga , Rebero , mu mujyi rwa gati no mu tundi duce tw'umujyi .
Abashaka gutembera bashobora kugenda mu modoka ya mu gitondo cyangwa ihaguruka nyuma ya saa Sita , bakagenda basobanurirwa byinshi kuri Kigali buri wese yishyuye ibihumbi 10frw gusa akaza no guhabwa ibyo kurya .
Akarusho kandi n'uko abashaka gutegura ibirori kandi banagenda bashobora kwishyira hamwe iyi modoka ikabatembereza bari no kwishimisha mu birori byabo .
Ushinzwe guteza imbere ubucuruzi muri Kigali City Tour , Hassan Yakubu Mapesa , yavuze ko izi modoka zazanywe mu Mujyi wa Kigali mu gufasha abashaka kuwumenya ndetse no guteza imbere ubukerarugendo butandukanye ku buryo abantu bishimisha mu buryo butandukanye .
Ati """" Izi modoka zifasha abantu kumenya Kigali ndetse no gusobanukirwa amateka yayo , ku buryo umuntu wakoze urugendo ataha yamenye byinshi kandi yanishimye yafashe amafoto meza n'ibindi byinshi byiza yabibonye . """"
Si abo mu Mujyi wa Kigali gusa kuko ushaka kwishimana n'abawe mushobora kwishyira hamwe ku buryo babatembereza aho mushaka hose mu gihugu .
Mantis uBuranga , ubwato bw'akataraboneka buzakora nka hotel mu Kivu bugiye gutahwa .
Ubu bwato bwiswe Mantis Kivu Queen uBuranga byari biteganyijwe ko buzatangira gukora mu kwezi kwa Kane uyu mwaka , ariko kubera imbogamizi zitandukanye zatewe n'icyorezo cya Covid - 19 , imirimo yo kubaka yagiye idindira .
Umuyobozi uhagarariye ibikorwa bya Mantis mu Rwanda , Dino Urbani , yabwiye IGIHE ko bataramenya neza igihe buzarangirira ariko bateganya ko buzatangira gukoreshwa mu kwezi kwa Karindwi .
Ati """" Ntituramenya neza igihe ubwato buzaba bwarangiye , bityo sinakubwira ngo ni iyi tariki , cyangwa ni uku kwezi [ . . . ] gusa turifuza ko mu kwezi kwa Karindwi bwaba bwarangiye . """"
Yakomeje avuga ko nyuma y'ukwezi n'igice ni ukuvuga mu mpera za Werurwe , hazaba hamenyekanye igihe nyacyo buzaba bwarangiye .
Ibikoresho byo kubaka ubu bwato bituruka muri Afurika y'Epfo bigateranyirizwa mu Rwanda .
Dino yakomeje agira ati """" Twahuye n'imbogamizi nyinshi , kubera Covid - 19 ibintu byose byarafunze , nta kintu cyavaga mu gihugu kimwe kijya mu kindi [ . . . ] imvura nyinshi yaraguye muri Kibuye abantu ntibabona uko bakora bituma ibikorwa bitinda . """"
Yakomeje avuga ko uretse izo mbogamizi bahuye nazo , ibikorwa byo kubaka byasubukuwe ndetse ko hari gutegurwa aho ubwato buzakorera , kandi ko hari gushyirwamo imbaraga nyinshi kugira ngo burangire .
Mantis Kivu Queen uBuranga ni ubwato buzaba bufite ibyumba bigezweho ( cabin ) icumi , kimwe gishobora kwakira abantu bo ku rwego rwo rw'abakuru b'ibihugu n'ikindi cy'abanyacyubahiro basanzwe .
Buri cyumba kizaba kirimo ikintu cyose umuntu yakenera , nk'uko nyine yaba ari muri Hotel , ni ukuvuga ubwiherero n'ubwogero , ibyuma bitanga ubushyuhe n'ubukonje , televiziyo , restaurant , bar , n'ibindi bitandukanye .
Ubu bwato buri kubakwa na sosiyete yo muri Afurika y'Epfo yitwa AfriNest , imikorere yabwo ikazagenzurwa na Mantis izobereye mu gucunga amahoteli .
Mantis isanzwe ifite hotel mu Rwanda mu Karere ka Rusizi nayo yo ku rwego rwo hejuru .
Yitwa Mantis Kivu Marina Bay , ifite ibyumba 79 birimo kimwe gishobora kwakira nk'Umukuru w'Igihugu .
Ubushobozi bwo kwitunga bwa Pariki y'Akagera bwaragabanyutse cyane kubera Covid - 19 .
Imibare yatangajwe n'iyi Pariki igaragaza ko mu 2019 yasuwe n'abakerarugendo barenga 50 000 , mu gihe mu 2020 yasuwe n'abagera ku 15 844 gusa , ni ukuvuga ko bagabanutseho 68 % .
Ushinzwe Ubukerarugendo n'Imenyekanishabikorwa muri Pariki y'Igihugu y'Akagera , Karinganire Jean Paul yabwiye IGIHE ko kimwe n'izindi nzego zose , urwego rw'ubukerarugendo narwo rwagizweho ingaruka cyane n'icyorezo cya COVID - 19 , bikaba byaratumye amafaranga ava mu bukerarugendo yinjizwaga na pariki y'Akagera
agabanuka cyane .
Yagize ati """" Ugereranyije ukwezi na Mutarama 2020 n'ukwezi kwa Mutarama 2021 , harimo ikinyuranyo kinini cyane cy'igabanuka , bitewe na none n'uko abakerarugendo batakigenda nk'uko bagendaga COVID itaraza n'ubundi haracyariho COVID - 19 , ibihugu byinshi byo mu Burayi byashyizeho Guma mu rugo , abaturage babyo ntabwo
babasha gutembera nk'uko batemberaga . """"
Kuva muri Werurwe 2020 COVID - 19 igeze mu Rwanda , ibikorwa by'ubukerarugendo byahise bihagarikwa , byongera gusubukurwa muri Kamena ubwo abantu bari bavuye muri Guma mu rugo .
Karinganire yavuze ko n'ubwo ibikorwa by'ubukerarugendo byongeye gufungura , hakiri ikibazo cy'uko ibintu bitarasubira mu buryo , kuko ahenshi hakiri ingamba zo kwirinda zituma bidashoboka ko baza mu gihugu ku mpamvu z'ubukerarugendo .
Yagize ati """" Ingaruka za COVID - 19 n'ubundi ziracyariho uko ibihugu biracyafunze , n'ubwo ubukerarugendo bufunguye .
Abanyarwanda baraza , abanyamahanga batuye mu Rwanda baraza , ariko abanyamahanga bava mu mahanga bazanywe n'ubukerarugendo baragabanutse n'ubundi kubera Coronavirus . """"
Yakomeje avuga ko mu mibare y'abantu nta gihinduka cyane , ariko amafaranga ya pariki ava mu bukerarugendo ngo yo ariyongera , kuko nk'ayinjiye muri Mutarama uyu mwaka aruta ayinjiye muri Kamena na Nyakanga ndetse na Kamena 2020 , mu gihe mu Ukuboza ari bwo hinjiye menshi kuko mu Rwanda hari hafunguye n'abantu bashobora gutembera bisanzwe .
Pariki y'Akagera mu Ukuboza yinjije arenga miliyoni 120 Frw , mu gihe muri Mutarama yinjije arenga miliyoni 100 Frw .
Karinganire yavuze ko ingaruka za COVID - 19 kuri Pariki y'Akagera ari nyinshi cyane , kuko nk'umwaka wa 2019 yabashaga kwibonamo ubushobozi bungana na 90 % ikaba yari ifite intego yo kugera ku kigero cya 100 % ariko bigakomwa mu nkokora n'icyorezo , kuko kuri ubu ngo byasubiye inyuma bari ku kigero cya 34 % gusa .
Yavuze ko mu rwego rwo kurushaho guhangana n'izi ngaruka zatewe n'icyorezo bashyizeho poromosiyo ku Banyarwanda n'abandi banyamahanga baba mu Rwanda bifuza gusura pariki y'Akagera , aho bagabanyirijwe ibiciro byo kurara mu macumbi ( lodge ) agenzurwa n'iyi pariki ari yo ya Ruzizi na Karenge .
Kuri ubu ngo kurara muri rimwe muri ayo macumbi kuva ku ijoro rimwe kugera kuri atatu , ni 100 $ , mu gihe ngo mu bindi bihe byari 199 $ .
N'ubwo iyi pariki yahuye n'ibizazane mu mwaka ushize , yabashije kugira umwanya wo kunoza uburyo bwo kurushaho kwita ku nyamaswa ziri muri iyo pariki .
Mu mwaka ushize inzovu eshanu n'intare zambitswe utwuma dupima amerekezo ( GPS ) , ndetse n'inkura icyenda zashyizwemo """" transmitters , """" ibyo byose ni mu rwego rwo kumenya aho izo nyamaswa ziherereye ndetse n'uko zimeze mu rwego rwo kurushaho kuzitaho .
Mu mwaka ushize kandi muri iyi pariki hagaragaye ubwoko bushya bw'inyoni bwa """" Flamingo , """" Karinganire yavuze ko ari amahirwe bagize kuko ari zimwe mu nyoni ubundi zidakunda kuboneka .
Ati """" Ni ubwoko bw'inyoni buba budakunze kuhaza , izi rero flamingo ni imwe mu nyoni zidakunze kuba mu Akagera , iyo yaje iba yavuye nko muri Tanzania , iyo zibonetse biba ari amahirwe cyane , hari n'izo tuba dufata ko zanarangiye , kuzibona rero ni amahirwe . """"
Pariki y'Igihugu y'Akagera ni imwe mu zujuje inyamaswa zisurwa cyane kuri uyu mugabane , nyuma yo gusubizwamo Inkura n'Intare zari zarahacitse kubera ibikorwa bya muntu .
Ubu iyi pariki ibarizwamo inyamaswa zikomeye muri Afurika arizo Intare , Inzovu , Imbogo , Inkura n'Ingwe .
Mu mwaka wa 2020 abasura Pariki y'Akagera bagabanutseho 68 %
Pariki y'Akagera ivuga ko iyi mibare itari yitezwe ariko kubera icyorezo cya Coronavirus cyahungabanyije bikomeye uru rwego , bituma n'abayisura bagabanuka .
Mu mwaka wa 2019 iyo pariki yari yasuwe n'abakerarugendo 49 000 , yinjiza miliyoni 1 . 5 z'amadolari .
Ubuyobozi bw'iyi pariki bwatangaje ko umwaka ushize nta bantu basuye pariki ngo bahamare igihe kinini nkuko byakorwaga mbere ndetse n'abagiye bahaza , ntabwo bagiye bakoresha amafaranga menshi nkuko byahoze .
Pariki y'Igihugu y'Akagera ni imwe mu zujuje inyamaswa zisurwa cyane kuri uyu mugabane , nyuma yo gusubizwamo Inkura n'Intare zari zarahacitse kubera ibikorwa bya muntu .
Ubu iyi pariki ibarizwamo inyamaswa zikomeye muri Afurika arizo Intare , Inzovu , Imbogo , Inkura n'Ingwe .
Bisate Eco Lodge yashyizwe mu mahoteli 10 ya mbere ku Isi atangiza ibidukikije .
Uru rutonde rwakozwe n'Urubuga Elite Traveler , rwandika amakuru arebana n'ibintu bihenze kandi bigezweho , ubukerarugendo n'ibindi , rugaragaraho hoteli nziza kandi zigezweho hagendewe kuri buri mugabane .
Umugabane wa Afurika ufitemo hoteli ebyiri zirimo Bisate Eco Lodge yo mu Majyaruguru y'u Rwanda ndetse na Grootbos Private Nature Reserve yo muri Afurika y'Epfo .
Urubuga Elite Traveler ruvuga ko rwakoze uru rutonde mu rwego rwo gufasha ba mukerarugendo guhitamo aho bashobora kuruhukira hajyanye n'igihe kandi hatangiza ibidukikije .
Imiterere ya Bisate Lodge ituma ba mukerarugendo bizihirwa no kuharara .
Ni hoteli iri mu rwego rwa hoteli z'inyenyeri eshanu yatashywe ku mugaragaro na Perezida Paul Kagame ku wa 1 Nzeri 2017 .
Kuva iki gihe Bisate Eco Lodge yatangiye kwirahirwa n'abatari bacye barimo icyamamare mu mukino wa Tennis , Maria Sharapova wayirayemo igihe yasuraga u Rwanda mu 2019 .
Iyi hoteli yubatswe hagendewe ku muco Nyarwanda kuko uwayikoreye inyigo yagendeye ku buhanga bw'imyubakire gakondo ndetse n'ibirunga by'u Rwanda .
Igizwe n'inzu z'ibyatsi esheshatu , buri yose ifite ishusho ya kimwe mu birunga byo mu Rwanda ikaba ahitegeye ku gasozi keza kari mu ishyamba , ku buryo uburanga bw'imisozi iyikikije n'ikirere bituma uhari yumva umwihariko waho .
Uretse kuba ifite ishusho y'ibirunga nka Bisoke , Mikeno na Kalisimbi , urebye Bisate Lodge uhita kandi uyibonamo ishusho y'ingoro y'Umwami yo mu Rukari i Nyanza .
Urwego rw'Igihugu rushinzwe Iterambere ( RDB ) ruvuga ko kuba mu Rwanda harafunguwe Bisate Eco Lodge ari ikimenyetso ko umuhate w'igihugu mu kubungabunga ibikorwa bikurura ba mukerarugendo , amabwiriza yorohereza ishoramari ndetse na politiki iharanira impinduka nziza byatangiye gutanga umusaruro .
Kuba kandi iyi hoteli igenewe kwakira ba mukerarugendo bo ku rwego rwo hejuru bifuza kugirira ibihe byiza muri Pariki y'Ibirunga , ihorana abashyitsi bishyura amafaranga abarirwa muri miliyoni imwe y'amafaranga y'u Rwanda , bishimangira ko hari byinshi byisumbuye igihugu cyasangiza abaturutse mu mahanga .
Uretse Bisate Eco Lodge , u Rwanda rufite n'izindi hoteli zubatswe mu buryo bugabanya ingaruka mbi ku bidukikije zigera ku 10 zirimo nka Inzu Logde iri mu Karere ka Rubavu , intego akaba ari ukubaka izindi nyinshi .
Urutonde rwa Elite Traveler rugaragaraho izindi hoteli zifite umwihariko wo kutangiza ibidukikije nka Pikaia Lodge yo mu Birwa bya Galápagos , Habitas Tulum yo muri Mexique , Whitepod yo mu Busuwisi , Borgo Pignano yo mu Butaliyani , Song Saa Private Island Resort yo muri Cambodia , Soneva Fushi yo muri Maldives na Kokomo Private Island yo muri Fiji .
Amabwiriza mashya ku basura pariki z'u Rwanda n'ahantu nyaburanga .
Kuva kuwa Kabiri tariki ya 19 Mutarama 2021 , Umujyi wa Kigali washyizwe muri gahunda ya Guma mu Rugo y'iminsi 15 nyuma y'uko ubwandu bwa Coronavirus bukajije intera mu gihugu no muri uyu mujyi by'umwihariko .
Icyo gihe Inama y'Abaminisitiri yatangaje ko usibye serivisi z'ingenzi zizakomeza gukora , izindi zizafunga aho bishoboka abantu bagakorera mu ngo .
Iki cyemezo cyaje gisanga ikindi cyari cyafatiwe mu yabanje cyahagarikaga ingendo zihuza Umujyi wa Kigali n'Intara .
Mu rwego rwo kubahiriza imyanzuro y'iyi nama , kuri uyu wa Gatatu RDB yashyize ahagaragara amabwiriza arebana n'ibikorwa by'ubukerarugendo azakomeza kubahirizwa mu gihe hategerejwe izindi ngamba zizagenda zifatwa n'inzego zishinzwe ubuzima mu Rwanda .
Mu bikubiye muri ayo mabwiriza harimo ko ingendo zijyanye n'ubukerarugendo zemewe mu Mujyi wa Kigali no hagati ya Kigali n'izindi Ntara n'Uturere , hubahirizwa amabwiriza yo kwirinda COVID - 19 .
Harimo kandi ko abagenzi bose , baba abinjira cyangwa abasohoka mu gihugu bagomba kugaragaza icyemezo cy'uko bapimwe COVID - 19 hifashishijwe uburyo bwihuse bwa RT - PCR mu masaha atarenze 120 , mbere yo kuza cyangwa kugenda kandi abaganga bakaba barasanze batayirwaye .
Andi mabwiriza
Hoteli zakira abaturutse mu mahanga by'igihe gito zizakomeza gukora hubahirizwa amabwiriza yo kwirinda COVID - 19 .
Ibikorwa by'ubukerarugendo , harimo no gusura Pariki z'Igihugu , ingoro ndangamurage , ahantu nyaburanga ho gutembera ndetse no gusura imijyi bizakomeza mu gihugu hose , haba ku banyamahanga cyangwa abatuye mu gihugu , mu buryo bwubahiriza amabwiriza yo kwirinda COVID - 19 .
Abatanga serivisi zifasha ba mukerarugendo basabwa kumenyesha RDB gahunda zabo ndetse n'inzira bateganya kunyura .
Abagenzi ubariyemo n'abashoferi , basabwa kuzuza inyandiko isaba urushushya rw'inzira bagashyiraho kopi z'ibyemezo by'uko bipimishije COVID - 19 kandi batayirwaye , bakabyohereza hasigaye nibura amasaha 24 ngo batangire urugendo .
Ibigo by'ubukerarugendo bisabwa gusabira abakozi babyo uruhushya rw'inzira byuzuza buri cyumweru .
Hoteli zemerewe kwakira gusa inama za ngombwa , zibanje kubihererwa uruhushya rwanditse na RDB .
RDB , yongeye kwibutsa abantu bose ko bagomba kubahiriza amabwiriza y'isuku no kwirinda yatanzwe na Minisiteri y'Ubuzima hagamijwe kurwanya ikwirakwira ry'icyorezo cya COVID - 19 .
Kuva ku wa 14 Werurwe 2020 ubwo umurwayi wa mbere yabonekaga mu Rwanda hamaze gufatwa ibipimo bya Coronavirus 804 337 , byasanzwemo 11 548 banduye .
Muri bo 7580 barasezerewe nyuma bikemezwa ko nta bwandu bagifite mu mibiri yabo mu gihe 3820 bakiri kwitabwaho , abapfuye ni 148 .
Umunara nk'uwa Eiffel i Kigali : Umushinga mushya u Rwanda rweretswe wakongera ubukerarugendo .
Ni umunara wa metero 200 yagaragaje ko waba wihariye umwimerere Nyarwanda kuko ugaragaramo imirya y'inanga , ukaba wajyamo utubari , restaurants , inzu ndangamateka , indebakure ( Jumelles ) n'ibindi .
Umunara wa Eiffel umwe mu miremire ku Isi , ufite metero 300 z'uburebure .
Uwo mu Rwanda uramutse wubatswe waba uwugwa mu ntege .
Icyo gitekerezo kiramutse cyemewe , nyir'umushinga agaragaza ko byakongerera u Rwanda kuba igicumbi cy'ubukerarugendo muri Afurika , amafaranga rwinjiza akiyongera .
Didier Gakuba ni inshuti y'uwo munyamahanga utifuje ko amazina ye atangazwa umushinga we utaremerwa dore ko we icyo atanga ari icyo gitekerezo n'igishushanyo , hagashakwa abashoramari .
Gakuba ni na we watangaje bwa mbere kuri Twitter amafoto agaragaza igishushanyo mbonera cy'uwo munara , asaba abayobozi mu Rwanda gusesengura niba uwo mushinga ushoboka .
Mu butumwa buherekejwe n'amafoto , Gakuba yagize ati """" Muraho bayobozi bacu .
Inshuti yanjye yakoze iki gishushanyo kiri mu bwoko bw'Umunara wa Eiffel .
Yifuzaga ko gishyirwa kuri Mont Kigali kuko gifite metero 200 , kikaba kijyamo restaurants , utubari n'indebakure .
Iki gitekerezo murakibona gute ?
Ese abashoramari babyinjiramo nk'umushinga w'ubukerarugendo ? """"
Meya w'Umujyi wa Kigali ni umwe mu bayobozi bahise basubiza kuri Twitter , bavuga ko igitekerezo ari cyiza , anatanga igihe cyo guhura na nyir'umushinga ngo baganire .
Yagize ati """" Umwaka mushya Didier Gakuba .
Bwira iyo nshuti yawe ko byaba byiza tuganiriye birambuye kuri uyu mushinga .
Ese yaba ari hafi ngo dupange uko twahura mu cyumweru gitaha ? . """"
Meya w'Umujyi wa Kigali ni umwe mu bayobozi bahise basubiza kuri Twitter , bavuga ko igitekerezo ari cyiza , anatanga igihe cyo guhura na nyir'umushinga ngo baganire .
Yagize ati """" Umwaka mushya Didier Gakuba .
Bwira iyo nshuti yawe ko byaba byiza tuganiriye birambuye kuri uyu mushinga .
Ese yaba ari hafi ngo dupange uko twahura mu cyumweru gitaha ? """"
Ubukerarugendo butavugwa bushingiye ku buhinzi i Nyamasheke .
Abakorana na bamukerarugendo mu karere ka Nyamasheke barashishikariza abantu gusura ibikorwa by'ubukerarugendo bishingiye ku ubuhinzi .
Ibi babigarutseho mu rugendo rw'iminsi ibiri bakoze basura ubukerarugendo bushingiye ku mateka n'ibihingwa birimo ubuhinzi bw'icyayi mu karere ka Nyamasheke .
Ni urugendo rwari rugamije kumenyekanisha ibikorwa by'ubukerarugendo bishingiye ku muco n'amateka y'abantu birimo n'ubushingiye ku buhunzi .
Nyuma yo gusura bimwe mu bikorwa birimo ubuhinzi bw'icyayi cya Gisakura n'uruganda rugitunganya biherereye mu murenge wa Bushekeri , babwiye IGIHE ko usanga abantu bakunze gusura za pariki z'inyamanswa , ibiyaga , imigezi ariko ugasanga badasura ibikorwa by'ubukerarugendo bushingiye ku buhinzi .
Rugero Jeannette uherekeza ba mukerarugendo yagize ati """" Ntabwo baragira amakuru yimbitse ku gusura ubuhinzi , nashishikariza buri wese gusura ubukerarugendo bushingiye ku bihingwa .
Urugero abantu benshi banywa icyayi batazi uko gitunganywa , gihingwa gute .
Abenshi babisura ni abanyamahanga . """"
Kamugisha Kirenga yunzemo ati """" Ntabwo abantu bafite amakuru ahagije , bayafite bajya babishyira muri gahunda zabo bakamenya ko nibagera hano bazajya gusura inganda z'icyayi , imirima y'icyayi , uko basoroma ndetse akaba yanasoma kuri icyo cyayi .
Ni ukutabimenyekanisha , hari ibindi byinshi bitamenyekana harimo icyayi kuko abenshi bazi icyayi ku meza .
Bipfira mu kumenyekanisha . """"
Karangwa Anaclet uhagarariye Ivomo , umuryango uteza imbere ubukerarugendo bushingiye ku umuco n'abaturage yavuze ko abantu benshi bazi ko ubukerarugendo ari parike na hoteli kandi hari n'ubundi bwafasha abantu .
Ati """" Hari ikintu cyagiye kijya mu bantu kumva ko ubukerarugendo ari amaparike na za hoteli ariko hari ibintu byinshi byakorwamo ubukerarugendo .
Bakeneye kuza kureba umuturage ahinga gute , nk'ibi twajemo by'icyayi biri mu buzima bwo guhinga .
Hari abantu rero bishimira kugenda muri kiriya cyayi gisa neza , akareba uburyo bagisoroma . """"
Mu karere ka Nyamasheke , ni hamwe mu hantu hari ibikorwa by'ubukerarugendo birimo ishyamba rya Nyungwe , ikiyaga cya Kivu ndetse n'ubuhinzi bw'icyayi n'amateka .
Aba bakora mu bikorwa by'ubukerarugendo bakaba biyemeje kuzamura imyumvire ku bukerarugendo bushingiye ku muco , ubuhinzi n'abantu .
Abashoramari b'i Rusizi beretswe amahirwe bakwiye kubyaza umusaruro .
Mu nama yahuje abayobozi muri RDB n'abashoramari bo muri Rusizi , bagaragaje ko hari amahirwe yo kwihutisha ishoramari batari bazi ko ari muri aka karere .
Umuyobozi ukuriye Ishami ry'Ishoramari muri RBD , Lucky Philip , yagaragaje ko abashoramari bafite amahirwe yo kubakiraho babyaza umusaruro .
Mbere y'uko Isi yibasirwa na Coronavirus yatumye hafatwa ingamba zitandukanye zirimo no guhagarika ingendo zihuza ibihugu , imipaka ya Rusizi ya I n'iya II , n'uwa Bugarama yanyurwagaho n'Abanyarwanda n'Abanye - Congo mu ngendo z'ubucuruzi .
Rusizi ifite abashoramari banini 65 bahafite amahoteli n'ibindi bikorwa binini ariko hari ibicuruzwa byinshi bigitumizwa mu Mujyi wa Kigali , bigatuma bihagera bihenze cyane .
Abitegereza Akarere ka Rusizi bakabona nka zahabu ikiri mu gitaka kuko katarabyazwa umusaruro mu buryo bugaragara ukurikije ko gafite n'isoko utasanga ahandi ry'abaturanyi b'i Bukavu muri Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo batuma kagira isoko ryagutse ry'ibicuruzwa bitandukanye .
Abashoramari bo muri Rusizi beretswe ko hari amahirwe batarabyaza umusaruro kuko nko mu cyanya cyahariwe inganda kugeza ubu hamaze kugeramo rumwe gusa .
Ikiyaga cya Kivu uretse kugishakiramo isambaza na zo ubu zisigaye zarabuze , nta kindi kintu kigaragara abagituriye bagikesha nyamara , abazi iby'ubukerarugendo bakibonamo imari ikomeye .
Izi ngingo kimwe n'izindi ziri mu zo abashoramari bo mu Karere ka Rusizi beretswe nk'izo bakeneye kubyaza umusaruro .
Umujyi wa Rusizi ni umwe muri itandatu yunganira uwa Kigali muri gahunda ya Leta y'u Rwanda y'uko 35 % by'Abanyarwanda bazaba batuye mu mijyi bitarenze 2020 .
Teddy Riley yasazwe n'ibyishimo ubwo yasuraga ingagi mu Birunga .
Uyu mugabo w'umunyabigwi muri muzika , agiye kumara icyumweru mu Rwanda mu rugendo rwe bwite ariko byitezwe ko rushobora gushibukamo imikoranire yo mu yindi sura .
Amashusho yashyizwe ku rukuta rwa Twitter rwa Visit Rwanda , amugaragaza ari mu Birunga yagiye gusura ingagi , ndetse asangiza abantu ibyishimo afite .
Yasuye umuryango wa Kwitonda , abona uburyo izi nyamaswa zifite imiterere igiye kumera nk'iy'umuntu n'ibindi .
Ku rukura rwe rwa Instagram naho yasangije abamukurikira amashusho y'umwana usa n'uri ahantu mu cyumba uri kubyina , avuga ko yishimiye kuba ari mu Amakaro ( hotel y'akataraboneka iri hafi ya Pariki y'Ibirunga ) , avuga ko ari ahantu bakirana ababagana urugwiro ha mbere yabonye mu buzima bwe .
Teddy Riley wageze mu Rwanda ku wa Gatandatu tariki 5 Ukuboza akabanza gushyirwa mu kato kugira ngo apimwe Covid - 19 , ku wa Mbere tariki 7 Ukuboza yasuye Urwibutso rwa Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi rwa Kigali ku Gisozi , anunamira inzirakarengane ziharuhukiye .
Nyuma yasuye ishuri rya muzika rya Nyundo aganira n'abanyeshuri baho ndetse abemerera kuzagaruka azanye n'inshuti ze bakareba impano ziri mu Rwanda .
Yagiranye ibiganiro kandi n'abakora mu ruganda rw'imyidagaduro mu Rwanda anasura inzu ihanga imideli ya House of Tayo .
Abandi ba mukerarugendo bo muri Israel basuye u Rwanda .
Ahagana saa sita kuri uyu wa Kane nibwo iyi ndege yageze i Kigali .
Ambasaderi wa Israel mu Rwanda , Ron Adam , niwe watangaje ko aba ba mukerarugendo bageze mu Rwanda , baje """" kureba ibyiza """" birutatse .
Baje nyuma y'aho mu mpera za Ugushyingo Sosiyete ya Israel itwara abantu n'ibintu mu kirere , Israir , yatangizaga ingendo zayo mu Rwanda za buri cyumweru itwaye ba mukerarugendo 80 .
Mu Ugushyingo Israir yari yatangaje ko izatangira gukora ingendo rimwe mu cyumweru uhereye kuri uyu wa Kane tariki ya 26 Ugushyingo , aho ikiguzi cyo kugera i Kigali uvuye muri Israel ari amadolari 399 , ni ukuvuga hafi ibihumbi 400 Frw .
U Rwanda na Israël byatangiye imibanire mu 1962 ubwo u Rwanda rwabonaga ubwigenge .
Uyu mubano waje gusa n'uhagarara kubera Jenoside u Rwanda rwaciyemo n'ibibazo byayikurikiye , ariko urasubukurwa ku buryo rufite ambasade ifite icyicaro i Tel Aviv guhera mu 2015 .
Tariki ya 1 Gicurasi 2019 nibwo Israel yafunguye Ambasade yayo mu Rwanda ; nibwo bwa mbere iki gihugu cyagize Ambasaderi [ Ron Adam ] , ugihagarariye i Kigali kuva mu myaka 50 ishize .
Yafunguwe nyuma y'uko muri Nzeri 2018 , Perezida Kagame na Minisitiri w'Intebe wa Israël , Benjamin Netanyahu , bemeranyije kubaka umusingi uhamye w'umubano mu bya dipolomasi n'ubukungu ushingiye ku kugira za ambasade mu bihugu byombi .
Ku wa 25 Kamena 2019 nibwo indege ya Sosiyete Nyarwanda ikora ingendo zo mu kirere , RwandAir , yageze i Tel Aviv muri Israel .
Ni igikorwa cyazamuye amahirwe y'ubukerarugendo , ubucuruzi n'ishoramari ku bihugu byombi ndetse abakora ingendo za gihanuzi boroherwa no kugana i Yerusalemu .
Forest of Hope Guest House and Camp Site yafunguye imiryango muri Pariki ya Gishwati - Mukura .
Forest of Hope Guest House and Camp Site yashyizweho na Forest of Hope Association ( FHA ) isanzwe ibungabunga Ishyamba rya Gishwati ifatanyije n'Urwego rw'Igihugu rw'Iterambere ( RDB ) .
Ba mukerarugendo bazacumbikirwa mu nyubako yabugenewe ndetse no mu ihema ryubatswe mu buryo bugezweho mbere cyangwa nyuma yo gutambagizwa muri Pariki ya Gishwati - Mukura bitegereza ibyiza biyitatse .
Iyi nyubako ifite ibyumba bibiri bishobora kwakira abantu bane , bahabwa serivisi zose bakenera zirimo amafunguro atatu ku munsi , aherekejwe n'ikinyobwa kidasembuye .
Ihema ryubatswe hafi ya Pariki ya Gishwati - Mukura ryo rishobora gukambikwamo nibura n'abantu umunani .
Ba mukerarugendo basura iyi pariki bazoroherwa no kubona ibimera gakondo n'ubwoko bw'inyamaswa zinyuranye ziganjemo inkende n'impundu ( chimpanzee ) n'inkima ( golden monkey ) , inyoni n'izindi nyamaswa nto zinyuranye .
Mu rwego rwo gukomeza kubungabunga urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima ndetse n'ibidukikije , buri mukerarugendo uhasura azajya asabwa gutera igiti .
Umuhuzabikorwa wa FHA , Thierry Aimable Inzirayineza , yavuze ko biteguye kwakira ba mukerarugendo ba mbere muri Forest of Hope Guest House and Camp Site .
Yagize ati """" Turi gukorana na Wilderness Safaris mu bijyanye no kubungabunga urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima no guteza imbere umuryango , twita ku gukurikirana inguge , gutanga uburezi ndetse tuzabisangira n'abashyitsi bacu .
"""" Forest of Hope Association yishimira umubano twubatse n'abafatanyabikorwa bacu muri sosiyete mu myaka ishize ndetse imyumvire ihuriweho ku gaciro ko kurinda no kubungabunga Gishwati yatumye tugera kuri iyi ntambwe yo kuyibyaza umusaruro mu buryo burimo no gukurura ba mukerarugendo . """" """"
Umuyobozi w'Ishami ry'Ubukerarugendo muri RDB , Belise Kariza , yashimangiye ko Forest of Hope Guest House and Camp Site ari inyongera ku bikorwa remezo byakirirwamo ba mukerarugendo , bituma bishimira serivisi zinoze bahabwa .
Yakomeje ati """" Ndashimira Forest of Hope Association na Wilderness Safaris ku kongera imbaraga muri gahunda y'u Rwanda yo kuba igicumbi cya ba mukerarugendo giha agaciro , kikanarinda umutungo wacu kamere . """" """"
RDB iheruka gutangaza ko Pariki ya Gishwati - Mukura iherutse no gushyirwa mu murage w'Isi n'Ishami ry'Umuryango Mpuzamahanga ryita ku Burezi n'Umuco ( UNESCO ) , igomba gutangira kwakira abakerarugendo mu Ukuboza 2020 .
Iyi ntambwe ni irindi tafari ryiyongereye mu rugendo u Rwanda rufite rwo kongera amafaranga rukura mu bukerarugendo , ku buryo mu 2024 , ruzaba rwinjiza miliyoni $ 800 ku mwaka avuye kuri miliyoni 438 $ mu 2017 .
Mu 2014 nibwo u Rwanda rwakiriye miliyoni 9 , 5 $ agamije kurufasha gutunganya neza ishyamba rya Gishwati - Mukura , yavuye mu Kigo Mpuzamahanga cyita ku Bidukikije , kibinyujije muri Banki y'Isi .
Muri Gashyantare 2016 nibwo ishyamba cyimeza rya Gishwati - Mukura riherereye mu ruhererekane rw'Imisozi y'isunzu rya Congo - Nil , ryemejwe nka Pariki y'Igihugu ya kane , yitezweho gutanga umusanzu mu kwinjiza amadevize binyuze mu bukerarugendo n'izindi nyungu zituruka ku bidukikije .
Iyi pariki iherereye mu Turere twa Rutsiro na Ngororero mu Ntara y'i Burengerazuba bw'igihugu , ingana na hegitari 3 558 , harimo icyanya cya Gishwati gifite ubuso bungana na hegitari 1 570 , n'icya Mukura kingana na hegitari 1 988 .
Ayo mashyamba azwimo ibimera gakondo n'ubwoko bw'inyamaswa zinyuranye ziganjemo inkende n'impundu n'inkima , amoko arenga 130 y'inyoni , harimo 15 aboneka muri iyi pariki gusa , n'izindi nyamaswa nto zinyuranye .
Ni pariki yabashije kubaho kubera uruhare rwa leta n'abaturage , kuko nyuma ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi yari yakendereye , ituzwamo abaturage ndetse ibindi bikorwa byabo birushaho kuyangiza .
Mu 2009 nibwo yatangiye kubungabungwa no gusubiranywa , ngo yongere ibe igicumbi cy'urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima .
Muri Mata 2019 , RDB yagiranye amasezerano y'imyaka 25 n'Ikigo Imizi Eco - Tourism Development Ltd yo gutunganya no gucunga Pariki y'Igihugu ya Gishwati - Mukura , ku buryo ihinduka igice gikorerwamo ubukerarugendo .
Bigiye kwikuba kabiri : Menya impinduka nshya mu biciro byo gusura Pariki y'Igihugu y'Akagera .
Mu ihame ry'ubucuruzi busanzwe , uko ugira abakiliya benshi niko utera imbere kurushaho , ariko iryo kurengera ibidukikije ribivuga ukundi , kuko iyo abantu babaye benshi cyane , ibihombo biba byinshi .
Imibare igaragaza ko nko mu mwaka wa 2010 , Pariki y'Igihugu y'Akagera yasurwaga n'abantu bagera mu 15 , 000 ku mwaka , kugeza mu 2019 barazamuka cyane kuko bageze hafi ku 50 . 000 .
Ubuyobozi bw'iyi pariki buheruka kumenyesha abafatanyabikorwa bayo ko bijyanye no kuba ba mukerarugendo benshi bayisura mu mezi ane y'umwaka , hari igihe yarenzaga ubushobozi ifite bwo kubakira , kandi bifite ingaruka mbi kuri pariki n'abayisura .
Yakomeje iti """" Bumwe mu buryo bwo kugabanya iri zamuka n'ingaruka rigira kuri pariki , kandi hagakomeza kuboneka ubushobozi bukenewe mu gucunga pariki , ni mu kugena ibiciro . """"
"""" Uburyo bushya bwo kugena ibiciro bigamije gushishikariza abantu kuhamara igihe kirekire , ikintu dukeneye kongeramo imbaraga kandi twanabonye cyane muri iki gihe cyo kuzahura ubukerarugendo bw'imbere mu gihugu . """"
Ibiciro byakubwe akarenga kabiri
Mu mpinduka zikomeye zakozwe , harimo kongera igiciro cyo kwinjira muri pariki , ariko bikagenda bigabanywa igihe umuntu ahamaze ijoro rya kabiri n'irya gatatu .
Bibarwa ko nta kiguzi cy'inyongera umuntu azajya asabwa kuva ku ijoro rya 4 - 7 , bizaba nk'inyongezo ya pariki .
Mu byiciro bishya kandi hashyizwemo igiciro cyo kuba indege yagwa hagati muri Pariki , aho umuntu yishyuzwa $ 50 .
Mu biciro bizatangira kubahirizwa guhera ku wa 15 Mutarama 2021 , bigaragara ko Umunyarwanda cyangwa umuturage wo muri kimwe mu bihugu bigize Umuryango wa Afurika y'Iburasirazuba ( EAC ) wishyuraga $ 7 . 50 cyangwa 6 , 500 Frw nk'ikiguzi cyo kwinjira muri Pariki ,
azaba yishyura 16 $ cyangwa 15 , 000 Frw ku munsi cyangwa ijoro rimwe .
Mu gihe mbere habarwaga gusa igiciro cy'umunsi ukwawo , ubu umuntu namara amajoro abiri muri iyi pariki azishyura 24 $ cyangwa 22 , 500 Frw , amajoro naba atatu yishyure 30 , 000 Frw yo kwinjira gusa .
Naho umunyamahanga ubusanzwe winjiraga yishyuye 50 $ , guhera muri Mutarama 2021 azaba yishyura 100 $ , ku majoro abiri yishyure $ 150 , mu gihe kuri atatu azishyura $ 200 .
Mu biciro byashyiriweho abana , abafite munsi y'imyaka itanu ntabwo bazajya bishyuzwa .
Ku bayirengeje ariko nabo ibiciro bizazamuka .
Abana bafite imyaka 6 - 12 bo mu Rwanda na EAC bishyuraga $ 4 ( 3 , 500 Frw ) , bazajya bishyura $ 11 ( 10 , 000 Frw ) .
Ku majoro abiri igiciro kizaba $ 16 ( 15 , 000 Frw ) naho ku majoro atatu kibe $ 21 ( 20 , 000 Frw ) .
Uretse igiciro gitangwa ku muntu , no ku gitangwa ku winjije imodoka nacyo hazabamo impinduka .
Imodoka nto y'inyarwanda cyangwa yanditswe muri EAC yishyuzwaga $ 12 ( 10 , 000 Frw ) azaba $ 10 , naho zimwe nini zitwara ba mukerarugendo zishyuzwaga $ 24 ( 20 . 000 Frw ) , yagabanyijwe aba $ 20 .
Ku modoka nto n'inini zo hanze ya EAC zo ntibyahindutse , ni $ 40 na $ 100 nk'uko bikurikirana .
Impinduka ku matsinda n'abishyura umwaka wose
Mu buryo busanzwe , byateganywaga ko iyo abantu bishyize hamwe ari Abanyarwanda barenga 20 , bahitaga bagaranyirizwa 1500 Frw kuri buri muntu , maze bakishyura 5000 Frw kuri buri umwe winjiye muri Pariki y'Igihugu y'Akagera .
Mu buryo bushya guhera muri Mutarama 2021 , """" amatsinda y'Abanyarwanda bishyize hamwe basaga 20 bagabanyirizwaho 20 % ku giciro gisanzwe cyo kwinjira muri pariki ; 12 . 000 Frw ku muntu mukuru na 8000 Frw ku bana . """"
Mu mpinduka kandi harimo izamuka mu biciro by'umuntu wishyura gusura pariki mu mwaka wose .
Ku munyarwanda cyangwa umuturage wa EAC , umuntu ku giti cye yishyura 95 , 000 Frw ( nta cyahindutse ) , ariko ku bantu babiri yavuye 115 , 000 Frw agera ku 150 , 000 Frw ; naho ku muryango ava ku 150 , 000 Frw agera ku 205 , 000 Frw .
Ni mu gihe ku banyamahanga batuye mu Rwanda cyangwa muri EAC bo bishyuraga $ 250 ku muntu umwe , yabaye $ 300 .
Ku bantu babiri yari $ 400 yabaye $ 500 , mu gihe ku muryango wose yari $ 600 yabaye $ 700 .
Ku bantu bari baramaze kwishyura gusura Pariki mu mwaka utaha ntabwo bazishyuzwa andi mafaranga .
Ntabwo izi mpinduka ariko zageze ku biciro byo kurara ahantu nka Ruzizi Tented Lodge cyangwa Karenge Bush Camp .
Ni nk'uko ibiciro byishyurwa abayobora ba mukerarugendo muri pariki bitahindutse , ni $ 25 ku gice cy'umunsi na $ 40 ku munsi wose .
Pariki y'Igihugu y'Akagera ni intaho y'inyamaswa eshanu zikomeye kuri uyu mugabane , zirimo Intare , Inkura , Inzovu , Imbogo n'Ingwe .
Ni n'iwabo w'inyoni z'amoko asaga 482 , ikanagira umwihariko ko uretse ibinyabuzima byo mu gasozi , iyi pariki inabamo ibinyabuzima byinshi byo mu mazi .
Ibyo wamenya ku ishyamba rya Ibanda - Makera rigiye kugirwa icyanya cy'ubukerarugendo ( Amafoto ) .
Ni ishyamba ribarizwamo inyamanswa zirimo inkima , inkende , isatura , ingwe , amoko y'inyoni zitandukanye , isha n'amoko menshi y'inzoka .
Habarizwamo kandi amoko 124 y'ibiti birimo n'ibivura indwara zitandukanye .
Umugabo witwa Rugira Ananias yavuze ko muri iri shyamba mu myaka yo mu 1970 habagamo inyamanswa nyinshi zitandukanye zirimo imbogo , intare , inzovu n'izindi .
Ngo zagiye zigenda bitewe n'uburyo abantu baturaga hafi y'ishyamba bakazisagarira .
Umuhuzabikorwa w'umushinga ushinzwe kubungabunga ibidukikije NAP ukorera muri REMA , Mugabo Fabrice , yatangaje ko Akarere ka Kirehe mu gihe iri shyamba ritaba ryitaweho rizagabanuka .
Ati """" Uko tutaryitaho rigenda rigabanuka ku buso , byagaragaye ko nitutaryitaho rizagabanuka kurushaho akamaro ryari rifitiye abaturage n'igihugu muri rusange , niyo mpamvu REMA ifatanyije n'abafatanyabikorwa habayeho ibikorwa byo kwita kuri iri shyamba aho ryashyizweho uruzitiro ruritandukanya n'abaturage hakazanaterwamo ibiti
bishya byinshi hanongerwemo n'ibindi byari bisanzwemo . """"
Mugabo yavuze ko abaturage barituriye bazahabwa ibiti birimo iby'imbuto n'ibindi bisanzwe ndetse banafashwe mu bundi buryo burimo kubahuriza mu makoperative abakora ubuvumvu bahabwe inkunga , yavuze ko mu myaka ine leta igiye kurishoramo miliyoni 400 Frw .
Abaturage baturiye iri shyamba batangiye kubona inyungu
Rugina yavuze ko gutangira kurivugurura byatangiye kubafasha kuko bamwe mu baturage batangiye kuhabona akazi abandi basabwa kwibumbira mu makoperative kugira ngo bahabwe ubufasha .
Ati """" Abaturage benshi babonye akazi mu kurizitira abandi bakabona mu gukora imihanda itandukanya ishyamba n'imirima , abandi basabwe kwibumbira mu makoperative kugira ngo bazabashe gufashwa bari hamwe . """"
Nikuze Clementine we yavuze biteguye kwakira abakerarugendo baza kurisura agasaba leta kubakorera umuhanda ukaba mwiza ndetse bakanagezwaho n'amashanyarazi kugira ngo nabo bagire ibikorwa by'iterambere bakora .
REMA ivuga ko mu myaka ine iri shyamba rizaba rimaze kuvugururwa aho rizashorwamo miliyoni 400 Frw .
Iri mu biganiro na RDB bigamije kureba uko ryahindurwa ahantu nyaburanga ku buryo nyuma y'iyo myaka ine ryatangira gusurwa na ba mukerarugendo .
Ni ku nshuro ya mbere iyi kompanyi ikoreye urugendo mu Rwanda , gusa byitezwe ko izi ngendo zizakomeza kujya zikorwa buri Cyumweru .
Mu Ugushyingo , iyi sosiyete yari yatangaje ko izatangira gukora ingendo rimwe mu cyumweru uhereye kuri uyu wa Kane tariki ya 26 Ugushyingo , aho ikiguzi cyo kugera i Kigali uvuye muri Israel ari amadolari 399 , ni ukuvuga hafi ibihumbi 400 Frw .
Saa Munani nibwo iyi ndege yageze i Kigali itwaye ba mukerarugendo bari bakandagiye ku butaka bw'u Rwanda ku nshuro yabo ya mbere , ibyishimo byari byose ku bari bayirimo muri uru rugendo rwanditse amateka .
Abageze mu Rwanda , bagaragaje ko gusura u Rwanda ari ukwifatanya narwo nk'ibihugu byombi bihuje amateka , kandi banyotewe no kubona ibyiza birutatse .
RwandAir yari isanzwe ikorera ingendo mu Mujyi wa Tel Aviv muri Israel gusa zahagaritswe kubera icyorezo cya Coronavirus , ndetse ntiharatangazwa itariki zizasubukurirwa .
Bivugwa ko iyi ndege ya Israel mu cyumweru gitaha nabwo izongera gukorera urugendo mu Rwanda , kuri iyo nshuro izaba itwaye ba mukerarugendo barenga 100 .
Sosiyete y'indege ya Israel igiye gukorera urugendo rwa mbere mu Rwanda .
Ku manywa yo kuri uyu wa Gatanu nibwo iyi ndege iza gusesekara ku Kibuga cy'Indege Mpuzamahanga cya Kigali i Kanombe itwaye ba mukerarugendo 80 bagamije gutembera mu bice bitandukanye nyaburanga by'u Rwanda .
Ambasaderi wa Israel mu Rwanda , Ron Adam , yatangaje ko """" Israir iza kugera ku butaka bwiza bwa Kigali itwaye abakerarugendo 80 . """"
Yakomeje agira ati """" Murakaza neza . """"
Amakuru agera kuri IGIHE ni uko mu bari bukorere urwo rugendo mu Rwanda harimo na Minisitiri ushinzwe ibijyanye n'indege ugomba kugirana ibiganiro na bagenzi be b'u Rwanda .
Ni ibiganiro bigamije ko iyi sosiyete yatangira gukorera mu Rwanda ingendo ziva i Kigali zerekeza i Tel Aviv muri Israel .
RwandAir yari isanzwe ikorera ingendo muri uyu mujyi gusa zahagaritswe kubera icyorezo cya Coronavirus , ndetse ntiharatangazwa itariki zizasubukurirwa .
Bivugwa ko iyi ndege ya Israel mu cyumweru gitaha nabwo izongera gukorera urugendo mu Rwanda , kuri iyo nshuro itwaye ba mukerarugendo baruta abo iza kugerana i Kigali kuri uyu wa Kane .
Abarenga 100 bagiye kwifashishwa mu rugendo mbarankuru ruva imuzi ibyiza bitatse u Rwanda ( Amafoto ) .
Rwanda Nziza ni urugendo ruzagera mu turere twese tw'igihugu , hagamijwe kuvumbura no kumenya ahantu nyaburanga hadakunze kuvugwa ndetse no kwerekana ishusho nyarwo y'u Rwanda rwo muri iki gihe .
Ni igitekerezo kigamije ahanini guteza imbere uburyo bwo kubara inkuru z'u Rwanda kandi bikozwe n'Abanyarwanda aho gutegereza ko bigirwamo uruhare n'abanyamahanga .
Rwanda Nziza izifashisha abafotozi n'abakora amashusho kugira ngo berekane imiterere y'u Rwanda , Isi yose irusheho kurumenya .
Ni muri gahunda yo gukomeza gushishikariza ba mukerarugendo ko hari ibyiza nyaburanga byo gusura mu rwa Gasabo no gukuza umuco wo gusura iby'iwacu mu Banyarwanda .
Abatangije iyi gahunda bizeye ko izafasha mu kuzahura urwego rw'ubukerarugendo rwazahajwe n'icyorezo cya COVID - 19 cyarusubije inyuma by'umwihariko .
Ku bufatanye n'Urwego rw'Igihugu rw'Iterambere ( RDB ) na gahunda ya Tembera u Rwanda , Rwanda Nziza izakorwa n'itsinda ry'abantu barenga 100 , harimo abafotora , abafata amashusho , abashakashatsi , abanyamateka , abayobora ba mukerarugendo n'abakora ibijyanye no kubungabunga ibidukikije .
Rwanda Nziza ni rwo rugendo rwa mbere rwo muri ubu bwoko ruzaba ari runini mu Rwanda kuko ruzagera mu turere 30 twose tw'igihugu .
Iyi gahunda yatangijwe na Image Rwanda n'abanyamuryango bayo nyuma yo kubona ko hakenewe ibikorwa bituma ubukerarugendo bwongera kuzamuka , kandi amashusho akaba ari bumwe mu buryo bwizewe ibi byakorwamo .
Uru rugendo ruzakorwa mu byiciro bibiri birimo icyo gufata amashusho kizatangira mu Ukuboza 2020 kugeza muri Gicurasi 2021 n'icyo kuyatunganya no kuyatangaza kizakomerezaho kugera mu mpera z'umwaka utaha .
Amashusho azakusanywa muri uru rugendo azerekanirwa mu mamurika atandukanye ndetse hanifashishwe ikoranabuhanga rihambaye rya """" Virtual Reality , """" mu Rwanda no hanze yarwo .
Bizamurikirwa ku rubuga rwa Image Rwanda ( ) , rusanzwe rucuruza ibihangano by'Abanyarwanda .
Biteganyijwe kandi ko hazakorwa igitabo kizitwa """" Rwanda Nziza """" kizaba gikubiyemo ibyiza bitatse buri karere k'u Rwanda .
Image Rwanda ni ihuriro ry'abafotora n'abakora amashusho n'ibindi bijyanye nabyo .
Ifite urubuga rucururizwaho ibi bikorwa ( Stock Photo ) rufite amafoto arenga 200 000 n'amasaha arenga 3000 y'amashusho .
Iri huriro ryashinzwe na Ishimwe Innocent na Habimana Jean Luc , kuri ubu rifite abanyamuryango barenga 100 barimo abafotora , abafata amashusho n'abashushanya bifashishije ikoranabuhanga rigezweho .
Amashusho ya Image Rwanda amaze gukoreshwa n'imbuga zinyuranye nini ku Isi harimo nka Paris St Germain , urwa Visit Rwanda n'ahandi .
Burera Beach Resort hotel igiye kwegurirwa abikorera .
Iyo hotel iherereye mu Murenge wa Kagogo , hafi y'Ibiyaga bya Burera na Ruhondo .
Yubatswe mu rwego rwo guteza imbere ubukerarugendo muri ako gace .
Yuzuye mu 2016 ariko ntabwo iratangira gukoreshwa .
Umwanzuro wo kuyegurira abikorera ufashwe nyuma y'aho akarere gasheshe amasezerano na rwiyemezamirimo wari wahawe kuyicunga .
The New Times yatangaje ko Barakabuye Nsengiyumba ari we wari wahawe gucunga iyo hotel , icyakora muri Nzeri uyu mwaka amasezerano yarasheshwe , akarere kamushinja kuzana andi mabwiriza atandukanye n'ayari mu masezerano basinye .
Visi Meya ushinzwe ubukungu muri Burera , Joseph Munyaneza , yavuze ko bahisemo gusesa amasezerano kuko rwiyemezamirimo yabasabaga guhindura inyigo ya hotel , gukora ubusitani no kugezamo internet kandi bitari biri mu masezerano .
Munyaneza yavuze ko nibura rwiyemezamirimo yari kubisaba yatangiye imirimo aho kubisaba ataratangira .
Yavuze ko bahisemo kuyegurira abikorera , kuri ubu Urwego rw'Igihugu rw'Iterambere ( RDB ) rukaba ruri gushaka umushoramari wayegukana .
Hatangiye uburyo bwo kuyigenera agaciro kugira ngo babone uko bayegurira abikorera .
RDB yavuze ko bakiri kwiga uko iyo hotel izagurishwa , icyakora amahirwe menshi ngo ni ukuyegurira burundu umushoramari aho gusigaranamo imigabane mike .
RDB yatangiye gushaka abashoramari bayegukana , nyuma yo kubabona nibwo hazamenyekana igihe hotel izatangirira .
Iyi hotel imaze imyaka ine yuzuye ariko itarakoreshwa , ubuyobozi bw'akarere buvuga ko byatewe no gutinda kubona ibikoresho n'ibindi byangombwa bizifashishwa .
U Rwanda ku rutonde rw'ibihugu bitangaje bizakorerwamo ingendo z'ubukerarugendo za Four Seasons .
Izi ngendo zizwi nka Four Seasons Private Jet Experience zitabirwa n'abakerraugendo batandukanye bashaka kureba ibyiza bitatse isi .
Bitewe na gahunda iba yateguwe , indege ihagurukana abantu ikabajyana mu gihugu kimwe , bahava bagakomereza mu kindi gutyo gutyo .
Four Seasons Hotels yatangaje ko muri izi ngendo zizaba umwaka utaha , izaba ikoresha indege yayo yihariye ( Private Jet ) kuko ngo yasanze abakora izi ngendo z'ubukerarugendo badakunda kugenda mu ndege rusange cyane cyane muri ibi bihe bya Covid - 19 , bityo ngo izakoresha indege yayo nshya yo mu bwoko bwa Airbus ikaba ifite imyanya 48 .
Izatangira ingendo mu mpera za 2021 .
U Rwanda ni kimwe mu bihugu iyi ndege izanyuzamo ingendo zayo z'ubukerarugendo bw'ibihugu bidasanzwe kandi bitera benshi amatsiko .
Umuyobozi ushinzwe ibikorwa muri Four Seasons Hotels Limited , Christian Clerc avuga ko biteze kubona abagenzi benshi muri 2022 .
Ati : """" Ingendo zacu zaraguzwe cyane , kandi zakunze kugurwa n'abantu bamwe , mu gihe rero abagenzi bareba ahazaza , turitegura kubona abakiriya benshi mu nzira tugiye gufungura muri 2022 , abagenzi b'uyu munsi bahitamo kujyana n'abo bizeye ko bazarinda ubuzima bwabo n'umutekano wabo kandi bakanabaha serivise nziza .
""""
Iyi ndege izajya ikora ingendo ikurikije umwihariko w'ibihugu .
U Rwanda ruri mu cyiciro cy'ibihugu bya Afurika izakoreramo ingendo bitewe nuko ari ibihugu bitera abantu amatsiko bakifuza kubimenya , ibyo bise mu cyongereza """" Africa Wonders . """"
Urugendo rwo muri Afurika ruzaba hagati y'amatariki ya 28 Ukuboza 2021 na 9 Mutarama 2022 .
Mu bindi bihugu iyi ndege izageramo biri muri icyo cyiciro harimo Afurika y'Epfo , Misiri , Tanzania , Ibirwa bya Maurice , Zambia na Tanzania .
Ingendo z'iyi ndege kandi zizongera kunyura mu Rwanda ku matariki yo hagati ya 28 Gicurasi kugeza 20 Kamena 2022 , icyo gihe bizaba ari mu cyiciro cyo gusura ibihugu bidasanzwe kandi bishimishije kurusha ibindi ku isi , mu cyongereza byiswe """" World of Adventures . """"
Ibyo bihugu birimo u Rwanda , Miami , umujyi wa Kyoto uri ku kirwa cya Honshu mu Buyapani ; Ikirwa cya Bali muri Indonesia ; Ibirwa bya Seychelles ; Marrakech muri Maroc ; Bogota muri Colombia ; n'Ikirwa cya Galapagos kiri mu Nyanja ya Pasifika .
Izi ngendo zigamije gufasha abantu kumenya ahantu hadasanzwe baba bafite amatsiko yo kugera .
Ni ingendo zizaba zigenzurwa na sosiyete yo mu Buhinde izobereye ibyo kugenzura ingendo z'indege yitwa TCS ( Tata Consultancy Services Limited ) serivise zayo zikazunganirana n'iza Four Seasons Hotels zo kwita ku buzima n'umutekano w'abagenzi .
Four Seasons Hotels itegura izi ngendo z'ubukerarugendo ifite amashami arenga 100 mu bihugu bitandukanye , ikaba ifite icyicaro i Toronto muri Canada .
Pariki ya Gishwati - Mukura igiye kugururirwa abakerarugendo .
Iyi ntambwe ni irindi tafari ryiyongereye mu rugendo u Rwanda rufite rwo kongera amafaranga rukura mu bukerarugendo , ku buryo mu 2024 , ruzaba rwinjiza miliyoni $ 800 ku mwaka avuye kuri miliyoni $ 438 mu 2017 .
U Rwanda rukomeje gukaza umuvuduko mu kuzahura ubukerarugendo , bwari bwarazahaye cyane kubera icyorezo cya COVID - 19 .
Umuyobozi w'Ishami ry'Ubukerarugendo muri RDB , Kageruka Ariella , yavuze ko biteguye gutangira kwakira abakerarugendo basura Pariki ya Gishwati - Mukura vuba .
Yagize ati """" Turateganya gukoresha Pariki ya Gishwati - Mukura mu bikorwa by'ubukerarugendo .
Twari tukiri gutunganya ibintu bimwe na bimwe , tuzayifungurira abakerarugendo mu mpera z'uyu mwaka . """"
Ibi Kageruka yabitangaje ubwo Urwego rw'Igihugu rw'Iterambere ( RDB ) ari narwo rweguriwe imicungire y'iyi pariki , rwashyikirizwaga n'Ikigo cy'Igihugu gishinzwe kubungabunga Ibidukikije ( REMA ) , icyicaro cyayo gifite agaciro ka miliyoni 900 z'amafaranga y'u Rwanda .
Mu 2014 nibwo u Rwanda rwakiriye miliyoni $ 9 , 5 agamije kurufasha gutunganya neza ishyamba rya Gishwati - Mukura , yavuye mu Kigo Mpuzamahanga cyita ku Bidukikije , kibinyujije muri Banki y'Isi .
Kageruka yavuze ko kuba Gishwati - Mukura yaragizwe pariki , bizagira uruhare runini mu kuzamura ubukungu bw'igihugu , kuko izunganirana n'izindi pariki zisanzwe mu kwakira abakerarugendo , kuko irimo urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima bishobora kunyura abakerarugendo .
Muri Gashyantare 2016 nibwo ishyamba cyimeza rya Gishwati - Mukura riherereye mu ruhererekane rw'Imisozi y'isunzu rya Congo - Nil , ryemejwe nka Pariki y'Igihugu ya kane , yitezweho gutanga umusanzu mu kwinjiza amadevize binyuze mu bukerarugendo n'izindi nyungu zituruka ku bidukikije .
Iyi pariki iherereye mu Turere twa Rutsiro na Ngororero mu Ntara y'i Burengerazuba bw'igihugu , ingana na hegitari 3 558 , harimo icyanya cya Gishwati gifite ubuso bungana na hegitari 1 570 , n'icya Mukura kingana na hegitari 1 988 .
Ayo mashyamba azwimo ibimera gakondo n'ubwoko bw'inyamaswa zinyuranye ziganjemo inkende n'impundu n'inkima , amoko arenga 130 y'inyoni , harimo 15 aboneka muri iyi pariki gusa , n'izindi nyamaswa nto zinyuranye .
Ni pariki yabashije kubaho kubera uruhare rwa leta n'abaturage , kuko nyuma ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi yari yakendereye , ituzwamo abaturage ndetse ibindi bikorwa byabo birushaho kuyangiza .
Mu 2009 nibwo yatangiye kubungabungwa no gusubiranywa , ngo yongere ibe igicumbi cy'urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima .
Muri Mata 2019 , RDB yagiranye amasezerano y'imyaka 25 n'Ikigo Imizi Eco - Tourism Development Ltd yo gutunganya no gucunga Pariki y'Igihugu ya Gishwati - Mukura , ku buryo ihinduka igice gikorerwamo ubukerarugendo .
Nyuma y'iminsi ihawe abayicunga bashya , muri Kigali Arena hagiye gushyirwa restaurant igezweho .
Umunyabigwi mu guteka , Coco Reinarhz , ni we uzatangirana n'icyo gikoni mu ntangiriro za 2021 , nk'uko ikigo QA Venue Solution Rwanda cyahawe gucunga Kigali Arena cyabitangaje .
QA Venue Solution Rwanda iherutse gusinyana amasezerano na Guverinoma y'u Rwanda y'imyaka irindwi yo gucunga iyo nyubako yakira abantu bagera ku bihumbi icumi .
Umutetsi Coco Reinarhz ugiye gutangirana n'igikoni cya Kaffé Sports , yavukiye mu Burundi .
Yakoze imirimo yo guteka mu bigo bikomeye mu bihugu nk'u Bubiligi , Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo , Côte d'Ivoire na Afurika y'Epfo .
Ni we nyiri restaurant Épicure iherereye i Sandton mu Mujyi wa Johannesburg muri Afurika y'Epfo .
Coco Reinarhz yagize ati """" Tuzakira abashyitsi b'ubwoko bwose , duhereye ku ku batekera indyo nyafurika na mpuzamahanga .
Intego yanjye ni ugukorana n'abanyempano b'imbere mu gihugu ngo tugaragaze umwihariko mu ndyo zitandukanye .
Turifuza ko abantu bazana imiryango yabo n'inshuti zabo bakishima . """"
Coco Reinarhz yizeye ko ibiribwa n'ibinyobwa bizajya bitangwa na Kaffé Sports bizatuma abantu benshi bagana Kigali Arena ku bwinshi .
Umuyobozi wa QA Venue Solutions , Kyle Schofield , yavuze ko amasezerano bagiranye na Coco Reinarhz ari intambwe ya mbere mu byo biyemeje , byo kugira Kigali Arena ahantu hafasha abagana iyo nyubako bakabona serivisi nziza kandi zigezweho .
Coco Reinarhz azwi ku guteka indyo zitandukanye yagiye ahererwa ibihembo mpuzamahanga .
Indyo azwiho guteka ni iyitwa """" Sel et Poivre """" yanatoranyijwe mu bihembo American Express Fine Dining .
Iyo ndyo yanahawe igihembo mu 2013 mu bihembo byiswe Diners Club Diamond Award .
Ubuhanga bwe mu guteka yabugaragaje kuri televiziyo zitandukanye ku Isi nka SABC1 , SABC3 , E - tv , CNN , TV5 na BBC Food .
QA Venue Solutions izakorana n'amashyirahamwe y'imikino yo mu gihugu na mpuzamahanga kimwe n'abategura inama n'ibindi bikorwa binini , hagamijwe gutegura ibikorwa bizabera muri Kigali Arena .
Biteganyijwe ko QA Venue Solutions izashora miliyoni 2 , 4 $ , hagamijwe kwakira ibikorwa binyuranye kandi bikomeye .
QA Venue Solutions Rwanda izanoza imikorere ya Kigali Arena binyuze mu gushyiraho uburyo bwo kuyicunga , kugurisha amatike , gutegura ibijyanye n'amajwi ( sound ) , kubyaza umusaruro ibikoresho bya Made in Rwanda ku buryo umuntu uzajya ahagera azajya yizihirwa n'igihe yahamaze .
Iki kigo kandi kizahuza imbaraga n'abafatanyabikorwa b'imbere mu gihugu no hanze yacyo mu gushyiraho ishuri rizafasha kongerera ubushobozi abari mu ruganda rwo gutegura inama n'ibitaramo bitandukanye .
Ibyiza bya Sainte Famille Hotel nyuma y'umwaka umwe ifunguye imiryango ( Amafoto ) .
Ku wa 5 Ugushyingo 2020 , umwaka umwe wari wuzuye itangiye imirimo , ari nabwo yatumiye abafatanyabikorwa bayo bifatanya mu kwishimira iyi ntambwe imaze guterwa .
Arkiyepiskopi wa Diyosezi ya Kigali , Musenyeri Antoine Kambanda uheruka no gutorerwa kuba Cardinal , yashimiye abafatanyabikorwa bayo , abizeza ko bazakomeza kwakiranwa urugwiro muri iyi hotel .
Yashimiye byimazeyo abakiliya n'abafatanyabikorwa batahwemye kubana na Sainte Famille Hotel mu bihe bitoroshye by'icyorezo cya COVID - 19 .
Ati """" Ni umwaka utari woroshye kuko twatangiye COVID - 19 ikadukoma mu nkokora , ariko twanze guhera hasi turabyuka .
Nk'abafatanyabikorwa ba hafi mwakomeje gufatanya natwe , turabashimiye ku buryo bw'umwihariko . """"
"""" Inshuti nyanshuti igaragarira aho rukomeye , kuba mwarakomeje kutuba hafi mu bihe bikomeye kugira ngo tuzanzamuke , ubu tukaba duhagaze , reka dushingure tugende , dukomezanye urugendo . """"
Yavuze ko kwakira abantu neza ari imwe mu nshingano za Kiliziya Gatolika .
Ati """" Mu ivanjili biratubabaza kubona umwana w'Imana yaraje ku Isi akabura icumbi , akazenguruka mu mahoteli y'i Yeruzaremu bakavuga bati haruzuye nta cumbi .
Ubwo rero Kiliziya biri mu butumwa bwayo , kwakira abantu ibifite ku mutima . """"
Umuyobozi wa Sainte Famille Hotel , Egide Bukumura , yavuze ko mu mwaka umwe iyi hoteli imaze ikora , bishimira urwego igezeho .
Ati """" Tumaze kumenyekana mu rwego rushimishije , noneho byisumbuyeho kuba ari hoteli ya Kiliziya Gatolika ifite umwihariko mu gutanga serivisi nziza , bituma abakiliya bacu batugirira icyizere . """"
Yavuze ko bishimiye cyane kuba Cardinal Kambanda yifatanyije na bo mu kwizihiza isabukuru y'umwaka wa mbere bamaze bakora .
Ati """" Ni ibyishimo kuri hoteli yacu , kuba Cardinal yaje akifatanya natwe mu gushimira abafatanyabikorwa babanye natwe muri uyu mwaka , biragaragariza abakiliya ko abatekereza umunsi ku munsi . """"
Sainte Famille Hotel ifite ibyumba 67 byo kuraramo , ikagira n'ibyumba by'inama birimo ibiringaniye byakira abantu 40 , ibinini byakira 100 , n'ikindi kinini cyane gikorerwamo inama , ubukwe n'indi myidagaduro gishobora kwakira abantu hagati ya 800 na 1000 .
Iyi hoteli kandi ifite ibyumba byiza byo gukoreramo imirimo irimo ibiro , bikodeshwa ku biciro byiza .
Ifite pisine ( piscine ) , restaurant n'akabari bigezweho .
Amafunguro ya ku manywa ahoraho kuva ku wa Mbere kugeza ku wa Gatanu , hagati ya saa Sita na saa Cyenda .
Iyi hoteli ifite umwihariko wo kuba ikozwe ahanini n'ibikoresho byakorewe mu Rwanda , ikagira parikingi ihagije ku bakiliya n'abahakorera , kandi ifite ahantu hanini yakirira abakiliya ku buryo babasha kwisanzura mu mahumbezi .
Sainte Famille Hotel iherereye mu Mujyi wa Kigali , hafi y'inyubako ya Paruwasi Ste Famille .
U Rwanda rwashyizwe mu hantu 20 ku Isi ho gusurwa mu 2021 .
Uru rutonde rwakozwe nyuma y'aho buri hantu muri 20 hari kuri uru rutonde hagiye hatoranywa n'abantu bazobereye ibijyanye n'ubukerarugendo , bafite ubunararibonye mu gutembera hirya no hino ku Isi cyangwa se bafasha ba mukerarugendo .
Kuri iyi nshuro , u Rwanda rwatoranyijwe n'Umunyamerikakazi , Julie Danziger , ukunze kugaragara kenshi mu bikorwa byo gusura ahantu hatandukanye ubarizwa mu kigo gifasha ba mukerarugendo cya Embark Beyond .
Buri muntu uhitamo igihugu abandi basura , aba asabwa gusobanura impamvu koko kibereye kuba cyasurwa .
Danziger asobanura impamvu yatoranyije u Rwanda , yavuze ko mu gihe COVID - 19 yatumye ingendo hirya no hino ku Isi zihagarara , ibyerekezo bitandukanye byatangiye kureba uburyo mu gihe kiri imbere abantu bazakora ingendo mu mutuzo .
Ku ruhande rw'u Rwanda , yavuze ko gukora ingendo mu buryo butekanye byashyizwe ku isonga rya buri kimwe igihugu gikora , ndetse ko buri gikorwa kijyanye n'ubukerarugendo kuva mu 2005 giteguwe neza kugeza no kuri gahunda zigamije gufasha abaturage baturiye za pariki .
Ati """" U Rwanda rwakoze akazi gakomeye mu gusubukura bwangu ibikorwa by'ubukerarugendo , hashyirwaho ingamba zo kwirinda bitari mu rwego rwo kurinda ba mukerarugendo ahubwo n'abaturage b'igihugu , hamwe n'inyamaswa ziba mu mashyamba . """"
Danziger yahamagariye ba mukerarugendo bashaka kumenya byinshi kuri Afurika no kumenya ibice bitandukanye gusura u Rwanda .
Mu Rwanda hari ibice byinshi bikurura ba mukerarugendo , aho ku isonga haza Pariki y'Igihugu y'Iburanga ibonekamo ingagi .
Ahandi ni nka Pariki ya Nyungwe ibonekamo ikiraro cyo mu kirere kiri hake muri Afurika , iy'Akagera irimo inyamaswa eshanu z'inkazi arizo Intare , Inzovu , Imbogo , Inkura n'Ingwe .
Hari kandi nka Pariki ya Gishwati n'ibindi bice bitandukanye byishimirwa na ba mukerarugendo .
Ibi binajyana n'uko ari kimwe mu bihugu bifite hotel ziteye amabengenzi zirimo Bisate Eco Lodge iherereye mu Birunga , Magashi Camp iherereye muri Pariki y'Akagera , One & Only Nyungwe House n'izindi .
Mu handi hantu hashyizwe mu ho umuntu akwiriye gusura mu mwaka utaha harimo Qatar , Kenya , Ibirwa bya Tahiti , Misiri , Paris , Nouvelle - Zélande , Tunisie , Ireland n'ahandi .
Dusure inyamaswa eshanu zihatse izindi muri Pariki y'Igihugu y'Akagera n'izizigaragiye ( Amafoto ) .
Ubu iyi pariki ibarizwamo inyamaswa eshanu zikomeye muri Afurika arizo Intare , Inzovu , Imbogo , Inkura n'Ingwe .
Muri iri shyamba uretse Intare yubahwa nk'Umwami w'Ishyamba , indi nyamaswa y'igitinyiro ni Inzovu , inagira umutima uzirikana ku buryo bukomeye , ari nayo nyamaswa itajya ipfa kwisukirwa .
Harimo n'Inkura nk'inyamaswa iheruka kuzanwa mu Rwanda vuba , abakurikiranira hafi iby'inyamaswa bahamya ko yiyemera nk'igisimba gifite imbaraga zihagije n'ihembe rikomeye , ku buryo nta cyayihagarika .
Umwe aheruka kubwira IGIHE ati """" Yumva byanga bikunda niba hari ikintu ibonye cyamaze kuyisatira , igomba gukoresha za mbaraga kugira ngo igikure imbere .
Ishobora gukubita n'igiti cyangwa indi nyamaswa . """"
"""" Ikindi kizwi kuri yo ntabwo ireba neza , ikoresha guhumurirwa no kumva cyane , ireba ari uko ibona ikintu gitambuka .
Ikintu gihagaze ntabwo iba ikibona .
Uramutse ucunze ukareba nk'umuyaga , niba uri kukuvaho uyiganaho uba uri hafi n'urupfu , ihita ikumva ako kanya . """"
"""" Na none iyo ikintu kigenda ikibona vuba , ariko uhise uhagarara cyangwa ukaryama , ishobora no kukunyuraho . """"
Iyi nyamaswa nta nubwo ibana n'izindi , ahubwo iba yonyine kuko zakwicana .
Mu nyamaswa ziri muri iyi Pariki habamo n'Isatura , yo ni inyamaswa ifatwa nk'idatekereza cyane , ku buryo ishobora kumva urusaku rw'imodoka igaturumbuka iyinyura imbere ku buryo yanayigonga .
Mu mazi ho umwami ni Imvubu , ku buryo ibindi binyabuzima biyibererekera , bitayitinyiye ubunini bwayo gusa , ahubwo n'iryinyo ryayo rinini kandi rikomeye .
Pariki y'Akagera kandi ni ahantu hakunze gusurwa cyane , aho umuntu abasha kwibonera ndetse akamenya nk'inyamaswa yitwa Indonyi ifite ububasha bwo kwishariririza mu gihe yikanze , bigatuma n'inyamaswa yayica itabasha kuyirya , cyangwa se ko Imparage ifite umugeri w'inyuma uremereye , ku buryo n'iyo Intare
iyisukiriye ishaka kuyica ikayitera wa mugeri iba itakiharenze .
Inyamaswa muri Pariki y'Igihugu y'Akagera kandi zikomeje kwiyongera , aho ubuyobozi bwayo buheruka gutangaza ko Intare zimaze kuba 37 kuva muri 2015 , ubwo zagarurwaga mu Rwanda .
Ibintu icumi ukwiye kumenya kuri Nyiragongo , ikirunga gifite ikiyaga gihora gitogota .
Ni byinshi byibazwa kuri iki kirunga mu miterere yacyo ndetse n'ibyago gishobora guteza abantu , hagendewe ku hantu giherereye na kamere yacyo by'umwihariko .
1 . Ni kimwe mu birunga bifite ikiyaga cy'amazuku
Ikirunga cya Nyiragongo ni kimwe mu birunga bitanu byonyine ku Isi bifite ibiyaga by'amazuku ( igikoma kiremye ikiyaga gihora gitogota , gituruka ku bibuye byashonze byo mu nda y'Isi ) , cyavutse guhera mu 1980 ndetse na n'ubu kiracyariho .
Ibindi biyaga nkacyo ni mu kirunga cya Kilauea muri Hawaii , Mount Erebus muri Antarctica , Ambrym muri Vanuatu na Erta """" Ale muri Ethiopia .
Agasongero kacyo kareshya na kilometero ebyiri
Agasongero k'ikikirunga kazwi nka crater ari nako kagizwe n'ikiyaga cy'amazuku ( Lava Lake ) , kareshya na kilometero ebyiri z'ubugari .
Uretse aya mazuku aba arimo hagati , ku mpande hari ibisa n'ibikuta binini by'amazuku yumye akarema ibibuye binini , ku ruhande rumwe rureshya na metero 3 , 175 naho urugufi rukareshya na metero 2 , 975 .
Nyiragongo imaze kuruka inshuro 34
Ntabwo ari byinshi bizwi neza kuri iki kirunga nk'igihe cyatangiriye kuruka , ariko ababikurikiranira hafi bavuga ko kuva mu 1882 kimaze kuruka inshuro 34 , ndetse iheruka ku rwego rukomeye ni iyo mu 2002 .
Ubujyakuzima bw'amazuku bushidikanywaho
Ubutumburuke bw'ikiyaga cy'amazuku ntabwo buvugwa mu buryo ntakuka , ariko habarwaga metero 3250 mbere y'iruka ryo muri Mutarama 1977 , ariko imibare ya vuba yo yerekaga metero 2700 .
Nyiragongo yigeze gusuka ibikoma kuri 60km / h
Ubwo iki kirunga cyarukaga mu mwaka wa 1977 , cyoherezaga amazuku yagendaga kilometero 60 ku isaha amanuka ku musozi , icyo gihe ariko bwo cyahitanye bake kuko bari 70 .
Yasandaye ku muvuduko wo hejuru kurusha izindi nshuro , ku buryo mu minota 30 cya kiyaga cy'amazuku cyari gikamye .
Nyiragongo na Nyamuragira , bisangiye nibura 40 % by'iruka ry'ibirunga rya vuba ku mugabane wa Afurika .
Iruka ryo mu 2002 ryangije byinshi
Iruka rikomeye rya Nyiragongo ryatangiye ku wa 17 Mutarama 2002 , nyuma y'iminsi yari ishize imitingito yarabaye myinshi mu bice byegereye ikirunga , kugeza ubwo iki kirunga cyaje kwiyasa maze gisuka ibikoma mu masaha menshi hagati ya metero 2 , 800 na 1 , 550 , bigera mu mujyi wa Goma uri hafi aho , ku nkengero z'ikiyaga cya Kivu .
Abaturage bari baburiwe ndetse abagera ku 4000 bari bamaze kuvanwa muri aka gace kimwe no mu mujyi wa Gisenyi , mu gihe cy'iruka ry'icyo kirunga .
Abantu bagera kuri 245 bahasize ubuzima kubera kubura umwuka bitewe na gaz yoherezwaga n'ikirunga , ndetse inzu zimwe zirahirima kubera amazuku n'imitingito .
Bibarwa ko hafi 15 % by'umujyi wa Goma byangijwe n'icyo gikorwa , ku buryo abantu 120 000 basigaye badafite aho kwikinga .
Nyuma y'amezi atandatu Nyiragongo yongeye kuruka
Nyuma y'iruka ryo mu 2002 , ikirunga cya Nyiragongo cyongeye kuruka nyuma y'amezi atandatu , ku buryo ibikoma bitasohotse byahise biharema ikiyaga cy'amazuku .
Ikirunga cya Nyiragongo gikurikiranwa n'itsinda ryihariye ry'abahanga mu bumenyi bw'ibiri mu Isi , Goma Volcanic Observatory .
Bakurikirana iki kirunga buri munsi mu minsi yose igize umwaka , aho baba bakurikirana amakuru atangwa n'ibipimo yaba ajyanye n'ubushyuhe cyangwa ibibera imbere muri ibi birunga .
8 . Iki kirunga kizamura imyuka myinshi ihumanya
Kuva ku iruka ryo mu 2002 , iki kirunga cyazamuye mu kirere imyuka ihumanya , bikekwa ko yanatumye hari abantu benshi bahasiga ubuzima cyane cyane mu bana .
Hari ubushakashatsi buheruka kugaragaza ko indwara z'ubuhumekero ziri mu zivuzwa cyane mu bice byegereye ibirunga bya Nyiragongo na Nyamuragira ( 12 . 2 % ) , mu gihe malaria yari ku mwanya wa mbere ( 32 . 3 % ) .
Ntabwo byoroshye kugisura
Ku bantu bamenyereye gusura ibirunga cyangwa guterera imisozi miremire , Nyiragongo ni ahantu hadakunda kwisukirwa n'ubonetse wese , kuko bisaba kuzamuka kilometero 3 . 47 kugira ngo ubashe kugera hejuru ku kiyaga cy'amazuku .
Ikiyaga cy'amazuku cyahageze mu 1994
Bibarwa ko ikiyaga cy'amazu kigaragara hejuru kuri Nyiragongo cyahanzwe mu 1994 , ariko kiza kwisubiza mu 2002 nyuma y'iruka ry'ikirunga .
Iki kirunga kitarazima , bibarwa ko kiruka nibura mu mpuzandengo y'imyaka 30 hagati y'iruka rimwe n'irindi .
Pariki y'Igihugu ya Nyungwe yeguriwe African Parks .
Aya masezerano agamije gukomeza kubyaza umusaruro iyi pariki no kwita ku nyamaswa zibarizwamo kimwe n'ibindi binyabuzima .
Aya masezerano asanga imikoranire yari imaze imyaka icumi hagati ya RDB na African Parks agamije kwita no kubungabunga ibimera n'inyamaswa ziboneka muri iri shyamba kimwe no kubibyaza umusaruro mu buryo bw'amafaranga .
Umuyobozi Mukuru wa RDB , Clare Akamanzi , yatangaje ko aya masezerano ashimangira ubufatanye bwiza hagati y'u Rwanda na African Parks mu myaka icumi ishize .
African Parks niyo yafashije RDB maze mu 2015 muri Pariki y'Akagera hasubizwamo intare zari zimaze imyaka 20 zihacitse , mu 2017 hongerwamo inkura .
Akamanzi yakomeje avuga ko ikigamijwe muri ubu bufatanye , ari ugutuma Pariki y'Igihugu ya Nyungwe iba ahantu heza umuntu yakwifuza gusura binyuze """" mu kwita no kubungabunga ibinyabuzima , kwagura ibikorwaremezo by'ubukerarugendo no kurushaho kumenyekanisha ubukerarugendo . """"
Yavuze kandi ko ubu bufatanye buzarushaho gutanga umusaruro binyuze mu gukorana n'abaturiye pariki .
Pariki y'igihugu ya Nyungwe ni ishyamba cyimeza ribarizwa mu burengerazuba bw'amajyepfo y'u Rwanda .
Rifatanye na Pariki y'Igihugu ya Kibira yo mu Burundi aho rifite ubuso bwa 1019 km2 .
Ribarizwamo amoko 13 y'inyamaswa zo mu bwoko bw'inguge n'inkende n'amoko asaga 300 y'inyoni bikurura ba mukerarugendo .
Ririmo kandi ubwoko bw'ibiti birenga 1000 .
Mu 2018 , abashakashatsi bigisha ibijyanye n'ibinyabuzima muri Kaminuza ya Moscow bageze muri Pariki y'Igihugu ya Nyungwe inshuro eshatu biga ku bimera n'indabo ziyirimo , hari ubwoko bahabonye butakiba ahandi ku Isi batekereza ko burimo umuti ukomeye .
Umuyobozi wa African Parks , Peter Fearnhead , yatangaje ko gushora imari y'igihe kirekire mu kwita kuri Pariki ya Nyungwe , bijyanye n'intego za Guverinoma y'u Rwanda yo gukomeza kubungabunga ibinyabuzima nka kimwe mu bifasha mu mibereho myiza ya muntu , ubuzima bw'abaturiye izi pariki no mu buryo bw'ubukungu .
Nyungwe ni kimwe mu bigega by'amazi y'u Rwanda kuko itanga hafi 70 % by'amazi y'u Rwanda kandi isoko y'uruzi rwa Nil iri muri iryo shyamba .
Ibarizwamo ikiraro cyo mu kirere , Canopy Walk , kiri mu bikurura ba mukerarugendo cyane .
Kireshya na metero 70 z'ubutumburuke ( kuva hasi kugera hejuru ) na metero 150 z'uburebure cyubatswe mu byuma n'imigozi ikomeye .
Cyafunguwe ku mugaragaro mu 2010 .
Ni icya mbere mu Karere ka Afurika y'Uburasirazuba , kikaba icya gatatu muri Afurika nyuma y'icyo muri Ghana na Nigeria .
Imibare ya RDB igaragaza ko nko mu 2017 Pariki ya Nyungwe yinjije amadolari 534821 nyuma yo gusurwa na ba mukerarugendo 13941 .
Imiterere ya """" Resorts """" 10 zabaye iza mbere ku isi zirimo na Bisate Lodge ( Amafoto ) .
Ni urutonde rwakozwe mu bihembo bizwi nka Condé Nast Traveller Readers """" Choice Awards 2020 , aho ibikorwa bihiga ibindi byatangajwe kuri uyu wa Kabiri .
Ni ibihembo byatangajwe mu gikorwa kibaye ngarukamwaka ku nshuro ya 33 , aho abasomyi b'uru rubuga batora """" resort """" bakunze kurusha izindi ku Isi .
10 . y'Igihugu y'Ibirunga , Rwanda
Bisate Eco Lodge yatashywe ku mugaragaro na Perezida Paul Kagame tariki ya 1 Nzeri 2017 .
Yubatse muri Pariki y'Ibirunga aho uba witegeye neza udusongero tw'ibirunga bya Bisoke , Kalisimbi na Mikeno .
Iyi hoteli iza mu za mbere zakira ba mukerarugendo bo ku rwego rwo hejuru mu Rwanda , yubatswe n'ikigo Wilderness Safaris .
Impumeko yayo yavuye ku miterere y'Ingoro y'Umwami iherereye i Nyanza mu Ntara y'Amajyepfo .
Bisate Lodge ifite ibyumba bitandatu bigiye biteretse mu ishyamba hagati , bisakaje ibyatsi hejuru , ndetse byihagazeho kuko kuharara ijoro rimwe wishyura amadolari ya Amerika ari hagati ya 1100 - 1400 .
Chamilandu , The Bushcamp Company - South Luangwa National Park , Zambia
Ni inyubako zigezweho muri Pariki y'Igihugu ya Luangwa y'Amajyepfo muri Zambia , aho Bushcamp Company ari cyo kigo cyonyine gifite izo nyubako ahantu nk'aho , ku buryo ibyiza uhabona biba bizira kirogoya .
Ni inyubako zitegeye umugezi wa Luangwa n'imisozi ya Chindeni , ku buryo umuntu abasha kwitegereza neza inyoni , inzovu n'imvubu icya rimwe .
Morukuru Family Beach Lodge - De Hoop Nature Reserve , Afurika y'Epfo
Agace ka Morukuru gaherereye nibura mu masaha atatu uturutse mu Mujyi wa Cape Town , umuntu akabasha kuruhukira ku nkombe z'inyanja y'Abahinde , bitandukanye n'uko Afurika y'Epfo izwiho cyane kugira umwihariko ku bakerarugendo bashaka gusura ibinyabuzima by'agasozi binyuze muri pariki .
Ni ahantu umuntu ashobora kuruhukira ku mucanga w'umweru , akagira n'ibindi bimushimisha birimo gusura inyamaswa cyangwa indi mikino yo mu mazi .
Abantu bagirwa inama yo gusura Afurika y'Epfo hagati ya Nyakanga - Ukwakira , aho umuntu anabasha kubona amafi ya rutura agenda ku nkombe z'amazi , nubwo umuntu yaba ari mu cyumba cye .
Singita Grumeti - Grumeti Game Reserve , Tanzania
Zipline yakusanyije miliyoni 250 $ yo kwagura ibikorwa .
Coronavirus yasubije ubukungu bw'Isi inyuma n'ibigo byinshi bigwa mu gihombo .
Serivisi itanga ni zo ziri ku isonga mu bikenewe cyane muri ibi bihe , haba mu gukwirakwiza imiti , ibikoresho by'ubwirinzi ku baganga n'inkingo .
Miliyoni 250 $ Zipline yakusanyije zatumye agaciro kayo kazamuka kagera kuri miliyari 2 , 75 $ ndetse zitezweho kurushaho kwagura ibikorwa byayo muri Afurika na Amerika .
Mu Rwanda Zipline izwi cyane kubera ikoreshwa rya drones yahatangirije mu 2016 , zifashishwa mu gukwirakwiza amaraso , inkingo , imiti n'ibindi bikoresho byo kwa muganga zibigeza aho bikenewe mu bitaro biri hirya no hino mu gihugu .
Uretse aho bikenewe vuba , hari n'aho zifashishwa bitewe n'uko imihanda yaho itameze neza ku buryo byagora imodoka kuhagera cyangwa yatwara iyo miti ikayangiza kubera kugenda yicunda .
Ubu itanga izo serivisi mu bigo nderabuzima 260 , ifite ibyicaro i Kayonza na Muhanga .
Muri Gashyantare uyu mwaka yatangiye kujya itanga serivisi zayo amasaha 24 ku yandi iminsi yose mu Rwanda , naho muri Werurwe yatangaje ko ifite gahunda yo kugeza imiti mu ngo z'abarwayi hirya no hino hifashishijwe izo drones n'ubundi .
Zipline kandi itanga serivisi zo gukwirakwiza imiti n'ibikoresho byo kwa muganga no muri Ghana , Nigeria na Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika .
Umuyobozi Mukuru wa Zipline , Keller Rinaudo , yabwiye Tech Crunch ko hari n'amasezerano mashya y'imikoranire aherutse gusinywa muri ibyo bihugu y'ahantu hashya hazajya hagezwa serivisi nk'izo .
Yavuze ko ibikorwa byayo bikomeje kwaguka kubera imikoranire bafitanye n'ibigo bikomeye nabyo bisanzwe bifasha mu kugeza ibicuruzwa n'ibindi bintu iyo bijyanwa .
Ibyo ni iby'Abanyamerika birimo icyitwa UPS ( Ishami rikorera mu Rwanda ) n'icyitwa Walmar hakaba n'icy'Abayapani , Toyota .
Rinaudo yakomeje agira ati """" Kuba ibigo byinshi bikomeye nka Toyota na Walmart bitangiye gushora muri ubu bwikorezi , ntekereza ko ari ikimenyetso cyiza cy'uko abantu babona ko birimo kuza . """"
Zipline yagiye yitabazwa mu gukwirakwiza ibikoresho abaganga bifashisha mu bwirinzi , igira n'uruhare mu bwikorezi bw'inkingo aho iteganya kuzaba yaratwaye dose miliyoni 2 , 4 mu mpera z'uyu mwaka .
Ubu iri mu biganiro n'Urwego rushinzwe iby'Indege za Gisivile muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika ( FAA ) bigamije ko ihabwa icyemezo kiyemerera gukora no mu bihe bigoye by'icyorezo , aho izaba ibaye iya mbere igihawe muri sosiyete zifite drones .
Microsoft mu ntambara y'ikoranabuhanga ihanganyemo na Apple
Ubwo Microsoft yamurikaga OS nshya ya Windows 11 , umuyobozi wayo , Satya Nadella , yavuze udushya twinshi iyi Windows izaba ifite ndetse yongeraho ko tuzerekana ko Microsoft itandukanye n'ibindi bigo bifite Operating System zikoreshwa cyane .
Bimwe mu byo iyi Windows 11 izaba ifite harimo kuba yemerera umuntu kumanura [ download ] """" application """" n'imikino byakozwe n'ibindi bigo bitari Microsoft .
Ibintu uruganda rwa Apple rutarakora , kuko kenshi rugira ibyo rugenderaho rwemerera izindi application zitari izayo gukoresha OS yayo .
Nadella kandi yavuze ko abahanga mu by'ikoranabuhanga ubu bemerewe kugurisha porogaramu zabo n'iyo zaba zitari iza Microsoft , bakoresheje uburyo bwa Microsoft Store kandi ntibishyure amafaranga ku nyungu baba babonye .
Bitandukanye n'ibindi bigo nka Google cyangwa Apple , aho yo mbere yishyuzaga 30 % by'inyungu abakoresha Operating System yayo baba bakuye mu kugurisha application zabo , gusa ikaza kugabanya ubu ikaba yishyuza 15 % by'inyungu ku mwaka cyo kimwe na Google , nyuma y'aho hari abayireze .
Mu ijambo rye Umuyobozi wa Microsoft yagize ati """" Ubu Isi ikeneye urubuga rufunguye kuri bose , urubuga ruha application ubwigenge busesuye bwo kuba urubuga ubwayo .
Windows ni urubuga rwemerera izindi mbuga ziyirusha ubushobozi kuvuka . """"
"""" Turashaka gukuraho imbogamizi zose zikiriho mu Isi y'ikoranabuhanga kugeza ubu , maze tugaha abantu amahitamo nyayo no kwisanga mu bandi .
Operating Systems n'ibikoresho by'ikoranabuhanga bigomba kubaho bijyanye n'ibyo dukeneye . """"
Muri Windows 11 , Microsoft yashyizeho application ituma abantu bashobora kuvugana barebana ndetse yemerera application zitandukanye gukora n'iyo zaba ari iz'izindi porogaramu z'ibanze za mudasobwa nka iOS , Android , Mac , Linux n'izindi .
Ni mu gihe Apple ari gake yemerera izindi app zose gukoresha OS yayo .
Gusa mu ntangiriro za Kamena yavuze ko igiye kwemerera apps za Android na Windows gukoresha OS yayo .
Mu bihe byashize Apple yararwanyijwe izira kuba iteza imbere application zayo muri Operating System zayo .
Na Microsoft yarabikoraga ariko ubu iki kigo cyo gitangiye korohereza buri wese kumanura [ Download ] Application za Android muri Windows 11 , ndetse iri guha abantu amahitamo y'ibyo bashaka gukoresha .
Microsoft yaherukaga gushyira hanze porogaramu y'ibanze ya mudasobwa mu 2015 ubwo yasohoraga """" Windows 10 """" gusa uko imyaka yagiye ishira yagiye ikorerwa amavugurura .
Windows 10 yagiye ku isoko ikurikira """" Windows 8 . 1 . """"
Microsoft yazanye Windows 11
Habura imyaka ine ngo Windows 10 yatangiye gukoreshwa mu 2015 ite agaciro nk'uko Microsoft iheruka kubitangaza .
Abayikoresha , bazajya bakora """" update """" babone Windows 11 ku buntu .
BBC yatangaje ko ubwo Windows 11 yamurikwaga Umuyobozi Mukuru w'iyo sosiyete , Satya Nadella , yavuze ko ari """" ibuye ry'ifatizo mu mateka ya za windows . """"
Izaba yemera ikoreshwa rya applications za Android kuri mudasobwa , bitandukanye n'uko byasabaga kwiyambaza porogaramu yitwa Bluestacks ku zindi windows .
Izaba ifite imiterere itandukanye n'izindi , aho mudasobwa yashyizwemo Start Menu yayo izajya iza hasi ariko rwagati kuri écran bitandukanye n'uko isanzwe iza ibumoso .
Uyikoresha kandi azabasha gukorera byinshi kuri mudasobwa imwe nta gikingiriza ikindi ( multiple desktops ) ku buryo wakwitabira nk'inama , ureba na filime , wandika cyangwa ukina n'imikino icya rimwe nta kibangamiye ikindi .
Windows 11 izajya kuri mudasobwa zifite nibura RAM ya 4G na processor ya 1GHz .
nkomoko yatanze telefone 500 zigezweho zo gufasha impunzi muri gahunda ya Connect Rwanda .
Byakozwe muri gahunda ya Connect Rwanda igamije guteza imbere ikoranabuhanga .
Izi telefone zatanzwe ku bufatanye bwa Inkomoko Entrepreneur Development , MTN Rwanda , Minisiteri ishinzwe Ubutabazi n'Ishami ry'Umuryango w'Abibumbye ryita ku Mpunzi ( UNHCR ) .
Iyi nkunga yemejwe kuri iki Cyumweru mu gihe Isi yose yizihiza Umunsi Mpuzamahanga wahariwe Impunzi , wizihizwa buri tariki 20 Kamena .
Intego ni ugufasha ba rwiyemezamirimo batandukanye b'impunzi kugera kuri serivisi zitandukanye mu buryo buboroheye zirimo iza Leta , iz'imari n'iterambere ry'ikoranabuhanga muri rusange .
Gahunda ya Connect Rwanda yatangijwe mu Ukuboza 2019 igamije gufasha imiryango idafite telefone zigezweho kuzibona kugira ngo ijyane n'abandi mu iterambere ry'ikoranabuhanga .
Inkomoko yatangaje ko iyo nkunga yatanzwe ku Munsi Mpuzamahanga wahariwe Impunzi , ari uburyo bwiza bwo gufasha impunzi n'abaturage baturiye inkambi kurushaho kugera kuri serivisi z'imari .
Ibikorwa byo gutanga telefone mu mpunzi bizatangirizwa mu Nkambi ya Gihembe mu Karere ka Gicumbi aho Inkomoko imaze imyaka itanu ikorera .
Umuyobozi ushinzwe ibijyanye n'Impunzi mu Inkomoko , Olive Ashimwe , yavuze ko telefone zizagira uruhare mu gukomeza gutanga serivisi muri ibi bihe bya COVID - 19 .
Yagize ati """" Mu gihe cya COVID - 19 , kugabanya ingendo byagabanyije uburyo twajyaga dutangamo serivisi mu miryango y'impunzi .
Nk'ubundi bucuruzi bwose , byabaye ngombwa ko twifashisha ikoranabuhanga mu gufasha abagenerwabikorwa bacu .
Byadufashije gukomeza gukorana na ba rwiyemezamirimo bacu nubwo ingendo zitari zemewe . """"
Umuyobozi Mukuru wa Inkomoko , Julienne Oyler , yavuze ko gutera inkunga impunzi bigira uruhare mu kwihutisha iterambere .
Ati """" Imikoranire ya Inkomoko na ba rwiyemezamirimo byagaragaje ko gushora imari mu bucuruzi bw'impunzi ari umusemburo w'iterambere ry'ubukungu .
Twabashije kugeza amahirwe mashya y'iterambere , ishoramari n'ikoranabuhanga mu bafatanyabikorwa bacu . """"
Telefone 500 Inkomoko yatanze zitezweho gukomeza kuziba icyuho muri serivisi z'imari , mu gihe uwo mushinga ugiye gutangiza porogaramu y'ikoranabuhanga izafasha impunzi n'imiryango ituranye n'inkambi kubona inguzanyo mu buryo bworoshye .
Iyi porogaramu ya telefone izaba iri mu Kinyarwanda , Icyongereza , Igifaransa n'Igiswahili .
Telefone zose zizatangwa na Inkomoko muri Connect Rwanda zizana n'iyo porogaramu .
Umwaka ushize ku munsi Mpuzamahanga wahariwe Impunzi , Inkomoko ku bufatanye na Mastercard Foundation byatanze inkunga ya miliyoni 2 . 6 z'amadolari kuri ba rwiyemezamirimo b'impunzi basaga 3600 , mu kuzahura ubukungu bwashegeshwe na Covid - 19 .
Kuri ubu Inkomoko igaragaza ko iyo nkunga yatanzwe umwaka ushize , ubucuruzi bwatewe inkunga bumaze kunguka asaga miliyoni 10 z'amadolari , bwanahaye akazi abasaga ibihumbi 20 .
Ni mu gihe 98 % by'ubucuruzi bwari bwarafunze kubera Covid - 19 bwongeye gufungurwa .
Inkomoko yiyemeje gukomeza gufasha mu guteza imbere impunzi harimo guha igishoro imiryango 25 . 000 y'impunzi mu myaka iri imbere , kandi byose bikazakorwa hashyirwa imbere ikoranabuhanga .
U Bushinwa bwohereje mu isanzure itsinda ry'abantu bazamarayo amezi atatu
Uru ni rwo rugendo rwa mbere rw'itsinda rizamara igihe kirekire mu isanzure rukozwe n'u Bushinwa , rukaba ari na rwo rwa mbere rukozwe muri rusange mu myaka itanu ishize .
Rwatangirijwe mu butayu bwa Gobi , ahasanzwe hatumbagirizwa ibyogajuru mu ntara ya Jiuquan , mu cyogajuru Shenzhou - 12 , kuri uyu wa Kane .
U Bushinwa bukomeje kugaragaza ubushobozi n'ubuhangange bwabwo mu ruhando mpuzamahanga mu rwego rw'ubumenyi bw'ikirere aho mu mezi atandatu ashize bwabashije kugeza mu gihugu ingero z'amabuye n'ubutaka ( sample ) bivuye ku kwezi ndetse bwoherezakuri Mars robot y'imitende itandatu muri gahunda yo gufasha iki gihugu mu
bushakashatsi .
Uru rugendo intego yarwo ni ugutangiza imirimo ya sitasiyo Tianhe iri mu isanzure nk'uko byatangajwe na Nie Haisheng wagiye uhagarariye itsinda .
Ati """" Niteze byinshi , dukeneye gushyiraho urugo rwacu rushya mu isanzure tukanagerageza uruhererekane rw'ikoranabuhanga rishya .
Rero uru rugendo rurakomeye kandi runarimo imbogamizi nyinshi ariko niringiye ko tuzakorana uko turi batatu tugatsinda izo mbogamizi kandi mfite icyizere ko intego izagerwaho . """"
Biteganyijwe ko mu gihe kizaza , abandi bantu batari Abashinwa bashobora kuzemererwa gusura iyi sitasiyo ya Tianhe cyangwa se inzobere zindi mu bumenyi bw'isanzure zikiyambazwa muri ubu bushakashatsi mu isanzure n'ikirere u Bushinwa bukomeje kugaragazamo umuvuduko wo hejuru .
Twitter igiye gukora impinduka zituma umuntu yikura mu bakorewe """" tag . """"
