Ntabwo biremezwa neza igihe uwo mushinga uzarangirira , ariko hagaragazwa ko bizatwara imyaka myinshi .
Stephen Hawking na Yuri Milner bibaza niba koko """" umuntu azaba ku Isi ubuzima bwe bwose , cyangwa ashobora no kugera ku nyenyeri """" cyane ko habarurwa miliyari nyinshi zazo mu isanzure .
Ni muri urwo rwego bashatse gusubiza icyo kibazo bategura inyigo bahereye ku yitwa Alpha Centauri iri hafi y'imibumbe igaragiye izuba .
Uretse Breakthrough Starshot , Ikigo cy'Abanyamerika gikora ubushakashatsi mu isanzure , NASA , gifite umushinga cyise Artemis wiga ku Kwezi na Mars naho Space X ya Elon Musk iri kwiga kuri Mars .
Apple yashyize hanze ibikoresho bishya birimo iPad Pro na mudasobwa za iMacs z'amabara atandukanye .
Ibi byose byashyizwe ahagaragara kuwa Kabiri tariki 20 Mata 2021 , aho uru ruganda kandi rwashyize hanze agakoresho ka Airtag kagufasha gushaka ibintu byatakaye na televiziyo zerekana amashusho ya 4K zifite telekomande za Siri Remote zifite umwihariko wo kuba wakoresha ijwi ushaka kugira icyo uhindura kuri Televiziyo yawe .
Dore tumwe mu dushya ibi bikoresho byashyizwe hanze n'uruganda rwa Apple bifite
Izi iPad z'ubwoko bushya zashyizwe hanze , zifite ubushobozi bwo kwihuta cyane , zakira internet ya 5G nayo yihuta bidasanzwe , umuntu ashobora kuzicomekaho ibikoresho by'ikoranabuhanga birenze kimwe ndetse zifite urumuri rwo muri tableaux rufite ikoranabuhanga rirenze iry'izindi iPad .
Zifite Camera ziteye imbere , zifite ubushobozi bwo gukora amashusho meza , ndetse ku bantu bakora inama bifashishije ikoranabuhanga , izi iPad zabazaniye udushya , aho zifite ikoranabuhanga ryitwa Center Stage rituma mu gihe uri gukoresha camera mu nama , isura yawe ituzura muri camera ahubwo izajya isubira inyuma ikagaragara neza nta ruhare wabigizemo .
Izi iPad zizatangira kugurishwa tariki 30 Mata 2021 uyu mwaka , zigurishwa amadolari 799 , hafi ibihumbi 800 Frw .
Mudasobwa za iMac zifite amabara atandukanye
Mudasobwa za iMac zari zisanzwe zimenyerewe ku ibara ry'umweru , uretse kuba zifite amabara atandukanye zifite n'undi mwihariko utandukanye n'izari zisanzwe .
iMac zashyizwe hanze , zifite ubwoko bushya mwa M1 Chip umuntu yakwita nk'icyumba cy'ikoranabuhanga rya musadobwa , aho ifite """" système """" ituma mudasobwa idashyuha , itume yihuta cyane birenze ibisanzwe ndetse izatuma uyifite agira ubushobozi bwo gukoresha porogaramu za iPhone muri iyi mudasobwa zirimo
Zillow na Headspace n'utundi dushya twinshi .
Izi mudasobwa zifite uburebure bwa cm 60 , pixel miliyoni 11 . 3 , ziri mu mabara arindwi , harimo umutuku , icyatsi na move byose byerurutse ,
iMac zizajya ku isoko mu matariki yo hagati muri Gicurasi , iziri muri aya amabara atatu zizaba zigurishwa amadolari 1 . 499 ( hafi miliyoni 1 , 5 Frw ) , mu gihe iziri mu yandi mabara ane asigaye zizagurishwa 1 . 299 $ ( hafi miliyoni 1 , 2 Frw ) .
Agakoresho gafasha mu kubona ibintu byatakaye , AirTag
Uruganda rwa Apple rwashyize hanze agakoresho ka Airtag rutari rusanzwe rufite , gakoreshwa mu kubona ibintu byatakaye .
Ugafatisha ku kintu runaka kagafasha kukibona mu gihe cyatakaye .
Ushobora kugashyira ku mfunguzo , ku ikofi , kuri mudasobwa cyangwa se ku modoka .
Iyo wagahuje n'uburyo bwa Apple bwitwa """" Find My app """" ushobora kubona icyo wataye udataye umutwe .
AirTag za Apple zifite ubushobozi bwo kutangizwa n'amazi , cyangwa ivumbi , gakozwe ku buryo iyo wabuze ikintu ( kariho ) kavuga mu ijwi riranguruye ukabasha kukibona .
Aka gakoresho kari gasanzwe gasohorwa n'uruganda rwa Samsung , Sony na Tile , uruganda rwa Apple ruzagashyira ku isoko tariki 30 Mata 2021 , kamwe kagura 29 $ ( hafi ibihumbi 30 Frw ) mu gihe tune tuzagurwa 99 $ ( hafi ibihumbi 100 Frw ) .
Si ibi gusa kandi uru ruganda rwasohoye na Televiziyo z'ubwoko bushya zibasha kwakira amashusho ya 4K , zifite telekomande ya Siri Remote , ikozwe muri aluminium 100 % .
Izashyirwa ku isoko ku itariki 30 Mata 2021 , aho izifite ububiko bungana na 32 GB zizaba zigura 179 $ naho izifite 64GB zigure 199 $
Hasohowe kandi na iPhone 12 na iPhone 12 mini ziri mu ibara rya move , ziyongera ku zari zifite amabara y'ubururu , icyatsi , umukara n'umweru .
Izatangira kugurishwa ku itariki 30 Mata 2021 , amadolari 799 ( hafi ibihumbi 800 Frw ) .
Space X yahawe ikiraka cyo gukora icyogajuru kizageza abantu ku kwezi . BBC yatangaje ko Space X yatoranyijwe igahabwa ayo masezerano ya miliyari 2 , 89 $ ihigitse izindi sosiyete zimaze igihe kinini mu byo gukora ibyogajuru zari zihurije hamwe .
Umuyobozi ushinzwe iby'ubuvumbuzi muri NASA , Kathy Lueders , yatangajko ayo masezerano azatuma uwo mushinga wa Artemis w'akataraboneka ugerwaho . Ati """" Ku bw'aya masezerano , NASA n'abafatanyabikorwa bacu bazuzuza uyu mushinga ugiye kuba uwa mbere ugaragaza ukuri ko ku kwezi muri iki kinyejana cya 21 . """"
Amakuru avuga ko muri sosiyete zasabaga icyo kiraka zose Space X ari yo yasabaga amasezerano ahendutse , nabyo bikaba byagize uruhare mu gutuma yegukana ayo mahirwe .
Biteganyijwe ko icyo cyogajuru kizageza undi mugabo n'umugore wa mbere b'Abanyamerika ku kwezi mu 2024 .
Bivugwa ko hari n'izindi sosiyete NASA ifite zishobora kuyifasha kugeza abantu ku kwezi mu gihe imwe yaba itabashije kubigeraho .
Space X ifite mu maboko ako kazi kugeza ubu , yatangijwe na Elon Musk mu 2002 ari nawe muyobozi wayo kugeza ubu .
Isanzwe ikora ibyogajuru ndetse nayo ubwayo ikora ubushakashatsi bwo mu kirere , aho ifite gahunda yo kugeza abantu kuri Mars mu 2026 .
Twitter yagize ikibazo cy'ikoranabuhanga bigira ingaruka ku barimo n'abo mu Rwanda .
Abarenga ibihumbi 80 barimo n'abo mu Rwanda bagaragaje ko bahuye n'ibibazo bakoresha urwo rubuga mu masaha ya nyuma ya saa kumi n'imwe kugera mu masaha y'igitondo gusa byaje gukemuka .
Ubutumwa bwagaragaraga nk'ibisanzwe , ariko umuntu akaba atakora like , comment cyangwa retweet .
Itsinda rya Twitter rishinzwe ubufasha , ryiseguye ku bagize ikibazo gusa ntiryavuga imvano yacyo .
Ibibazo nk'ibi byaherukaga kuba kuri Twitter mu Ukwakira 2020 , aho byamaze amasaha arenga abiri .
Icyo gihe yiseguye ivuga ko byatewe n'impinduka mu mikorere zitari zigambiriwe .
Hagiye gukorwa imodoka ifite ikirango cya Apple .
9To5 Mac yatangaje ko ayo masezerano azaba yakozwe mu mpera z'uyu mwaka , Apple isanzwe izwiho ibikoresho by'ikoranabuhanga birimo telefoni na mudasobwa ikazaba ari yo mukiliya w'imena .
Mu ntangiriro z'uyu mwaka byari byatangajwe ko Apple ishaka kugirana amasesezerano ya miliyari 4 $ na sosiyete za Kia na Hyundai zikora imodoka , ariko muri Gashyantare zitangaza ko zitakiri mu biganiro nayo .
Bivugwa ko Apple yifuza ko imodoka izakorwa yazayitirirwa maze sosiyete zayikoze zikabarwa nk'izabigizemo uruhare , ari nayo mpamvu izo zizwi zabyanze maze igahitamo gukorana n'izidasanzwe zifite amazina akomeye mu byo gukora imodoka .
Apple ya Tim Cook abenshi bayimenye kubera ibikoresho byayo by'ikoranabuhanga biba byivugira mu mikorere , bituma yizerwa cyane .
Ubwo buhangange bwayo irashaka kubugeza no mu isoko ry'imodoka , aho ifite gahunda yo kuzaba yamaze kwikorera imodoka ikoresha amashanyarazi mu 2025 .
Ampersand yashowemo asaga miliyari 3 Frw mu gukwirakwiza moto zikoresha amashanyarazi mu Rwanda .
Umushinga wa EIF ( Ecosystem Integrity Fund ) ukomoka muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika usanzwe ushora imari mu nganda no muri sosiyete zikoresha ingufu z'amashanyarazi ugamije kurengera ibidukikije , niwo washoye arenga miliyari 3 Frw muri Ampersand .
Ni ubwa mbere hashowe amafaranga angana gutya muri sosiyete itanga serivisi z'ibinyabiziga bikoresha amashanyarazi muri Afurika yo munsi y'Ubutayu bwa Sahara .
Umuyobozi wa Ampersand , Josh Wale , yavuze ko kuba hashowe amafaranga menshi mu binyabiziga bikoresha amashanyarazi , ari intambwe nziza itewe mu 2021 , bizatuma haboneka abashoferi benshi muri Afurika y'Iburasirazuba bakoresha moto z'amashanyarazi .
Yongeyeho ati """" Twishimiye iri shoramari ry'amateka EIF yakoze .
Ubu dufite ikizadufasha kugera ku ntego yacu , aho duteganya ko mu 2030 tuzaba twahinduye moto zingana na miliyoni eshanu zo muri Afurika y'Iburasirazuba , zigakoresha ingufu z'amashanyarazi aho gukoresha ibikomoka kuri peteroli . """"
"""" Ubu bufasha bwa EIF bugiye gukuraho imyumvire idahwitse y'uko ibihugu bikize ari byo bizabanza kugira ibinyabiziga bikoresha amashanyarazi maze ibikennye bikagerwaho nyuma , bikoresha ibinyabiziga byabanje gukoreshwa . """"
Moto , ni bwo bwoko bw'ibinyabiziga bwifashishwa cyane muri Afurika by'umwihariko iy'Uburasirazuba , aho hakoreshwa izigera kuri miliyoni 5 , ariyo mpamvu Ampersand ariho yashyize ingufu mu guteza imbere izikoresha ingufu z'amashanyarazi .
Umwe mu bayobozi ba EIF , James Everett , yavuze ko yishimiye gufatanya n'iyi sosiyete mu rwego rwo kwirinda ibihumanya ikirere .
Igitabo kivuga ku budasa bw'u Rwanda n'u Bushinwa cyashyizwe kuri Amazon .
Iki gitabo cyanditswe na Gerald Mbanda , kiri mu rurimi rw'Icyongereza .
Gifite umutwe ugira uti """" China and Rwanda : Effective Leadership is Key to Transformational Governance . """"
Mbanda wacyanditse afite uburambe mu mwuga w'itangazamakuru aho yakoze imirimo itandukanye dore ko yabaye Umuyobozi w'Ishami rishinzwe Itangazamakuru mu Rwego rw'Igihugu rw'Imiyoborere , RGB .
Iki gitabo cyamuritswe bwa mbere muri Kamena 2019 mu muhango wabereye i Kigali muri Marriott Hotel , witabiriwe n'abayobozi barimo Tito Rutaremara ; Ambasaderi w'u Bushinwa mu Rwanda Rao Hongwei ; Umuyobozi w'Urwego rw'Imiyoborere , RGB , Dr . Usta Kayitesi n'abandi bagera kuri 200 .
Muri icyo gitabo Mbanda yasobanuye ko u Rwanda n'u Bushinwa nubwo ari ibihugu biri ku migabane y'Isi itandukanye , byagaragaje ubudasa mu miyoborere yabyo aho abayobozi bagira uruhare mu gushyira mu bikorwa gahunda zihutisha iterambere bakurikije ibibabereye aho kwigana iby'ahandi .
Yavuze kandi ku bijyanye na demokarasi buri gihugu gifite uburenganzira bwo guhitamo uburyo bukinogeye , ko nta buryo bumwe bwabera ibihugu byose , ko icy'ingenzi ubuyobozi ari bwo bufite uruhare runini mu kuzana imiyoborere mpinduramatwara .
Amazon iki gitabo kiriho ni urubuga rwa kabiri rumaze kwakira iki gitabo nyuma ya Lambert Academic Publishing yo mu Budage .
Kiboneka ku buryo bw'ikoranabuhanga buhendutse ( electronic version ) ku rubuga ruzwi nka kindle kuri Amazon .
Inteko y'Umuco yiyemeje gushyira ingufu mu kunoza imyigishirize y'Ikinyarwanda .
Byagarutsweho mu nama nyunguranabitekerezo yahuje Inteko y'Umuco , abarimu n'abanyeshuri bafite aho bahurira n'ururimi rw'Ikinyarwanda , bagamije kurebera hamwe icyakorwa ngo imyigishirize y'urwo rurimo irusheho kunozwa .
Mu by'ingenzi byavuzwe harimo kunoza imyigishirize y'ururimi rw'Ikinyarwanda hashyirwaho ibitabo by'ikibonezamvugo birimo amuga azwi kandi ahuriweho na bose .
Amuga ni amagambo akoreshwa mu ngeri y'ubumenyi cyangwa umwuga runaka .
Urugero nk'aho usanga hakoreshwa ijambo """" mudasobwa """" aho gukoresha """" computer , """" internet ikitwa """" murandasi , physique ikitwa """" ubugenge , """" Chimie ikitwa """" ubutabire """" n'andi .
Abitabiriye batandandukanye bagaragaje ko mu rurimi rw'Ikinyarwanda hakoreshwa amuga anyuranye , aho usanga ijamo rimwe rivugwa mu buryo butandukanye , bikajijisha abakurikirana ubwo bushakashatsi .
Dr . Valentin Uwizeyimana , umushakashatsi akaba n'umwarimu muri kaminuza , yavuze ko ibi byakemuka hashyizweho inkoranyamuga .
Yagize ati """" Hategurwa inkoranyamuga , n'iyo itaba inkoranyamuga y'ikibonezamvugo yose muri rusange , ariko byibuze hagakorwa agatabo gato cyane kagerageza gushyira hamwe amuga y'ingenzi akoreshwa mu rurimi rw'Ikinyarwanda . """"
"""" Aho ngaho hahita hashakishwa uburyo abarimu n'abandi bantu bafite aho bahuriye n'ikibonezamvugo cy'Ikinyarwanda mu Rwanda bakoresha iyo nkoranyamuga cyangwa ako gatabo .
Icyo gihe rwose icyo kibazo numva cyahita gikemuka . """"
Yakomeje avuga ko ibi byakorwa habayeho ubufatanye bw'Inteko y'Umuco , Ikigo cy'Igihugu gushinzwe Uburezi , REB , ndetse na Kaminuza y'u Rwanda ishami ry'uburezi .
Umuyobozi Mukuru w'Inteko y'Umuco , Ambasaderi Masozera Robert , yavuze ko iki kibazo kizacyemuka , binyuze mu bufatanye maze amuga akoreshwa mu Kinyarwanda akegeranywa , akabonezwa , akemezwa ndetse agashyikirizwa abarimu bakayigisha mu mashuri .
Yagize ati """" Ni ibintu tuzakoraho mu bufatanye , abafatanyabikorwa twese .
Icyo twavanyemo ni umukoro w'ibyo gukora , umukoro ugamije gukemura ibibazo byagaragajwe , dufatanyije namwe mwese abashakashatsi , abarimu , n'abanyeshuri . """"
Masozera yasabye ubufatanye muri gahunda ya # NdigaIkinyarwanda yatangijwe yo kwigisha no kwiga Ikinyarwanda benshi bakakimenya .
Yavuze ko ibyo byose bitagerwaho hatabayeho ubufatanye n'abashakashatsi ndetse n'abarimu muri urwo rurimi .
Ati """" Ni gahunda twifuza ko aba ariyo twese dukoreramo ibikorwa byose byo kwiga no kwigisha Ikinyarwanda .
Iyi gahunda irimo bya bindi byose twavuze , harimo iby'imfashanyigisho , hazamo iby'amategeko ariko cyane cyane kuyisakaza . """"
Yavuze ko guteza imbere Ikinyarwanda bikwiriye kuba gahunda ya buri wese , ikamamazwa kandi igakoreshwa .
Ati """" Iyi # NdigaiKinyarwanda tuyigereranye n'izi gahunda ziriho zikorwa .
Murabona mu nganda no mu bukorikori haje ubukangurambaga bwitwa """" Made in Rwanda , """" ibikorerwa iwacu .
Urareba ugasanga ubukangurambaga buri hose n'abantu barabyumva vuba [ . . . ] Nifuza ko twazana ngo # NdigaiKinyarwanda , ikaba gahunda twakoreraho . """"
Ikinyarwanda gikoreshwa n'abantu bari hagati ya miliyoni 35 - 40 babarizwa mu Rwanda , Tanzania , Uganda , Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo n'ahandi hirya no hino ku Isi .
Inteko y'Umuco ikomeje gukora ibishoboka ngo Ikinyarwanda cyimakazwe , ndetse mu kiganiro giherutse guhuza Amb . Masozera n'abandi bantu batandukanye kuri RBA , yavuze ko ari iby'ingenzi ko ururimi rw'Ikinyarwanda rubungwabungwa kugira ngo rutazajya mu mubare w'indimi ziri mu kaga .
Indimi ziri mu kaga ni indimi zivugwa mu buryo butanoze , zikavuga zivangitiranye n'izindi ndimi nyinshi kandi zikandikwa nabi .
Habururwa ko indimi 40 % by'indimi 7 000 zivugwa ku Isi ziri muri aka kaga .
Rwagasani yanditse igitabo ku mbwirwaruhame za Perezida Kagame .
Iki gitabo'The Driven Wisdom from Paul Kagame """" giteganyijwe gusohoka muri Werurwe 2021 , Rwagasani yabanje kugishyira ahagaragara ngo abantu batandukanye batangeho ibitekerezo atoranyemo ibyo ashobora kongera muri iki gitabo , azabone kukimurikira abanyarwanda ku mugaragaro .
Amagambo yagiye atoranywa mu mbwirwaruhame Umukuru w'Igihugu yagiye atanga mu bihe bitandukanye .
Nko mu 2012 , ubwo yari I Gatsibo , Perezida Kagame yavuze ko """" Abanyarwanda bameze nk'abandi bantu , Imana yaduhaye ubuzima , ubwenge n'imbaraga n'igihugu yaduhaye twese ibikenewe by'ibanze kugira ngo duhindure ubuzima bwacu natwe ntabwo tugomba kubutakaza .
Iyo abantu bahinduye imyifatire yabo , byose bizashoboka . """"
Rwagasani yabwiye IGIHE ko yifuje guhuruza hamwe amagambo y'ingenzi , Perezida Kagame yagiye avuga mu mbwirwaruhame zitandukanye akenshi usanga zigaruka ku kubaka abakiri urubyiruko .
Yagize ati """" Ubundi ndi mu rubyiruko , iyo ubona ibintu Umukuru w'igihugu , akora cyangwa ibyo atubwira akenshi ntabwo abantu bakunze kubibika ngo babishyire hamwe .
Rero ugasanga ubishyize hamwe n'ibindi bihugu bishobora kuzajya byifashisha cya gitabo . """"
Yakomeje avuga ko """" Abantu bashobora gusoma , kandi uko ugenda usoma izo mbwirwarumahe usanga hari ibintu ugenda urushaho kwiga no kuzirikana ku Rwanda """"
Ni ibiganiro bigera kuri 41 yagiye atoranyamo amagambo cyangwa interuro zuje ubutumwa yagiye atoranyamo abihuriza hamwe muri iki gitabo .
Rwagasani yasabye urubyiruko bagenzi be , kujya rukurikira inama ruhabwa n'ubuyobozi bw'igihugu by'umwihariko Perezida Kagame .
Yagize ati """" Inama mpa urubyiruko ni ugukomeza umurage duhabwa n'ubuyobozi bwacu cyane cyane byinshi tubonera muri gahunda za leta cyane cyane ibyo tubwirwa n'umukuru w'igihugu kugira ngo tudatakaza iby'uyu munsi dukwiye kubibika mu buryo bwo kwandika ndetse n'abari hanze bakwiye kumva no gusoma
ibyo tubwirwa n'umukuru w'igihugu noneho bakazakomeza iyo nzira . """"
Rwagasani yanditse ibitabo bitandukanye birimo icyo yaherukaga kumurika cyitwa """" Ubumwe , Inzira yo Kugarura Ubumwe bw'Abanyarwanda no kubumbatira ubusugire bw'igihugu . """"
Ubushakashatsi no kongera umubare w'abakivuga : Imirongo migari yitezweho kwagura no gusigasira Ikinyarwanda .
Abahanga mu ndimi n'umuco bagaragaza ko ari amahirwe ataboneka henshi kuba u Rwanda rufite ururimi kavukire ari na rwo rw'Igihugu , ruvugwa n'abarenga 99 , 4 % .
Andi mahirwe ni ukugira uburezi bunigisha indimi kandi butangwa mu rurimi rw'Igihugu bukajijura rubanda benshi bigafasha mu kubaka ubukungu bushingiye ku rurimi kavukire .
Mu Rwanda , Ikinyarwanda cyemewe n'Itegeko Nshinga nk'Ururimi rw'Igihugu ndetse n'Ururimi rw'Ubutegetsi .
Indirimbo yubahiriza Igihugu na yo irubona nk'umusingi w'ubumwe n'agaciro by'Abanyarwanda aho igira iti : """" Umuco dusangiye uraturanga , ururimi rwacu rukaduhuza . """"
Leta y'u Rwanda yashyizeho Inteko y'Umuco nk'Ikigo cy'Igihugu gishinzwe kurengera , kubungabunga no guteza imbere ururimi rw'Ikinyarwanda nk'uko bigaragara mu Iteka rya Perezida no 082 / 01 ryo ku wa 28 / 08 / 2020 rishyiraho Inteko y'Umuco .
Mu kiganiro na IGIHE , Umuyobozi Wungirije w'Inteko y'Umuco , Uwiringiyimana Jean Claude , yavuze ko bashyize gahunda yo gusigasira ururimi rw'ikinyarwanda .
Yagize ati """" Mu kurengera ururimi ni uko turufata nk'ishingiro ry'ubumwe bw'Abanyarwanda .
Ubwo rero ikintu twita ishingiro ry'ubumwe bw'Abanyarwanda ugomba kukirengera kugira ngo igihe cyose urwo rurimi ruzahore ruduhuza . """"
Abavuga Ikinyarwanda bakwiriye Isi
Ubusanzwe ururimi rwose rugira indimi shami , nk'ikinyarwanda usanga gifite indimi shami zitandukanye zizwi n'izikirimo gukorwaho ubushakashatsi .
Abavuga Ikinyarwanda barimo abari imbere mu gihugu , abasigaye inyuma yacyo ubwo abakoroni bakataga imipaka mu myaka ya 1900 .
Imibare y'Inteko y'Umuco igaragaza ko ku Isi hose iyo urebye usanga abavuka Ikinyarwanda babarirwa muri miliyoni 30 [ harimo miliyoni 12 , abo basigaye inyuma y'u Rwanda kubera imipaka ndetse n'abari hirya no hino ku Isi ] .
Uwiringiyimana yavuze ko kugeza ubu Ikinyarwanda cyamaze kurenga imipaka aho usanga uretse mu Rwanda , hari n'amashuri makuru na za kaminuza zo hanze zigisha Ikinyarwanda .
Ingero zitangwa ni Kaminuza ya Indiana muri Leta ya Indiana , muri Leta Zunze ubumwe za Amerika yatangije isomo ry'ikinyarwanda mu 2019 .
Yakomeje agira ati """" Hari za kaminuza by'umwihariko izo muri Amerika zigisha Ikinyarwanda .
Buriya iyo Umunyarwanda agiye hanze , ajyana Ikinyarwanda n'iyo ahuriyeyo na mugenzi we bafite Ikinyarwanda ni cyo kibahuza .
Icyo kintu kirakomeye . """"
"""" N'Abanyarwanda benshi baba mu mahanga , Ikinyarwanda cyaragutse ku buryo bagenda bakigisha n'abandi .
Hari abazungu usanga bavuga Ikinyarwanda ukagira ngo bavutse bakivuga , kubera ubushake bwo kukimenya ndetse n'abo Banyarwanda bakigisha . """"
Uwiringiyimana avuga ko hari gahunda ikomeye yo gushakira Ikinyarwanda amuga kugira ngo hirindwe ko cyaba uruvangitirane rw'izindi ndimi bityo kizagumane wa mwimerere wacyo .
Yakomeje agira ati """" Ikindi hari uko kugikoraho ubushakashatsi kuko uririmi rudakorwaho ubushakashatsi rurapfa .
Ikindi mu kugiteza imbere hari n'uburyo dushyize imbere bwo kugishyira mu ikoranabuhanga . """"
Kuva muri Gashyantare 2020 , Ururimi rw'Ikinyarwanda rwashyizwe mu ndimi zizajya zihindurwa mu zindi hifashishijwe uburyo bw'Ikoranabuhanga rya Internet buzwi nka """" Google Translate . """"
Inteko y'Umuco igaragaza ko ibi na byo byitezweho kongera umubare w'abavuga Ikinyarwanda ku Isi kandi bikazanorohereza abagikoraho ubushakashatsi .
Inama Rusange y'Umuryango w'Abibumbye mu mwanzuro wayo A / RES / 61 / 266 wo mu kwezi kwa Gicurasi 2000 , yashyizeho itariki 21 Gashyantare kuba Umunsi Mpuzamahanga w'Ururimi Kavukire .
Ubuyobozi bw'Inteko y'Umuco bwatangaje ko ibikorwa bijyanye no kwizihiza ku nshuro ya 18 Umunsi Mpuzamahanga w'Ururimi Kavukire uzaba ku Cyumweru tariki ya 21 Gashyantare 2021 , bizaba hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga mu rwego rwo kubahiriza ingamba zo kwirinda ikwirakwira rya COVID - 19 .
Umunsi w'ururimi kavukire ugiye kwizihizwa herekanwa ibyakozwe mu kubungabunga Ikinyarwanda .
Insanganyamatsiko y'uyu mwaka igira iti """" Ururimi rw'Ikinyarwanda , umusingi w'ubumwe n'agaciro by'Abanyarwanda """" mu gihe ku rwego rw'Isi , hatoranyijwe igira iti """" Duharanire guteza imbere indimi nyinshi nta ruhejwe mu burezi no mu muryango . """"
Itangazo ryashyizweho umukono n'Umuyobozi Mukuru w'Inteko y'Umuco , Ambasaderi Masozera Robert , rivuga ko mu gihe isi muri rusange yugarijwe n'icyorezo cya Covid - 19 , uyu munsi uzizihizwa hifashishijwe iyakure ( Online ) .
Ibikorwa biteganyijwe
Ubuyobozi bw'Inteko y'Umuco kandi bwatangaje ko umunsi nyirizina uzabimburirwa n'icyumweru cyo kwizihiza Umunsi Mpuzamahanga w'Ururimi Kavukire 2021 .
Muri icyo cyumweru hateganyijwe ibikorwa birimo kuba Minisiteri y'Urubyiruko n'Umuco ibinyujije mu Nteko y'Umuco izagaragariza Abanyarwanda ibyagezweho mu rwego rwo gusigasira no guteza imbere Ikinyarwanda nk'ururimi rw'Igihugu n'Ururimi rw'ubutegetsi .
Hazibandwa cyane ku ngamba zo gushishikariza abakoresha n'abahugura Ikinyarwanda nk'abarezi , abanyamakuru , abashakashatsi , abanyeshuri n'Abanyarwanda muri rusange gukoresha Ikinyarwanda kinoze no kugiha agaciro .
Iki cyumweru kandi kizarangwa n'ibiganiro bigenewe Abanyarwanda baba mu Gihugu n'ababa mu mahanga ( Diaspora ) .
Ibiganiro bizagaruka ku guhuza imyigishirize y'Ikibonezamvugo cy'Ikinyarwanda mu mashuri , kizibanda ku ruhare rw'umuhanzi n'umunyamakuru mu gusigasira no guteza imbere Ikinyarwanda n'indangagaciro z'umuco w'u Rwanda .
Iki cyumweru kandi kizarangwa n'inama nyunguranabitekerezo izagaruka ku ngamba zo gukungahaza ururimi rw'Ikinyarwanda mu ngeri zose z'ubumenyi , izagaruka cyane cyane ku Kinyarwanda n'ikoranabuhanga , ubuhanzi n'ubuvanganzo , Ikinyarwanda n'itunganyandimi , amuga n'ikibonezamvugo by'Ikinyarwanda .
Umunsi nyirizina uzarangwa n'ibihangano gakondo bya muzika , ikinamico n'ubuvanganzo nyemvugo by'Abanyarwanda no gutangaza abatsindiye ibihembo bitandukanye .
Inteko y'Umuco ishishikariza Abanyarwanda kuzirikana ko Ikinyarwanda ari ingobyi y'umuco , kikaba ipfundo ry'ubumwe abenegihugu basangiye """" n'ishingiro ry'isano dufitanye aho turi hose ; kikaduha kugira icyerekezo kimwe . """"
Abanyarwanda bafite amahirwe yo kuba bavuga ururimi rumwe rwabo kavukire rukabahuza n'umuco wabo ukabaranga .
Ikinyarwanda kandi gifasha kwihutisha imigabo n'imigambi by'iterambere kuko ari umuyoboro w'ubumenyi , ikoranabuhanga n'ubuhanzi .
Kwizihiza Umunsi Mpuzamahanga w'Ururimi Kavukire bijyanye no kurushaho kwita ku Kinyarwanda , gutekereza ku kamaro kacyo , buri wese agahagurukira kugikoresha neza mu byo avuga no mu byo yandika .
Ishami ry'Umuryango w'Abibumbye ryita ku Bumenyi , Uburezi n'Umuco ( UNESCO ) niryo ryashyizeho Umunsi Mpuzamahanga w'Ururimi Kavukire mu mwaka w'i 1999 .
Inama Rusange y'Umuryango w'Abibumbye na yo mu mwanzuro wayo A / RES / 61 / 266 wo mu kwezi kwa Gicurasi 2000 , yashyizeho itariki 21 Gashyantare kuba Umunsi Mpuzamahanga w'Ururimi Kavukire .
Mu Rwanda , Ikinyarwanda cyemewe n'Itegeko Nshinga nk'Ururimi rw'Igihugu ndetse n'Ururimi rw'Ubutegetsi .
Indirimbo yubahiriza Igihugu na yo irubona nk'umusingi w'ubumwe n'agaciro by'Abanyarwanda aho igira iti """" Umuco dusangiye uraturanga , ururimi rwacu rukaduhuza . """"
Leta y'u Rwanda yashyizeho Inteko y'Umuco nk'Ikigo cy'Igihugu gishinzwe kurengera , kubungabunga no guteza imbere ururimi rw'Ikinyarwanda nk'uko bigaragara mu Iteka rya Perezida no 082 / 01 ryo ku wa 28 / 08 / 2020 rishyiraho Inteko y'Umuco .
Inkovu y'umutwe mwasatuye si uburanga navukanye , ntimukadutoneke - Kayitesi Judence .
Kayitesi wavukiye muri Rutongo muri Gasabo kuri ubu atuye mu Budage guhera mu mwaka wa 2010 aho yageze nyuma yo kurokoka Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 , yiciwemo ababyeyi be bombi n'abavandimwe babiri .
Uyu mubyeyi w'imyaka 38 , afite abana batatu barimo abahungu babiri b'imyaka 13 na 12 n'umukobwa w'imyaka 15 arera nk'umwana we .
Mu kiganiro cyihariye IGIHE yagiranye na Kayitesi , yavuze ko yanyuze mu bihe bikomeye ari nabyo byashibutsemo icyemezo cyo kwandika ayo mateka .
Yagize ati """" """" Ntabwo byoroshye kuvuga amateka twaciyemo ariko tuzajya tubikora kuko ni bwo buryo bwo gusubiza abadutse muri ibi bihe byo gupfobya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Ese iyi nkovu y'umutwe wanjye basatuye ni uburanga navukanye ? """" """"
Aya mateka avuga ko yayashyize mu gitabo yise """" """" Ein zebrochenes leben """" """" mu Rurimi rw'Ikidage , ari byo """" """" Broken life """" """" mu Cyongereza , bikaba bisobanura """" """" Inzira y'Inzitane """" . """"
Mu buhamya bwe yavuze ko muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi bamutemye mu mutwe ata n'ubwenge bimuviramo kugira ubumuga bwo kuvuga igihe kirekire ariko nyuma aza gukira .
Yakomeje ati """" """" Bakimara kuntema ubwo nari mfite imyaka 11 twari mu bihe bikomeye , sinigeze mvurwa , igisebe cyaje kumera nabi , kubera kutitabwaho , aho twari mu mpunzi n'abandi bana bakavuga ngo n'ubundi nzapfa simvurwe .
Nyuma babonye nkomeje gukomeza umutsi nibwo banshyizeho igipfuko batangira kubona ko ntahise mpfa .
Byanteye ubumuga kuko nagize ubumuga bwo kutavuga nkajya mvuga nkoresheje amarenga , nari mfite ubwoba bwo kutazabasha kuvuga ibyo nabonye . """" """"
"""" """" Ni bwo ngize amahirwe mbishyira mu gitabo kugira ngo abana be batazajya babaza amateka y'iwabo .
Bizaba n'uburyo bwo kwerekana ubukana bw'abateguye bakanashyira mu bikorwa Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi . """" """"
Kayitesi yavuze ko ikintu kimubabaza cyane ari uko abishe abantu banajugunye amafoto kuko basazabe be babiri barokokanye bahora bamubaza uko ababyeyi babo basaga .
Ati """" """" Duhora twibaza buri munsi uko babyeyi bacu basaga , ugasanga hari nka musaza wanjye muto ambwira ngo wowe uri nka Mama kuko numva musa n'ibindi byinshi twibaza tutajya tubonera ibisubizo . """" """"
"""" """" Tukiva muri Jenoside , najyaga njya kwa Rubangura nkategereza Mama ko namubona asohotse muri bisi , ibyo nabikoraga ntawe mbwiye .
Umugore wese nabonaga yambaye igitenge naramukurikiraga ngasanga si we , kuko numvaga ko Mama wanjye atapfa . """" """"
Mu kubara inkuru , yavuze ko yemeye ko umubyeyi we yishwe ubwo yabyaraga ntajye kumuhemba .
Akomeza ati """" """" Byari bikomeye kuri njye kubyara imfura yanjye ntahabe .
Kuva icyo gihe rero narabyemeye rwose . """" """"
Kayitesi yahisemo kwandika ashaka ko abana be bazamenya amateka ababyeyi babo banyuzemo ndetse n'igihugu .
Ati """" """" Sinigeze nibaza ko nzamara iyi myaka 27 nyuma ya Jenoside yadukorewe , maze kubyara numva nkunze ubuzima , kubona abana banjye bakura nabo bakazabyara nibwo batangiye kujya bambaza amateka y'iwabo kwa ba se na sekuru na ba nyirakuru .
Nafashe icyemezo cy'uko nta wundi wayababwira atari njye , ni ko kwandika iki gitabo kandi nari nsanzwe ntandika . """" """"
Yakomeje avuga ko nyuma yo kubyara abana bajyaga bamubaza ibibazo bikorogoshora ngo kuki batabona ba sekuru .
Ati """" Na nyuma yaho ntangiye ubuhamya mu 2018 mu ruhame mu gihe cyo kwibuka , nahise mfata icyemezo byanyongereye imbaraga zo gukomeza kwandika igitabo . """"
Kayitesi avuga ko kwandika igitabo byari ugutanga umusanzu we kugira ngo bitazongera kubaho ukundi haba mu Rwanda n'ahandi .
Yatangaje ko yifuza ko urubyiruko rwagisoma rukamenya amateka igihugu cyanyuzemo kugira ngo ntiruzagwe mu mutego nk'uwo bagenzi babo baguyemo .
Iki gitabo cyanditse mu buryo bworoheje kuko buri wese wagize ibihe bikomeye azibonamo .
Kayitesi avuga ko igitabo cye kizasohoka no mu Cyongereza hanyuma hagakurikiraho Igifaransa n'Ikinyarwanda .
Uko Kigeli IV Rwabugili yanze kugurisha Abanyarwanda mu bucakara avuga ko ari ab'Imana .
Abanyamateka bagaragaza ko nibura ku nkengero z'Inyajya y'u Buhinde hagurishirijwe miliyoni 17 z'Abirabura .
Icyo gihe ibice bimwe bya Afurika abaturage baragabanyutse , bicwa n'inzara , umuruho kubera ingendo ndende no gufatwa nabi .
Umwanditsi w'Umunyamerika , Sir Henri Morton Stanley nawe uri mu bageze muri Afurika mu bukoloni , yanditse ko nyuma yaje gusubira mu gace ka Maniema ko muri Repubulika Iharanira Demukarasi ya Congo asanga abaturage baragabanyutse cyane .
Iri curuzwa ry'abantu n'ubucakara byaherekejwe no gutesha agaciro , iyicarubozo , n'ihohoterwa ry'abirabura bo muri Afurika .
Byagize ingaruka zikomeye ku birabura bose aho bava bakagera kugeza n'uyu munsi baracyahangana n'ibisigisigi by'izi ngaruka .
Ku ngoma y'Umwami Kigeli IV Rwabugili nibwo abaturage bo mu bihugu byo muri Afurika yo munsi y'ubutayu bwa Sahara no mu Karere k'Ibihugu byo mu Biyaga Bigari muri rusange , bari imari ishyushye ku isoko ry'ibihugu bya Amerika n'iby'Abarabu .
Rwabugili ni we mwami wenyine wanze gufata abaturage be ngo abagurishe .
Ahandi mu bindi bice bya Afurika bararaga bafata abagabo n'abagore bafite imbaraga bakabagurisha abazungu n'Abarabu .
Abami bagurishaga abacakara , bahabwa impano zitandukanye zirimo indorerwamo , amasaro , imyenda n'ibindi .
Umwanditsi akaba n'Impuguke mu mateka , Nsanzabera Jean de Dieu agaragaza ko Umwami Rwabugili yari yaramenye amahano Abarabu bari gukora mu Banyamwezi , mu Bagande , mu Banyoro n'i Karagwe n'ahandi hirya no hino mu karere .
Abarabu bafatanyije n'Abami baho bari bamaze igihe bafata abaturage babo bakabagurisha .
Umwami Rwabugili amaze kumenyeshwa ko Abarabu bageze ku nkengero z'Ikiyaga cya Tanganyika , yahaye itegeko ingabo ze ko umuntu wese w'uruhu rwera bazabona akandagira ku butaka bw'u Rwanda bagomba kumwica .
Hari amateka agaragaza ko mu 1871 , Abarabu ba mbere binjiye mu Rwanda baje gufata abantu , nta n'umwe warusohotsemo .
Ayo makuru barayabwiranye , baratinya cyane .
Nyuma bagerageje kureshya umwami Rwabugili , bamuzanira impano nyinshi zirimo amatungo , imyenda n'ibindi kugira ngo yemere kugurisha Abanyarwanda ariko arabyanga ni yo mpamvu abarabu benshi bakambitse bakagarukira hakurya y'Akagera , ntibatinyuke kwinjira mu Rwanda .
Rwabugili yababwiye ko Abaturage ari ab'Imana
Abakoraga ubucuruzi busanzwe buzwi bo barambukaga neza bakinjira bagacuruza bakongera bagasubira iwabo .
Abarabu bakoze ibishoboka byose ngo binjire mu Rwanda bafate abagabo n'abagore ariko umwami Rwabugili ababera ibamba .
Umushakashatsi akaba n'Impuguke mu mateka , Innocent Nizeyimana [ yanditse igitabo yise """" Ubumwe bw'Abanyarwanda mu mateka yabo """" ] avuga ko abanyarwanda n'Ubwami bwabo bari bazi agaciro k'ikiremwamuntu ndetse n'uburenganzira bwe , ari nayo mpamvu bamaganye icuruzwa ry'abantu .
Mu kiganiro yagiranye na RBA , Nizeyimana yavuze ko Rwabugili yakundaga abaturage be ku buryo n'ubwo byari bisanzwe bizwi ko abaturage ari rubanda rw'Umwami , kuri we atari ko byari bimeze .
Yagize ati """" Iki gihe cyo gucuruza abirabura , Rwabugili yarabahakaniye aravuga ati njyewe ntabwo nagurisha abanyarwanda kuko si abanjye , ahubwo ninjye wabo .
Abanyarwanda ni ab'Imana . """"
Nizeyimana avuga ko muri icyo gihe Abanyarwanda bitaga Umwami wabo , Nyagasani .
Ni ukuvuga ko yari ahagarariye Imana , iyi akaba ari nayo mpamvu bikekwako yatumye yanga ko abanyarwanda bagurwa mu bucakara .
Ati """" Abanyarwanda bumvaga ko Umwami ahagarariye Imana , none se Nyagasani yari kubagurisha ku banyamahanga ?
N'ubwo Umwami baje bakamwinginga yakomeje kwimana abaturage be . """"
Amateka agaragaza ko hari abantu bagurwaga mu Burundi no muri Congo , mu Burengerazuba bwa Afurika no Mu burasirazuba icyo gihe banyuzwaga mu Rwanda bagiye gupakirwa mu bwato bwo ku cyambu cya Dar es Salaalam bakanyuzwa mu Nyanja y'Abahinde .
Mu banyuzwaga mu Rwanda habaga harimo abana , abagore n'abandi bantu barwaye , u Rwanda rwababona kubera ubumuntu bwahoze buranga abanyarwanda , rugasaba ko abo bantu bagumishwa mu gihugu noneho u Rwanda rugatanga ingurane .
Nizeyimana ati """" Abanyarwanda barazaga bakabategera mu nzira , u Rwanda rukemera rugatanga amaturo rukabagura , rugatanga ihene nyinshi rukemera rukarenza kubyo bari batanze aho babaguze rwarangiza rubabwira ruti aba bantu ntabwo mwabagezayo dore bararembye bameze nabi . """"
Yakomeje agira ati """" Babaguraga n'Abarabu babaga babajyanye muri Tanzania ku cyambu , ibyo rero byose birakwereka ko u Rwanda cyari igihugu kihagazeho .
Ntirwigeze rugurisha abantu barwo ahubwo n'abanyamahanga rwarabaguraga rukemera rukabishyurira . """"
Lt Col Gérard Nyirimanzi , umwe mu bagize Urwego rw'Intwari , impeta n'Imidari y'Ishimwe akaba no mu Ishyirahamwe ry'Abacukumbuzi b'Ireme ry'Umuco n'Amateka by'u Rwanda , yavuze ko kimwe mu bigaragaza uko Rwabugiri yanze gucuruza abantu ari uko bamwise """" Bwana Mkali """" cyangwa se umugabo ukaze .
Ati """" Abacuruza abacakara bo byari byarabananiye kwinjira mu Rwanda ku buryo hari umucuruzi umwe wavuze ati """" Pale musiende wana , kuna Bwana Mkali , """" banavuga ko kariya gace kitwa Bwana Mukari banakitiriye uwo Rwabugiri wari waranze gucuruza abantu . """"
Nyirimanzi avuga ko no mu Rwanda hari hari amasoko yacururizwagaho abantu ariko babaga ari abavanywe mu bihugu byo hanze nka Repubulika Iharanira Demukarasi ya Congo .
Ati """" No mu Rwanda hari isoko ry'icuruzwa ry'abacakara ariko igihamya gihari ni uko Rwabugili yanze gucuruza abantu .
Babimusabye arabaseka cyane . """"
Umusizi Nsanzabera yavuze ko Rwabugili yanashyizeho ingabo zo kurwanya abacuruza abacakara , zishyirwa mu Bugesera ngo zihangena n'Abarabu .
Icyo gihe ngo hapfuye abarabu icumi .
Kigeli IV Rwabugili yari mwene Mutara II Rwogera na Nyirakigeli Murorunkwere .
Yimye mu mwaka w """" 1853 kugera muri Nzeri 1895 .
Hagiye gusohoka igitabo kivuga ibigwi bya Nyirarumaga mu mateka y'u Rwanda .
Nyirarumaga yabaye umugabekazi w'ingoboka w'umwami Ruganzu II Ndoli .
Nsanzabera yabwiye IGIHE ko yatekereje kwandika iki gitabo afite intego yo gukeza intwari zigaragaje mu mateka y'u Rwanda , umuco avuga ko ukwiye gucengera mu Banyarwanda , maze abanyabigwi barwubatse rugahamya igitinyiro bagahabwa urubuga rubasingiza .
Yagize ati """" Bafite amavugwa n'amarorwa mu Rwanda .
Igiti ntikimenyekana kubw'izina cyitwa , kimenyekana ku bw'imbuto cyera , ibikorwa byabo by'ubutaneshwa bikwiriye gushyirwa ahabona , buri wese akabigira ibye , bikamubera igikabuzo cyo kubaka ahazaza hazira icyasha . """"
Yavuze ko ibyo abanyarwanda bagezeho byose bagiye babiharanira bityo ko bakwiriye gushimira no kumenyekanisha intwari zose zagize uruhare ngo ibyiza igihugu cyagezeho kibigereho .
Ati """" Ibikorwa byubaka igihugu cy'u Rwanda , ubuhangange n'ubudasa , byagiye bigira intwari zabimburiye izindi mu kubyitangira haba mu kubihanga , mu kubyubaka no mu kubirinda .
Ntacyo Abanyarwanda twagezeho kubera amahirwe , ahubwo byose twarabiharaniye , tubigeraho twiyushye akuya .
Ni byiza ko twimakaza umuco wo gukeza no gusingiza intwari zagize icyo zikora ngo u Rwanda rube urwo ruri rwo uyu munsi . """"
Amateka agaragaza ko Nyirarumaga ari umwe mu bagore babaye ibihangange mu Rwanda , aho yarunambiye kugeza ku munota wa nyuma , akabundisha ( guhungisha ) Ruganzu mwene Cyamatare ubwo Abanyabyinshi bamuhigiraga kubura hasi no kubura hejuru ngo bamwivugane , ingoma y'u Rwanda bayegukane .
Nyirarumaga yemeye gucibwa intoki ebyiri ku gaherere ubwo yangaga gutangaza aho Ndoli yabundiye ( yahungiye ) ubwo bashakaga kumwica .
Ruganzu Ndoli yaje kwitura Nyirarumaga amugira umugabekazi w'ingoboka ku ngoma ye , kuko nyina Nyabacuzi ba Kibogora yari yaraguye mu miko y'abakobwa i Rubi rw'i Nyundo .
Nyirarumaga na Ndoli batwaye u Rwanda ahasaga mu wa 1510 - 1543 .
Ni umwe mu bagabekazi 27 u Rwanda rwagize akaba umwe mu bakoze ibikorwa by'ikirenga byubatse u Rwanda mu rwego ruhanitse mu bihe by'ingoma ye , cyane cyane ku kubaka umuco mbonera w'ubumuntu n'ubumana .
Kubaka imibereho n'imibanire y'Abanyarwanda , imyidagaduro n'ubuvanganzo no kurushaho gukuza agaciro k'umugore w'i Rwanda .
Abasizi bo bamwibukira ku kuba ariwe nyirakuruza wabo kuko ibisigo bya mbere ari ibye .
Nsanzabera yavuze ko abanyabigwi nka Nyirarumaga , bakwiye kubahwa no kwibuka ibihe byose , abakiri bato bagatozwa umuco w'ubutwari bushingiye ku bwitange no guhanga ibishya .
Iki gitabo """" Nyiraruganzu II Nyirarumaga , Inkingi mwikorezi y'umuco n'amateka y'u Rwanda """" kizajya hanze mu minsi mike iri imbere .
Kwagura Urukari no kubaka Umudugudu Ndangamuco : Umushinga wihariye mu Karere ka Nyanza .
Ni umushinga watangiye ku bufatanye bw'Akarere ka Nyanza n'Inteko y'Umuco , ukaba uzakorerwa ahitwa mu Rukari ahari Ingoro y'Abami b'u Rwanda no mu nkengero zaho ndetse no hafi y'Icyuzi cya Nyamagana .
Umuyobozi w'Akarere ka Nyanza , Ntazinda Erasme , yabwiye IGIHE ko batangiye uwo mushinga ari umwihariko bafite nk'icyerekezo cy'Akarere .
Ati """" Icyerekezo cy'akarere ni ukuba izingiro ry'ubukerarugendo bushingiye ku muco n'amateka .
Icyakozwe ni uko twagerageje gushaka uburyo bwo kwagura Urukari dufatanyije n'Ikigo cy'Igihugu cy'Ingoro z'Umurage w'u Rwanda . """"
Yavuze ko abaturage batuye mu nkengero z'Urukari aho ruzagurirwa bamaze guhabwa ingurane hakaba hasigaye igikorwa cyo gushaka amafaranga kugira ngo kubaka bitangire .
Yakomeje avuga ko umushinga wo kwagura urukari uzajyana no kubaka Umudugudu Ndangamuco hafi y'icyuzi cya Nyamagana .
Uwo mudugudu ubwawo uzakorerwa ku buso bwa hegitari icyenda , kandi ibikorwa byo kwimura abaturage byari byaratangiye ariko bidindizwa n'icyorezo cya Covid - 19 .
Mu bazimurwa ahazajya uwo mudugudu hose hamaze kwishyurwa ahangana na hegitari ebyiri , bikaba biteganyijwe ko abatarishyurwa bo bazongera kubarirwa kuko ibiciro byahindutse .
Ntanzida ati """" Hari habazwe amafaranga agera muri Miliyoni 200 ariko tuzongera tubare kuko hashize hafi imyaka ibiri , ubwo tuzongera tubare tubihe agaciro bundi bushya . """"
Akarere ka Nyanza kabumbatiye amateka menshi yiganjemo ayo hambere kuko Nyanza yabaye Umurwa Mukuru w'Ubwami kuva mu 1899 kugeza mu mu 1962 .
I Nyanza hatuwe n'Abami bane ari bo Kigeli IV Rwabugiri wari utuye ku misozi ya Mwima na Mushirarungu ; Yuhi IV Musinga watuye i Mwima na Gakenyeri ; Mutara III Rudahigwa watuye mu Rukali ndetse n'Umwami Kigeli V Ndahindurwa watuye i Busasamana .
Hari ingoro y'Abami yo mu Rukari , Ingoro y'Umurage wo Kwigira , Umusezero w'Abami , Ibigabiro , Inzira Gakondo z'Ubukerarugendo ; haboneka Amariba ya Mutende yafukuwe ku ngoma y'Umwami Mutara III Rudahigwa , aho Inyambo ze ndetse n'inka z'abaturage ziturutse imihanda yose zashokaga .
Hari kandi icyuzi cya Nyamagana cyafukujwe n'Umwami Mutara III Rudahigwa afatanyije na agoronome w'Umubiligi witwaga Dubois .
I Nyanza kandi hafatwa nk'igicumbi cy'ubutabera kuko hahoze urukiko umwami yaciragamo imanza .
Inyubako ziri mu Mujyi wa Nyanza zose zatakishijwe imitako gakondo ifite ibisobanuro bijyanye n'umuco nyarwanda hagamijwe kuwurimbisha ugasa neza ; kubungabunga amateka ndetse no kongera umubare w'abawusura kandi bakahatinda .
Hashyizweho kandi Inzira eshatu z'Ubukerarugendo gakondo za kinyarwanda zizwi na The Nyanza Cultural Trials , zitezweho kongera umubare w'abahasura .
Icyorezo cya Covid - 19 kitaraza Akarere ka Nyanza kasurwaga na ba mukerarugendo basaga ibihumbi 70 ku mwaka .
Umurage urubyiruko rukwiye kuvoma kuri Gihanga Ngomijana wahanze u Rwanda .
Ni ubutumwa yageneye abitabiriye Uruhererekane rw'Ibiganiro by'Umuco n'Amateka byiswe """" Amateka Series """" bitegurwa n'Urubyiruko ruba mu bihugu bya Australie na Nouvelle - Zélande .
Iyi gahunda igamije gufasha urubyiruko ruba mu mahanga kumenya Umuco n'Amateka by'u Rwanda .
Abitabiriye iki kiganiro cyabaye mu buryo bw'ikoranabuhanga , baganirijwe ku nkomoko y'u Rwanda rwahanzwe na Gihanga , ubutwari bwaranze Abanyarwanda ba mbere y'Ubukoloni ndetse n'uruhare rw'abagore n'urubyiruko mu gukomeza gusigasira uwo murage .
Abatanze ibiganiro barimo Minisitiri Bamporiki Edouard , Umuhanzi Mukankuranga Marie Jeanne [ Mariya Yohana ] n'Umunyarwanda uba mu Mujyi wa Perth muri Australie , Niyonzima Jean Paul .
Umuhanzi Icyoyitungiye Jules Bonheur [ Jules Sentore ] niwe wasusurukije abari bakurikiye ikiganiro .
Minisitiri Bamporiki yabwiye uru rubyiruko ko Gihanga atekereza umushinga wo kubaka u Rwanda , yasize intekerezo zihamye zishobora kuyobora abazabaho nyuma kandi zanafasha abariho uyu munsi .
Ati """" Gihanga yatumye tugira igihugu ariko aravuga ngo kugira igihugu ni ukumva ko ukirwanirira , ukavuga ngo nzagikorera iki , nzakimarira iki , nzagisigamo iki , ko ngisanzemo umurage njyewe nzasiga ndaze abandi iki ?
Ugasigara wumva ko ikitwa inyungu z'igihugu , ziruta kure inyungu z'undi muntu . """"
Minisitiri Bamporiki yavuze ko umuntu urutisha inyungu ze iz'igihugu aba ari kure cyane y'umurage wa Gihanga , aba ahemukira abakurambere n'Intwari z'u Rwanda kuko zo zari zizi ko nta cyaruta u Rwanda .
Ati """" Iyo ni impamba yaguherekeza aho uri dukura kuri Gihanga .
Ariko yavuze n'ibintu bikomeye , yaravuze ngo """" Uwubaka u Rwanda ntagegena yigeraho , arwubakana n'abato . """"
Ni nayo mpamvu igihugu cyacu cyahisemo guha inshingano abakiri bato kugira ngo abahari batagegena bigeraho bubaka u Rwanda . """"
Yakomeje agira ati """" Ni ikintu cyavuzwe na Gihanga , ni umurage tumwubahira uyu munsi .
Kwigira no kwishakamo ibisubizo , kwihangira imirimo n'ubunyamwuga tubyikoreye , tubyishatsemo .
Gihanga birimo no guhanga , uyu munsi ubwo twubaha Gihanga bidusigire n'intekerezo yo kuvuga ngo ndahanga iki ? """"
Mbere y'umwaduko w'Abakoloni babibye amacakubiri n """" ivangura mu Banyarwanda babacamo ibice kugira ngo babategeke , Abaturarwanda bari bunze ubumwe nk'umurage basigiwe na Gihanga .
Umurage wa Gihanga wakomeje gukura mu Banyarwanda ndetse nk'uko amateka abigaragaza mu 1500 , Abaryankuna banze guhemukira u Rwanda biyita abadahemuka banga kuruhemukira kugeza ku munota wa nyuma .
Minisitiri Bamporiki ati """" Banze guhemukira u Rwanda , badusigira umurage w'ubudahemuka , umwana w'umunyarwanda , urubyiruko n'ubwo yaba ari mundiba y'Isi , iyo bigeze ku Rwanda agomba kurubera umudahemuka .
Singahemuke , ntimugahemuke , mu ruhererekane dukomora kuri Gihanga byaduhaye Abadahemuka . """"
Mu 1700 , ku ngoma ya Cyilima II Rujugira , u Rwanda rwaratewe nabwo abantu bahagurukira rimwe biyita abataneshwa bararurwanira kandi batsinda ibihugu bine birimo u Burundi , Igisaka , Ndorwa n'u Bugesera .
Icyo gihe nibwo Umwami Cyilima yahise avuga ngo """" u Rwanda ruratera ntiruterwa . """"
Minisitiri Bamporiki avuga ko nyuma y'abataneshwa haje Abakoloni banesha abanyarwanda , babahimbira amoko y'Abatwa , Abatutsi n'Abahutu ari nabyo byagejeje kuri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 .
Ati """" Abakoloni bo mu 1890 bishyira mu 1900 , batangira kutureba bati ariko wowe waturutse aha , undi bati wowe waturutse aha .
Barabivangavanga bica umurage , bica indangagaciro , bica igihugu bitugeza kuri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi . """"
Akomeza avuga ko Inkotanyi zabohoye u Rwanda zabahaye umurage w'abadaheranwa zakomoye kuri Gihanga , ari nawo ukomeye urubyiruko rw'ubu rukwiye gusigasira .
Yakomeje agira ati """" Umuntu yagutsinda ariko ntiyaguherana .
Rero rubyiruko aho muri hose , ntihagire uheranwa n'ubusinzi , ubwomanzi ubwo aribwo bwose , mwishakemo imibereho , umunyarwanda arababara , aratsindwa arakubitika ariko ntaheranwa .
Niko Inkotanyi zatwigishije . """"
Umuhanzikazi Mariya Yohana yabwiye urubyiruko by'umwihariko abakobwa ko bakwiye gukurikiza umurage barazwe n'abakurambere babo barimo ba Ndabaga n'abandi bagiye bagaragaza ubutwari bwo gukorera u Rwanda .
Yagarutse ku ruhare abakobwa n'abagore bagize mu rugamba rwo kubohora igihugu no guhagarika Jenoside .
Ati """" Abagore ntabwo bigeze bicara ku gushyira u Rwanda imbere , ari ibya cyera hari abagore bagize ishyaka , bagize agaciro kanini n'ubu twibuka , birashoboka ko ari nabo tureberaho .
Bana bacu rubyiruko namwe turashaka kuzabavuga nk'uko tuvuga abo bagore ariko kandi mugomba kumenya ko u Rwanda mugomba kururirimba kandi niko gaciro kanyu . """"
Gahunda ya """" Amateka Series , """" ni umushinga watangijwe mu Ukuboza 2020 , ukubiyemo ubukangurambaga bwatangijwe n'urubyiruko ruba mu mahanga hagamijwe kwigisha bagenzi babo , yaba ababa hirya no hino mu mahanga ndetse n'abari mu Rwanda , ibijyanye n'amateka y'u Rwanda hamwe n'ubugeni mu ngeri zitandukanye .
Beata Umubyeyi Mairesse yahawe igihembo """" """" Prix des Cinq Continents de la Francophonie """" """" ( Video ) .
"""" """" Prix des Cinq Continents de la Francophonie """" """" ni igihembo gihabwa intyoza mu buvanganzo , cyatangiye gutangwa mu 2001 bigizwemo uruhare n'Umuryango Mpuzamahanga w'ibihugu bikoresha Igifaransa ( OIF ) .
Gihabwa igitabo cy'umwanditsi wagaragaje umwihariko mu guteza imbere Ururimi rw'Igifaransa .
Umubyeyi wegukanye iki gihembo yavuze ko yishimiye kukibona ndetse ari icy'ingenzi mu rugendo rwe nk'umwanditsi .
Yatangiye kwandika afite imyaka 30 ndetse icyo gihe ntiyizeraga ko azaba umwanditsi w'ibitabo .
Yakomeje ati """" """" Nakunze gusoma kuva kera nkiri muto cyane , ngira amahirwe yo kuvukira mu Mujyi wa Butare , wari ufite inzu z'amasomero , izigurishirizwamo ibitabo n'ububiko bwabyo .
Tukiri abana byaradufashaga cyane kubona ibitabo ukabivanamo ubumenyi bwinshi , harimo kugukundisha na we kuzaba wavamo umwanditsi , ukiga neza ururimi usomamo n'ibindi .
Ni ho hampaye imbaraga zo kwandika no kubikunda . """" """"
Mu kiganiro cyihariye IGIHE , uyu mwanditsi yavuze ku gitabo cye """" """" Tous tes enfants dispersés """" , """" bishatse kuvuga """" """" Abana bawe bose batatanye """" """" cyamuhesheje igihembo .
IGIHE : Wakiriye ute iki gihembo ?
Umubyeyi : """" Prix des Cinq Continents de la Francophonie """" ni igihembo gikomeye nishimiye cyane , barampamagaye mu minsi ishize barabimbwira .
Ni igihembo gitangwa biciye mu kanama nkemurampaka ( Jury ) gashinzwe ijonjora , riba rigizwe n'abanditsi bakomeye bo mu bihugu byinshi bitandukanye bivuga Igifaransa .
Kari kayobowe na Paula Jacques , Jean - Marie Gustave Le Clézio , Lise Bissonnette , Ananda Devi , Hubert Haddad , Monique Ilboudo , Vénus Khoury - Ghata , Liliana Lazar , Wilfried N'Sondé , René de Obaldia , Lyonel Trouillot , Abdourahman Waberi , Jun Xu et Gilles Jobidon .
Aba barimo n'abigeze guhabwa iki gihembo .
Babanje guhitamo ibitabo by'abanditsi 10 , muri ibyo bakuramo ibindi bibiri bihembwa , ari na ho icyanjye cyaje ku isonga gikurikirwa n'icya Paul Kawaczak , umwanditsi w'imyaka 34 wo muri Québec .
Iki gitabo rero kikaba ari nacyo cya mbere nanditse mu buryo bwa Roman , bikaba byaranshimishije ko bwa mbere cyabonye igihembo .
IGIHE : Ni iyihe mpamvu wagize amahitamo yo kwandika roman aho kwibanda ku buhamya bw'amateka ya Jenoside warokotse ?
Umubyeyi : Ni byo koko kwandika ubuhamya kuri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi ni ibintu nubaha bikomeye .
Nshima kandi ngasanga ababikoze kugeza ubu ari ubutwari , kuva nagera hano mu Bufaransa nyuma yo kurokoka , uko hasohokaga igitabo kirimo ubuhamya naragisomaga , abenshi turi no mu kigero kimwe ndabazi .
Ibitabo byabo birakomeye cyane ku mateka yacu , kuko bituma abantu bamenya ibyakorewe Abatutsi muri kiriya gihe ku buryo nyabwo bivugwa n'ababibayemo babikorewe , bigatuma nta warengera avuga ibindi bitari byo .
Njye rero kwandika mu buryo bwa Roman hari impamvu nyinshi zabinteye , imwe muri izo ni uko wenda nari ntaragira ubwo butwari bwo kuvuga amateka yanjye .
Njya mbabazwa cyane n'Abafaransa bamwe usanga bavuga ngo ni amateka yabereye kure muri Afurika , mbese ugasanga bisa nkaho bitabareba , ariko Jenoside iyo ariyo yose ni icyaha cy'iyicarubozo kireba ikiremwamuntu cyose ku Isi .
Mu kwandika rero inkuru karemano ( Roman ) n'inkuru yihariye mba nshaka kwerekana ariko bitavuze ko ari amateka muri rusange aho uhuza abantu batandukanye mu nkuru ishobora kubaho ariko mpimbano .
Hari aho usanga ya mateka yo muri Jenoside ajemo , noneho wa muntu usoma igitabo uwo ariwe wese n'umugabane yaba aherereyemo wose , na we ashobora kumva bimureba cyangwa bisa n'ibyo yaciyemo , atavuze ko byabereye kure bitamureba .
Ubwo rero ni bwo buryo bwanjye bwo kuvuga ibintu bikomeye ariko bikakirwa mu buryo bworohera uwo ari we wese kandi akibonamo .
Hari umwanditsi wo mu Bwongereza witwa Zedie Smith wanditse mu gitabo cye inyandiko ya nyayo ya David Foster Wallace ngo """" La bonne littérature est faite pour réconforter les gens dérangés et déranger les gens confortables """" , """" bivuze ngo """" Inyandiko nziza ifasha abatameze neza kubera ibibazo bahuye nabyo mu buzima wenda , ikanababaza abari bamerewe neza
bashaka ko ikibi kitavugwa muri rusange . """" """"
Hari uba afite intimba ku mutima yasoma inkuru akumva hari abandi bahuje akababaro akumva biramufashije nkuko mu Rwanda bakunda kuvuga bati """" Si urw'umwe """" kuko abona muri iyo nkuru harimo abakomeza umutsi , bagakora ku buryo bagira ejo heza habo , na we bikamugiraho ingaruka nziza .
Aho abandi twavuze baba badashaka gusoma ibintu bikomeye babona gusa umutwe w'inkuru ko uvuga kuri Jenoside agahita avuga ati """" Sinshaka gusoma ibintu bintera umutwe aribo nise ( les gens confortables ) .
Muri make ni uko nabonye ibyiza byo gukoresha inkuru karemano .
IGIHE : Mu gitabo wibanze ku byo wise Métissage na Transmission , gifite uburemere bw'uruhererekane rw'umuco , uburere , ingiro ku cyo umuntu ari cyo ukanagaruka kuri Jenoside .
Iki gitekerezo cyo guhuza ibintu biremereye by'ingeri nyinshi cyakujemo gite ?
Umubyeyi : Byaturutse ahantu henshi , mu bitabo nasomye by'abanditsi batandukanye harimo n'abaturuka mu Birwa bya Antilles .
Abirabura bo muri Amerika n'abandi benshi bavuze amateka y'abirabura muri Diaspora ku Isi yose niho navuga navanye inganzo ( inspiration ) .
Ikindi ni uko umuntu ashobora no kwandika agendeye ku mateka azi nk'aya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi cyangwa kuba imvange y'umwirabura n'umuzungu ( Métisse ) nkuko Gaël Faye avuga ati """" ni hagati y'imigezi ibiri hagati y'intebe ebyiri . """"
Njyewe mu Rwanda batubwiraga ko turi abazungu , njyeze mu Bufaransa batwita abirabura .
Ibyo rero ni ibintu abantu benshi usanga baranyuzemo .
Icyo nagerageje gukora muri iki gitabo """" Tous tes enfants dispersés """" mu bihe bishize , ni ukuvuga nk'umukecuru wavukiye mu Rwanda , avukirayo , abyirukirayo , ahura n'Umufaransa barashakana babyarana umwana wa mbere bise Blanche , nyuma aza kubyara n'undi mwana yise Bosco , ariko we amubyarana n'Umunyarwanda bakundanye bakiri mu
mashuri yisumbuye .
Ubwo rero ukabona hari umwana umwe w'Umu - métisse , undi w'Umunyarwanda , kuri uwo mubyeyi ubarera wenyine , hakaba n'ibyo atababwira kubera umuco w'Abanyarwanda akenshi ababyeyi batavuga bumva ko ari ukurengera umwana ariko abana bakazakura bibaza ku mateka yaho bakomoka mu miryango yacu n'ibindi .
Icyo gihe rero mu Rwanda intambara yatangiye wa mwana Bosco ajya mu Inkotanyi , wa mubyeyi agumana n'umukobwa we .
Jenoside itangiye abwira uwo mukobwa ati """" Wowe uri Métisse jyana na bariya bazungu bava i Butare utoroke ugende uzagere i Burayi mu gihugu cya so uzarokokereyo .
Uwo mubyeyi na we yagize amahirwe aza kurokoka .
Igitabo gitangira Blanche umukobwa we yarize i Burayi mu Bufaransa ararangiza , ashaka umugabo w'umu - métisse na we aza gushaka uko yataha mu Rwanda gusura nyina na musaza we Bosco .
Nyuma rero igitabo kivuga ukuntu muri uwo muryango habaye agahinda kenshi n'ibintu byinshi bitabashije kuganirwaho kuko byagumye mu mitima yabo bikabatera intimba nyinshi .
Umubyeyi yagaragaje ko iki ari ikibazo kibaho ku miryango myinshi ivukamo aba - métisse ndetse yashakaga ko ibyo yashyize mu gitabo byaba imbarutso y'ibiganiro kugira ngo abana babakomokaho bazabashe kubaho neza no kumenya inkomoko yabo .
Uyu mwanditsi avuga ko mu myandikire ye akunda kwerekana imitekerereze itandukanye ku kintu runaka , cyangwa gufungura ibiganiro , kuko abantu bose batabona ibintu kimwe .
Umubyeyi ufite ubwenegihugu bw'u Rwanda n'u Bufaransa , yarokotse Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi ; yavukiye i Butare - Ngoma , ubu ni mu Karere ka Huye , mu 1979 .
Afite abana babiri akaba atuye mu Mujyi wa Bordeaux mu Bufaransa .
Musenyeri Alexis Kagame na Mgr Bigirumwami : Intwari zibagiranye ?
Babayeho mu bihe bimwe , byari bikomeye u Rwanda ruri mu maboko y'Ababiligi ariko baharanira ko amateka n'umuco nyarwanda bitibagirana , nk'imwe mu nkingi ikomeye yatumye igihugu kimara imyaka ibihumbi gishikamye .
Musenyeri Alexis Kagame yavutse tariki 15 Gicurasi 1912 i Kiyanza mu Buliza ( ubu ni mu Karere ka Rulindo , Umurenge wa Ntarabana ) , hari ku ngoma y'Umwami Yuhi V Musinga .
Yahawe ubupadiri mu 1941 .
Kagame ni umwe mu banyarwanda ba mbere bize kaminuza , ayiga mu mahanga mu bijyanye na filozofiya .
Mu mateka y'u Rwanda azwi nk'umwe mu ba mbere bakozeho ubushakashatsi butandukanye , yandika ibitabo byatumye abiga amateka bamenya aho bahera birimo nk'Inganji Kalinga , un abrégé de l'ethno - histoire du Rwanda .
Yanditse ibindi bitabo byinshi n'inyandiko yamenyekanye nk'Indyoheshabirayi , Umuririmbyi wa Nyiribiremwa , Isoko y'Amajyambere , La Philosophie Bantu - Rwandaise de l """" être """" n'ibindi .
Musenyeri Aloys Bigirumwami we yavutse kuwa 22 Ukuboza 1904 avukira i Gisaka i Zaza .
Mu 1952 yagizwe Musenyeri wa Nyundo , abimburira abandi birabura kwambikwa iryo kamba muri Afurika Mbiligi yari igizwe n'u Rwanda , u Burundi na Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo .
Mu 1954 , Musenyeri Bigirumwami yashinze akanyamakuru k'abana kitwa Hobe kamamaye cyane , kugira ngo bamenyere gusoma babone n'inkuru basoma mu Kinyarwanda .
Yanditse inyandiko zibanda ku muco n'imyemerere ya Kinyarwanda zirimo ; Imigani miremire ( 1972 ) , Imana y'abantu , abantu b'Imana , Imana mu bantu , abantu mu Mana ( 1979 ) ndetse n'Imihango , Imiziro n'imiziririzo mu Rwanda ( 1984 ) byose bigaruka ku muco nyarwanda .
Nubwo ibikorwa by'aba bagabo bitavugwa cyane , ni bimwe mu byabimburiye ubundi bushakashatsi bacukumbuye amateka n'umuco nyarwanda .
Ikirenzeho bagiye babikora nta zindi nyungu barambirijeho .
Buruga Aloys Gonzague , murumuna wa Musenyeri Alexis Kagame mu muryango , aherutse kubwira IGIHE ko mukuru we akwiriye guhabwa agaciro kuko ibyo yakoze ari iby'ubutwari .
Yagize ati """" Hari ubwo intwari ziba izo ku rugamba , izaguye igihugu zikagitsindira abanzi ariko hakwiriye kubaho n'abo twakwita abakurambere bafite ibindi bakoze bifitiye igihugu akamaro . """"
"""" Tumwise intwari , si ikigwari kuko yarwanye urugamba rw'uko umuco w'u Rwanda utazima , aharanira ko amateka y'u Rwanda atazimira ayashyira mu nyandiko .
Navuga ngo yakwibukwa nk'intwari . """"
Muri abo bombi , Musenyeri Kagame niwe wahawe impeta y'ishimwe , kuwa 5 Nyakanga mu 1979 ubwo yagirwaga """" Officier de l'ordre national des Grands lacs . """"
Kuwa 3 Nzeri 2014 , yahawe igihembo n'Inteko Nyarwanda y'Ururimi n'Umuco cyiswe """" Igihembo cya Akademi , """" cyashyizweho hagamijwe gushima abantu bakora ibikorwa by'indashyikirwa mu kubungabunga ubusugire n'iterambere by'ururimi n'umuco by'u Rwanda .
Icyakora hari ababona abo bagabo nk'abitanze batizigama ngo umuco nyarwanda n'amateka yarwo adasibangana , ku buryo bakwiriye ubutwari cyangwa impeta z'ishimwe bihanitse kandi ibikorwa byabo bikagaragara henshi .
Umunyamabanga Nshingwabikorwa w'urwego rushinzwe Intwari z'Igihugu , Impeta n'Imidari by'ishimwe , Nkusi Déo , yabwiye IGIHE ko Musenyeri Bigirumwami na Musenyeri Kagame batibagiranye nkuko bamwe babikeka , kuko gushyirwa mu ntwari cyangwa guhabwa umudari runaka , hakorwa ubushakashatsi bwimbitse .
Ubusanzwe kugira ngo umuntu akorweho ubushakashatsi bushobora kumushyira mu ntwari , hagomba kuba hari ababimusabiye cyangwa se urwego rubishinzwe rukibwiriza .
Nkusi yagize ati """" Abo bantu babiri rero ni abantu bazwi cyane mu mateka kandi birumvikana banakoze n'ibintu byinshi ku byerekeye amateka n'umuco , bafite inyandiko zinadusfsha nk'abanyarwanda ku bintu byinshi cyane , byumvikane rero ko abo bantu batibagiranye . """"
Nkusi yavuze ko kuba ibitabo n'inyandiko za Musenyeri Kagame na Bigirumwami bikoreshwa mu mashuri atandukanye no mu zindi nzego , nabwo ari ubundi buryo bwo kubaha agaciro .
Ntabwo yeruye ngo avuge niba haba hari ubushakashatsi buri kubakorwaho , kuko bitemewe kubitangaza ubushakashatsi butararangira , icyakora yumvikanishije ko hari ikiri gukorwa .
Ati """" Twakiriye amazina menshi cyane y'abantu batandukanye , birumvikana ko abantu bazwi cyane ntibabura n'ababavuga ariko inshingano zo kuvuga uwakozweho ubushakashatsi ntabwo ari izacu , hari inzego zibishinzwe igihe nikigera zizababwira ubushakashatsi icyo bwatanze . """"
Nkusi yavuze ko gukora ubushakashatsi ku muntu kugira ngo abe yagirwa intwari cyangwa yahabwa umudari bifata igihe kandi bigasaba ubushishozi buhambaye .
Ati """" Si nko kwatsa itara ngo pa ! riratse cyangwa rirazimye , ni ibintu bifata igihe , byitonderwa bigaca mu nzgeo zitandukanye akaba yashyirwa mu rwego runaka rw'intwari cyangwa yahabwa impeta y'ishimwe bitewe n'ibikorwa bye . """"
Kugeza ubu hari amazina asaga 200 y'abanyarwanda basabiwe gukorwaho ubushakashatsi kugira ngo bashyirwe mu ntwari , abandi babe bambikwa impeta z'ishimwe .
Kuwa 2 Ukuboza 1981 nibwo Musenyeri Alexis Kagame yitabye Imana aguye mu bitaro by'i Nairobi muri Kenya aho yari yagiye kwivuza .
Aloys Bigirumwami we yatabarutse afite imyaka 81 ku wa 03 Kamena 1986 mu bitaro bya Ruhengeri azize indwara y'umutima .
Ikiganiro n'Umunyamabanga Nshingwabikorwa CHENO , Nkusi Déo .
Menya byinshi ku bakurambere biziritse ku Rwanda bakanga kururekura .
Birashoboka ko u Rwanda rwari kuba rungana nka Seychelles , agahugu gato kaba muri Afurika , ariko kubera abami barurwaniriye bakagenda barwagura , bakarwizirakaho bamwe bagahara n'ubuzima bwabo , rwabaye u Rwanda rugari , nubwo abakoloni batarurebeye izuba bakarugabagabanya mu nama yabereye i Berilini .
Mu kiganiro RBA yagiranye n'abanyamateka batandukanye barimo Kalisa Rugano impuguke mu muco n'amateka ; Umuraza Landrada , komiseri mu itorero ry'igihugu ndetse n'umwanditsi w'amateka , Nizeyimana Innocent , bagarutse cyane ku butwari bukomeye bwaranze abanyarwanda kuva kera , harimo n'abami b'u Rwanda Ruganzu Bwimba ndetse na Ruganzu II Ndoli .
Ruganzu Bwimba niwe mwami wenyine w'u Rwanda wameneye igihugu amaraso
Mu bami barurwaniriye bakarwizirakaho , harimo Ruganzu Bwimba wategetse u Rwanda mu wa 1312 - 1345 , akarumenera amaraso , akemera kuba umutabazi w'umucengeri ari umwami , kugira ngo u Rwanda rwigarurire i Gisaka .
Umutabazi w'umucengeri ni umuntu wiyemezaga kuba igitambo akemera kumena amaraso mu gihugu cy'amahanga agamije kurinda u Rwanda no kurwagura .
Kalisa Rugano yavuze ko ibi byabaye ubwo i Gisaka cyashakaga kwigarurira u Rwanda bikabananira , niko kwiga umutwe wo gushaka mushiki wa Bwimba , Robwa Nyiramateke , kugira ngo azahabyarire umwana w'umuhungu maze agire u Rwanda ingaruzwamuheto , kuko yari kuba ari umunyarwanda akaba n'umunyagisaka .
Kugira ngo baramire u Rwanda byasabye ko Robwa apfa umwana ntavuke , ariko mu muco wa kera byari ngombwa ko hagira n'undi bapfana maze bikitwa ko batabaye u Rwanda .
Bararaguje ngo barebe uwo indagu zifata , maze zemeza ko ari Nkurukumbe nyirarume wa Ruganzu Bwimba ugomba kuba umutabazi w'umucengeri .
Abyumvise ahimba amayeri atuma atajya gupfira u Rwanda , nuko birakaza umwami Ruganzu maze ubwe yiyemeza kwitabarira bucengeli .
Aba abaye umwami wa mbere n'uwa nyuma mu mateka y'u Rwanda umeneye igihugu amaraso .
Ruganzu II Ndoli yategetse u Rwanda nyuma y'imyaka 11 rwarigaruriwe n'abanyamahanga
Undi mwami wamenyekanye cyane , wagaragaje ubutwari bukomeye ni Ruganzu Ndoli , wategetse u Rwanda akiri muto ku myaka 33 , akarukura mu maboko y'abanyabungo nyuma y'imyaka 11 bararwigaruriye .
Nizeyimana Innocent agaruka ku butwari bwe , yavuze ko hambere havutse amakimbirane hagati ya se Ndahiro II Cyamatare n'abavandimwe be aribo Byinshi na Bamara maze bagambanira u Rwanda , bituma rwigarurirwa n'abanyabungo .
Akomeza avuga ukuntu barugabagabanye , bakarutobanga aho bamaze imyaka 11 bari mu Rwanda .
Abahanuzi b'umwami babonye ko ibintu biri gufata indi ntera ni ko guterana babwira umwami ko yashaka ukuntu yohereza Ruganzu Ndoli kwa nyirasenge Nyabunyana wari warashatswe n'umwami w'i Karagwe ( Tanzania y'ubu ) .
Yagiye kwa nyirasenge mu buryo bwo kumuhungisha kugira ngo atazapfa , arindwe neza , yigishwe ategurwe kuzaba umwami , azaze aje gutabara u Rwanda .
Ni ko byagenze koko , arategurwa agaruka mu Rwanda .
Yagiye mu Rwanda se na nyina na nyirakuru barishwe , aza afite agahinda ariko ntiyihorera , aza aje gutabara abanyarwanda .
Ntabwo yagiye arwituramo kuko nta bantu bari bamuzi uretse abiru n'abatware b'i Bwami , yagiye arurwanirira yica mwene se Byinshi wari waragambaniye u Rwanda , aramunyaga igihugu agisigaramo wenyine ari umwami w'u Rwanda .
Ruganzu Ndoli yamenyekanye ku bintu byinshi , birimo ko yari azi ubwenge bwinshi cyane , yiswe Cyambarantama ndetse n'ingabo ze zitwaga ibisumizi .
Hari n'abandi bami benshi bagaragaje ubutwari barimo na Mutara III Rudahigwa , bimanye u Rwanda bakanarurwanira ishyaka .
Nsanzabera yashyize hanze igitabo gikubiyemo ikinamico yise """" Ingizi yabwo ntiyabugaruriwe . """"
Kamere y'iki gitabo cy'amapaji 56 , ni iy'Ikinamico zishobora gukinwa mu ruhame cyangwa se kuri Radiyo .
Ikaba ari Ikinamico yimakaza umuco wo kubabarira no gusaba imbabazi , ubumwe n'ubwiyunge , no kurwanya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi n'ingengabitekerezo yayo .
Mu kiganiro na IGIHE , Nsanzabera yagize ati """" N'ubwo umutima muhanano utuzura igituza , ariko ntujya uganza umutima w'imbabazi n'ubugiraneza burenga akahise bukubakira ku ntego yo kwimakaza amahoro n'imico mbonera y'ubumuntu """"
Si kenshi uwabereye undi imfura , akabugirira n'abandi , abwiturwa n'abo yabugiriye .
Nibyo byabaye ku musaza Rusaneza n'umugore we Nyirayuhi , batengushywe n'abaturanyi babo Rukarabankaba n'umugore we Nyirabyavu , babakoreye ibya mfura mbi kandi baranabagabiye Inka , bakababera abaturanyi beza .
Umukecuru Nyirayuhi , ni urugero rwiza rwo kurenga imitekerereze yo kubakira ku nzika , yimakaje kubabarira abamwiciye abana n'umugabo , arahindukira abahindura abana be , ndetse yiyemeza no kubaha umurage mu kigwi cy'abe batakiriho .
Nsanzabera yavuze ko urwo ari urugero rwiza buri wese akwiye kugira urwe , agaharanira kwimakaza umuco wo kubabarira .
Yavuze ko yifuza ko uzasoma iyi Kinamico cyangwa se uzayibona bayikina , izamubera urugero rwiza rw'ubutwari bwo kubabarira ku biciwe no gusaba imbabazi ku bishe imbaga y'Abatutsi muri Jenoside .
Ibitabo byanditswemo iyi Kinamico """" Ingizi yabwo ntiyabugaruriwe , """" byamaze kugera ku isoko , aho biboneka mu maguriro y'ibitabo nka Caritas no mu Ikirezi i Kigali .
Urwibutso ku miterere y'ibirango by'u Rwanda mu mateka y'impitagihe .
Kuva mu bihe by'Abami kugeza mu bya Repubulika , u Rwanda rwanyuze mu bihe bitandukanye bijyanye n'inkingi zikomeye igihugu cyubakiraho , bigatuma gihamya igitinyiro mu ruhando rw'ibindi .
Mu ihanga ry'ibihugu kuva u Rwanda rwaturwa ahasaga mu mwaka wa 300 , haremwe ibihugu bigera kuri 29 bya mbere y'uko urwa Gasabo rubaho .
Buri gihugu cyagize ikirango cyariho muri ibyo bihe cyitwaga """" Ingoma Ngabe """" wagereranya n'ibendera ry'igihugu .
Ikirangantego ni cyo cyari izina ryayo , ryabaga rikagiriyemo ibigwi bya ba nyiracyo n'intego bafite mu iyubaka bihugu byabo .
Muri ibyo bihe ni bwo ibihugu byose byahuriye ku kuramvura ingoma mu biti , bakayiha ishusho bashaka , bakayita izina rikagiriyemo intego zabo n'icyerekezo baganamo .
Aha ni ho dusanga nk'Ingoma Ngabe y'u Bugesera yitwaga Rukombamazi , iy """" u Bushiru ikitwa Nkundubushiru , iy'u Bungwe ikitwa Nyamibande , iy'u Rweya ikitwa Sera ,
iy'u Budaha n'u Bwishaza ikitwa Mpatsibihugu , iy'i Gisaka ikitwa Rukurura , iy'u Buliza ikitwa Bushizimbeho , iy'u Bwanacyambwe ikitwa Kamuhagama , iya Nduga ikitwa Nyabihinda , iy'u Bunyabungo ikitwa Karyamahugu , iy'u Bunyambilili ikitwa Nkunzurwanda , iy'u Bukunzi ikitwa Nyamuganza , iy'u Bugoyi ikitwa Nyamwishyura , iy'u Burera ikitwa Bazarubaze , iya Rwankeri y'Abalindi ikitwa Kabuce , iya Rwankeri y'Abaguyane ikitwa
Ndahaze , iy'u Bukonya ikitwa Ruvugamahame , iy'u Buhoma ikitwa Nkandagiyabagome , iy'u Bwanamwali ikitwa Rugoruhindingoma , iya Bugamba - Kigamba ikitwa Kayenzi - Iravumera , iya Cyingogo ikitwa Simugomwa , iy'i Ndorwa ikitwa Murorwa , iy'u Bugara ikitwa Rugara .
Ibi bihugu byose byabaga bifite ibyangombwa byuzuye ngo bibe biganje , bifite ubusugire bwabyo n'ubutavogerwa ku Isi , harimo n'ingoma ngabe nk'ibendera ry'igihugu n'ikirangantego cya ba nyiracyo .
Ni cyo cyatumye byitwa ibihugu n'ubwo wasangaga bifite ubutaka buto bungana n'akarere k'iki gihe cyangwa se ugasanga hari n'aho kamwe karimo ibihugu bibiri .
Muri iyi nkuru tugiye guterura amateka y'ibirango by'u Rwanda mu mateka yanzikira ku ihangwa ry'igihugu kugeza mu bihe bya Repubulika .
Ibirango bya Gihanga ahanga u Rwanda
Amateka yerekana ko u Rwanda rwahanzwe na Gihanga cya Kazi ahasaga mu wa 1091 .
Ahanga u Rwanda , yasanze rugandagajemo ibihugu 24 , icye cya Gasabo cyaje kubyara u Rwanda kiba icya 25 , hiyongeraho n'ibindi bine byahanzwe n'abana be mu bisigara by'ubutaka bwasigaye bahanga ibindi bihugu .
Mu ihangwa ry'u Rwanda , Gihanga na we yaje muri uwo mujyo wo kugira ibirango by'igihugu ariko bitandukanye n'iby'abami b'ibindi bihugu byamutanze kurema kuri ubu butaka .
Ibirango Gihanga yahanganye u Rwanda birimo urusengo , inyundo n'umuriro kandi byose byari bifite igisobanuro muri icyo gihe .
Urusengo : Ni igikoresho cy'umuziki cyashushanyaga ubwisanzure , ubusugire n'ibitaramo by'abaturage bafite amahoro , cyiswe """" Nyamilinga . """"
Iri zina rikomoka ku nshinga yitwa """" Kulinga """" """" isobanura """" Icyizere ntagamburuzwa cy'ahazaza h'igihugu kiramye . """"
Inyundo : Gihanga yahanganye u Rwanda inyundo isanzwe bifashisha mu bucuzi .
Yayihaye izina rya """" Nyarushara , """" bivuga """" Inyundo yacuze Abami , igahanga igihugu . """"
Umuriro : Umuriro uvugwa hano wagombaga guhora waka ubutazima .
Washushanyaga """" Uburame bw'ubwami , ubumwe bw'Abanyarwanda n'ubusugire bw'igihugu . """"
Ibirango by'ibihugu byiyunze bikaba kimwe
Ahasaga mu 1100 , ni bwo Gihanga yahaye igitekerezo Abami b'Abasangwabutaka cyo guhuza ibihugu bito bafite kandi bitubakitse , bakarema igihugu kimwe kigwije igitinyiro .
Aya masezerano yasinyiwe i Nkotsi na Bikara mu Buhanga [ Ubu ni mu Murenge wa Nkotsi mu Karere ka Musanze ] .
Nyuma yo kwemeranya ayo masezerano y'ihuzabihugu , bahise barema ikirango cy'igihugu gishya cy'ibihugu byiyunze .
Icyo kirango cyabaye Ingoma Ngabe Rwoga yaramvuwe na Nyamuhindura wa Rubunga w'Umusinga w'Umurenge , bakura igisekuruza cyabo ku Basinga b'Abasangwabutaka .
Ingoma - Ngabe """" RWOGA """" isobanura """" Kogera cyangwa Kwamamara . """"
Kuva Rwoga yaremwa , u Rwanda rwahise ruyigira iyarwo , kubera ko arirwo rwahawe ubunyamabanga nshingwabikorwa bushyira mu bikorwa umushinga w'ukwiyunga kw'ibihugu , n'ubwo bwose byari bitariyunga ngo bibe kimwe .
Kuva ubwo ibirango Gihanga yahanganye u Rwanda , byasimbuwe na Rwoga ariko bikomeza kuba mu mihango y'iyimikabami b'u Rwanda no mu yindi y'ubucamanza , iyo gutangiza intambara , kohera ibiza n'ibyorezo byabaga byibasiye igihugu .
Ibirango by'u Rwanda byaremwe na Ruganzu Ndoli
Nyuma y'aho bicikiye i Rubi rw'i Nyundo , bene Gahima barwaniye ingoma Ndahiro Cyamatare akahagwa , ingoma ngabe Rwoga ikanyagwa n'Abanyabungo u Rwanda rukamara imyaka 11 ruraranze , Ruganzu Ndoli amaze kubundura u Rwanda , yahise arema indi ngoma ngabe isimbura Rwoga yari yaranyazwe n'Abanyabungo .
Ingoma ngabe Ruganzu Ndoli yaremye , ni yo yiswe Kalinga mu mateka y'ibirango by'u Rwanda .
Kalinga yaramvuwe mu Ishyamba rya Cyungo ho muri Cyungo ( ubu ni mu Murenge wa Cyungo mu Karere ka Rulindo ) , iramvurwa na Minyaruko ya Nyamikenke ahasaga mu wa 1510 .
Imihango y'iramvura rya Kalinga yateguriwe kwa Minyaruko ya Nyamikenke mu Busigi ( ubu ni mu Mirenge ya Bushoki , Tumba na Mbogo yo mu Karere ka Rulindo ) , ha handi yarasukiye bwa mbere , mu ijoro yabundukiyemo ubwo yageraga i Rwanda .
Igisobanuro cy'Ingoma Ngabe Kalinga , ari na cyo kirangantego za ba nyiri u Rwanda , usanga n'ubundi gisa n'icya Nyamilinga yahangiweho u Rwanda .
Igisobanuro cya Kalinga n'ubundi gikomoka ku nshinga Kulinga , Kalinga yo bikavuga """" Inkingi y'icyizere cy'ahazaza . """"
Ibirango by'ingoma ya cyami by'agateganyo ku bwa Rudahigwa
Mu bihe abakoloni b'Ababiligi bari mu Rwanda , batangiye kugerageza ikirangantego cy'ingoma ya cyami mu buryo bwa kizungu butandukanye n'ingoma ngabe Kalinga yariho muri ibyo bihe .
Icyo gitekerezo bakizanye ku ngoma y'Umwami Mutara Rudahigwa mu 1935 , nyuma y'uko bamaze kureba Ibuku ari yo ndangamuntu ya mbere y'Abanyarwanda irimo ubwoko bw'Abahutu , Abatwa n'Abatutsi .
Muri icyo kirangantego kirimo interuro igira iti """" Imbaga y'inyabutatu ijya mbere . """"
Gusa ntaho amateka adutekerereza ko kigeze cyemerwa ngo gikoreshwe mu miyoborere y'Abanyarwanda .
Ibirango by'u Rwanda mu bihe bya Repubulika ya Mbere n'iya Kabiri
Aho ingoma ya cyami ibererekeye Repubulika , ibirango by'igihugu na byo byarahinduwe , babyambura umuco byahanzwemo .
Repubulika yakuyeho ingoma ngabe irema ibendera ry'igitambaro cyakorewe mu ruganda gifite amabara afite ibisobanuro by'intego zashyizweho , hakiyongeraho n'igishushanyo cy'ubugeni kirimo ibimenyetso biranga icyo bimirije imbere .
Imiterere n'imihangire y'ibirango by'igihugu mu bihe bya Repubulika , bayifatiye ku birango by'Abanyaburayi bakolonizaga Afurika muri ibyo bihe , bakuraho umuco wa Kinyafurika w'ibirango bifatiye ku ngoma ngabe .
Muri ibyo birango hiyongereyeho n'Indirimbo yubahiriza Igihugu .
Ibendera ry'u Rwanda rya mbere ryamuritswe ku wa 1 Nyakanga 1962 , ubwo u Rwanda rwabonaga ubwigenge , Kayibanda Grégoire , akarubera Perezida wa Kabiri warutegetse mu 1962 - 1973 .
Amabara yari agize ibendera rya Repubulika ya Mbere , yari """" Umutuku , umuhondo n'icyatsi . """"
Indirimbo yubahiriza Igihugu yari """" Rwanda rwacu . """"
Ikirangantego cyari kigizwe n'ibimenyetso bitandukanye ariko kivuga """" Ubumwe , Amahoro n'Amajyambere . """"
Ibyo birango by'u Rwanda rwa Repubulika , ni byo rwagendeyeho mu bihe bya Repubulika ya Mbere n'iya Kabiri kugeza ku wa 31 Ukuboza 2001 .
Iki cyemezo cyafatiwe mu nama zidasanzwe zo kwigira hamwe uko igihugu kizabaho mu myaka iri imbere zabaye mu 1998 - 1999 .
Ibirango by'u Rwanda mu bihe kuzuka k'u Rwanda
Nyuma y'uko habayeho amahano rurangiza ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi igahitana abasaga miliyoni , ikaza guhagarikwa n'Ingabo za FPR - Inkotanyi zari zirangajwe imbere na Kagame Paul , Leta y'ubumwe bw'Abanyarwanda , yashinzwe ku wa 19 Nyakanga 1994 , yatangiye kwiga uburyo ibirango by'igihugu byahindurwa .
Byakozwe hagamijwe gushyiraho ibijyanye n'ibyo igihugu cyifuza kugeza ku benegihugu mu Rwanda rushya .
Ibirango bya Repubulika ya Mbere n'iya Kabiri , byari byiganjemo amacakubiri , irondakoko n'irondakarere .
Aha ntiwakwirengagiza n'ubwishongoro bwinshi Abaparimehutu babigaragajemo ubwo birukanaga benshi mu baturarwanda bakajya kuba impunzi mu mahanga , n'abasigaye mu gihugu bakaba impetamugongo n'impunzi mu gihugu cyabo .
Nuko ku wa , 31 Ukuboza 2001 , ni bwo hasohotse ibirango bishya by'u Rwanda , birimo ibendera ry'igihugu rigizwe n'amabara atatu , ari yo """" Ubururu - juru , umuhondo w'izahabu n'icyatsi kibisi . """"
Ni na bwo kandi habonetse n'indirimbo nshya yubahiriza igihugu yiswe """" Rwanda Nziza . """"
Ikirangantego cyo kiganjemo ibimenyetso bitandukanye , bifite igisobanuro cy """" """" Ubumwe , Umurimo no gukunda igihugu , """" nk'intego y'Abanyarwanda bagiye kurandura icyo bapfa , bakabagarira icyo bapfana .
Ikirangantego gishya n'ibendera ry'igihugu , biranga u Rwanda muri ibi bihe byahanzwe n'umunyabugeni Alphonse Kirimobenecyo , aho yatsinze bagenzi be basaga 400 bari bahanganye .
Indirimbo yubahiriza igihugu yo yahanzwe n'abagororwa batatu bari bafungiye muri Gereza ya Karubanda barangajwe imbere na Munyaneza Vedaste , barimo Kalisa Evariste , Shenge Laurent na Mbonyizina Jean Marie Vianney .
Umurage w'u Rwanda mu birango b'igihugu
Ukurikiye amateka y'iremwa ry'u Rwanda n'iyubakwa rya rwo , usanga ari igihugu cyubakiye ku murage utajya uhinduka kugeza magingo aya ubwo aya mateka yandikwaga .
Uwo murage tunawusanga no mu birango by'igihugu uko byagiye bihererekanwa kuva kuri Gihanga , ugakomereza kuri Ruganzu Ndoli no kuri Perezida Kagame Paul , ariko twirengagije intego mbi zikubiye mu mitekerereze mibi yadukanywe mu birango bishya bya Repubulika ya Mbere n'iya Kabiri .
Mu busesenguzi bw'Amateka buri mu gitabo """" Nkurangire u Rwanda , igihugu cya Benimana , """" umwanditsi agaragaza ko ibirango by'u Rwanda byagiye bikagirirwamo umurage udasaza ugikoreshwa mu mushinga wo kubaka u Rwanda , no mu kinyejana cya 21 .
U Rwanda rwagize ibirango bitandukanye , byinshi muri byo bikaba bikagiriyemo umurage ndagwabuvivi uzafasha bene rwo kurwubaka rugwije igitinyiro n'icyubahiro mu mahanga aruzengurutse .
Igihamya gikomeye , ni iryo huzabitekerezo ryaremye ibirango by'u Rwanda byaba iby'abami na Perezida Kagame .
Ng'ayo ng'uko !
Ng'ayo mateka y'impitabihe ku birango by'u Rwanda bimaze imyaka isaga 930 ( 1091 - 2021 ) .
Nihaganze umurage ukagiriye mu birango by'u Rwanda twarazwe n'abakurambere batuboneye iryo mu museso .
Ibyadukanye umurage - mutindi , w'abadakunda u Rwanda na bene rwo , byo bigende nk'ifuni iheze .
No muri Paradizo hashobora kumeramo imifatangwe - Ev Uwagaba avuga ku rushako rwe rutarambye .
Nubwo aba bombi bari bamaze amezi atandatu bahamije isezerano ryo kubana nk'umugabo n'umugore [ basezeranye ku wa 3 Werurwe 2018 ] , iminsi mike ni yo bamaranye kuko igihe kirekire Mucyo yakimaze mu bitaro .
Mucyo Sabine yitabye Imana ku wa 4 Ukwakira 2018 azize indwara yitwa Systemic Lupus Erythematosusituma ; inkuru yabaye incamugongo kuri Uwagaba , inshuti n'umuryango we .
Uwagaba uvuka i Rwamagana yateye intambwe ya mbere yandika igitabo cy'amapaji 170 yise """" A Hundred days in marriage """" kivuga ku bigwi n'amateka y'umugore we .
Uyu mugabo w'imyaka 31 y'amavuko kuri ubu abarizwa muri Pologne aho yagiye kwiga amasomo y'Icyiciro cya Gatatu muri Kaminuza ya Varsovie mu bijyanye n'Ubwikorezi n'Ubucuruzi Mpuzamahanga .
Mu kiganiro cyihariye na IGIHE , Uwagaba yavuze ko igitabo cye """" """" A hundred days in Marriage """" """" bishatse kuvuga """" """" Iminsi 100 ya mbere y'urushako """" , """" yacyanditse ashaka gusohoza ibyo yemeranyije n'umugore we .
Yagize ati """" """" Nashakaga kubahiriza isezerano nagiranye n'umugore wanjye Mucyo Sabine mbere y'uko yitaba Imana .
Mu gihe yari arwaye hari ibyo namusezeranyije nzakora , impamvu ya kabiri ni uko namufashe nk'umuntu w'icyitegererezo numva ko ubuzima bwe n'amateka bye bitapfa kurangira gutya gusa kubera ko yitabye Imana .
Oya Sabine ntazibagirana kuko namushyize mu gitabo .
Nifuza ko umuntu wese uzabishaka azamenye amateka ye . """" """"
Yakomeje avuga ko ikindi cyamuteye kwandika ari uko abahanga mu bijyanye n'isanamitima bavuga ko ari umuti wavura agahinda cyangwa ihungabana runaka kuko """" bifasha kuvuga ibyo utabashaga kwatura ngo uvuge kubera amaranga mutima yawe . """"
Ati """" """" Nanditse rero ngo ibindimo mbikure ku mutima bisohoke bimvemo mbisangire n'abandi . """" """"
Yasobanuye ko ibikubiye mu gitabo bitanga n'igisubizo ku bibaza ku rupfu rw'umugore we .
Yakomeje ati """" """" Dukora ubukwe byari nk'ibisanzwe nk'uko abandi bose bakundanye babigenza twari tumaze igihe kinini tumenyanye , aha nashakaga no kwerekana ukuntu abantu bajya bivuga ko urugo ahanini ari Paradizo nibyo koko ariko ntibihira bose kuko muri iyo Paradizo hari igihe hashobora kumeramo amahwa
y'ibitovu cyangwa imifatangwe ku buryo utungurwa . """" """"
Uwagaba yavuze ko igitabo cye gifite amasomo by'umwihariko mu kubaka ingo .
Ati """" """" Urugo si ugutura muri paradizo ni nayo mpamvu , nibanze ku minsi mike twabanyemo na Mucyo kuko benshi bakeka ko ari iminsi ya buki yo kwishimisha mu buzima ariko byabaye ibindi kandi tuguma ku isezerano twagiranye . """" """"
"""" """" Nyuma y'ubukwe twagiye mu kwezi kwa buki nk'abandi bose , tujya mu gihugu duturanye , tujya ku Gisenyi turatembera , turataha tugeze mu rugo umugore atangira kugaragaza ibimenyetso by'uburwayi .
Twagiye kwa muganga batubwira ko ari ibintu bitagoye baduha imiti isanzwe , bavuga ko ari umunaniro . """" """"
Nyuma y'icyumweru , Mucyo yasubiye mu kazi ariko hashize igihe gito atangira kubyimba ibirenge , ibyo bamwe bitiranyije no gusama , ariko """" uko iminsi ishira akarushaho kuremba . """"
Uwagaba yahungabanyijwe n'urupfu rw'umugore we
Ku wa 28 Nzeri 2018 , Mucyo yajyanywe mu Bitaro bya CHUK ndetse abaganga baza kumenya indwara arwaye .
Uwagaba avuga ko icyo gihe yatangiye gushaka uko yajya kumuvuriza mu bihugu bifite ibikoresho bihambaye kuko mu Rwanda byari byananiranye ariko [ Mucyo ] ajya muri koma yamazemo ibyumweru bitatu , ahita yitaba Imana .
Ati """" """" Uburwayi bwe bwari bugoye ku buryo byampungabanyije cyane .
Sabine yari umukobwa ukora siporo , ubona ko afite ameze neza ariko nyine ubuzima burahinduka . """" """"
Mu gitabo cye , Uwagaba akomeza gushimangira isezerano yagiranye n'umugore we .
Ati """" """" Urukundo nyarwo , kurinda isezerano , kwitanga , ni byo nahaye umutwe wa kabiri w'izina ry'igitabo .
Kugira urugo rwiza cyangwa urushako rwiza bisaba kwitanga , kwitonda , kugira ibyo wigomwa kugira ngo uwo mugiye kubana abe we wuzuye . """" """"
Mu gihe umugore we yari arwaye , Uwagaba yagombaga kumwitaho ariko agakomeza gushaka imibereho ngo abone ikibatunga .
Ati """" """" Umugore wanjye arwaye twarakubititse cyane kuko nagombaga no gukora ngo tubeho , na we nkamugeraho kenshi bishoboka .
Haje kugera igihe yumva yorohewe yakize , twaraganiriye arambwira ati """" ariko uzi ko ubuzima twaciyemo bugoye kandi bubabaje ? """"
Icyo gihe yacurangaga gitari , arambwira ngo """" uwazahimba indirimbo cyangwa nkakora umuvugo ariko nkagira ikintu nkora nk'inkuru ivuga iminsi twabanyemo muri aya mezi . """" """"
Icyo kiganiro ni cyo cyanogerejwemo igitekerezo cyo kwandika igitabo """" """" A hundred days in Marriage """" """" kigaruka ku minsi ya mbere yabo mu rushako .
Uwagaba ati """" """" Abari aho bamubwiye bati """" byaba birebire kereka mubishyize mu gitabo .
Sabine ati """" nimumbwire rero tuzakita dute ? """"
Avuga ko ubwo tumaze amezi atatu mu bibazo reka tuzacyite """" Mu minsi 100 twubatse urugo . """"
Ni we wihitiyemo , nibyo nise isezerano .
Ubwo twaje gusezererwa turataha nyuma aza kwitaba Imana . """" """"
Urupfu rw'umugore we rwaramuhungabanyije kugeza aho yagiye gushaka umuganga w'indwara zo mu mutwe amugira inama yo kuruhuka bitewe n'ihungabana yari afite .
Ati """" """" Uwo muganga yangiriye inama yo kwandika kuko njye rwose sinigeze ntekereza ko nzandika igitabo . """" """"
Akimara kumurika """" A Hundred days in marriage , """" Kaminuza yigamo i Varsovie muri Pologne yamugeneye igihembo cy'umunyeshuri wakoze ikintu gikomeye .
Igitabo cya Uwagaba kiri mu Cyongereza , anateganya kugishyira mu Gifaransa no mu Kinyarwanda .
Kiboneka ku maguriro ya murandasi azwi ku Isi yose nka , , Barnes , Noble , Google , iBooks , Scribd , Booktopia n'ayandi .
Reba ikiganiro na Uwagaba Joseph asobanura Igitabo cye """" A Hundred days in marriage """"
Imigogo ibiri y'abami b'u Rwanda iri gukorwaho ubushakashatsi .
Ntabwo muri iyo ngoro ariho abo bami batabarijwe ahubwo imigogo yabo ihari ngo ikorweho ubushakashatsi buzafasha abahanga kumenya byimbitse amateka y'u Rwanda .
Uruhererekane nyemvugo rugaragaza ko Cyilima II Rujugira yatanze nyuma yo
gutegeka u Rwanda kuva mu 1675 kugeza mu 1708 .
Mu migenzo ya cyami , abami bitwa ba Cyilima bagombaga gutabarizwa ( gushyingurwa ) n'abami bitwa ba Mutara .
Cyilima amaze gutanga , umugogo we wasizwe imiti ituma udashanguka , ubikwa mu rugo rwe rwari ruherereye i Kayumbu muri Kamonyi .
Umwami witwa Mutara wagombaga gutabariza Cyilima ni Rwogera wategetse u Rwanda hagati ya 1830 na 1853 .
Ntabwo byakozwe kuko Rwogera yatanze atunguranye .
Byabaye ngombwa ko bategereza undi mwami uzima ingoma yitwa Mutara , umugogo wa Cyilima ukomeza kubikwa .
Umwami wagombaga gutabariza Cyilima Rujugira ni Mutara III Rudahigwa mu 1931 , icyakora yimye mu bihe bibi u Rwanda rwari rwarinjiriwe n'abakoloni ndetse ni nabo bamwimitse bitandukanye n'imigenzo y'ubwiru .
