Igitabo """" Ibitaramo ku mateka y'u Rwanda """" cya Zephrin Kagiraneza kivuga ko abiru aribo bafashe umwanzuro wo gutabariza Cyilima Rujugira , bikorwa rwihishwa mu 1931 i Gaseke ( Rutobwe : Ubu ni mu murenge wa Kayumbu mu karere ka Kamonyi ) .
Umwami Kigeli IV Rwabugiri we yiciwe mu Bunyabungo ( muri Congo ) mu gitero yari yahagabye , umugogo we uzanwa mu Rwanda atabarizwa i Rutare mu karere ka Gicumbi , ahari imisezero y'abami .
Imigogo yabo iri gukorwaho ubushakashatsi
Igitabo cya Kagiraneza kivuga ko umugogo wa Cyilima Rujugira wataburuwe mu mwaka wa 1969 kugira ngo ukorerweho ubushakashatsi .
Muri icyo gihe ni nabwo hataburuwe uwa Nyirayuhi Kanjogera , nyina w'umwami Yuhi V Musinga .
Kanjogera yapfuye mu 1933 .
Mu musezero ( imva ) wa Cyilima , hakuwemo ibindi bikoresho byo mu gihe cye birimo nk'amacumu , amasaro , imitako , utubindi n'ibindi .
Ubushakashatsi bwakorewe kuri ibyo bikoresho byasanzwe mu mva ye , bwagaragaje ko mu gihe yari akiri umwami amasaro n'indi mitako byakorerwaga i Burayi cyangwa mu Buhinde , byageraga mu Rwanda binyuze mu nyanja y'Abahinde .
Umusizi Nsanzabera Jean de Dieu yavuze ko nta gitangaza kirimo kuba mu mva ya Cyilima Rujugira barasanzemo amasaro , kuko imyenda n'imitako nk'amasaro byaje mu Rwanda ku ngoma ya Yuhi III Mazimpaka ( 1642 - 1675 ) , ari we se wa Rujugira .
Umushakashatsi mu Kigo cy'Igihugu cy'Ingoro z'Umurage w'u Rwanda , Maurice Mugabowagahunde , yavuze ko n'umugogo wa Kigeli IV Rwabugiri uri mu ngoro y'umurage i Huye , aho uri gukorerwaho ubushakashatsi .
Kugeza ubu abemererwa kugera aho iyo migogo ibitse , ni abashakashatsi babiherewe uburenganzira gusa , abasura ingoro ndangamurage ntabwo babyemerewe .
Ati """" Keretse uri umushakashatsi naho umushyitsi ntiwawubona .
Icyo wabona ni ibindi bikoresho byari biri kumwe na we , ariko turacyari mu bushakashatsi ariko duteganya ko ubushakashatsi niburangira uzongera ugatabarizwa . """"
Mugabowagahunde yavuze ko umugogo wa Cyilima ukimara gutabururwa , wajyanywe mu Bubiligi muri laboratwari zifite ubushobozi bwo gupima ibya kera , zigaragaza ko yabayeho imyaka igera ku ijana mbere y'iyo uruhererekane nyemvugo nyarwanda ruvuga ko yatangiyeho .
Yagize ati """" Amagufa ye yagiye mu Bubiligi muri laboratwari bigaragaza ko n'igihe Mgr Alexis Kagame yagerageje gukora agaragaza igihe yapfiriye , laboratwari yo igaragaza ko ari vuba cyane .
Yabayeho mu myaka ijana mbere y'iyo Kagame yandikaga .
Ibyo bituma umenya neza igihe kurusha kugenekereza . """"
Biramutse byemejwe neza , byaba bivuze ko umwami Cyilima Rujugira yabayeho mu myaka yo hagati ya 1500 na 1600 .
Ibikoresho byasanzwe mu musezero ( imva ) wa Cyilima Rujugiro nabyo byakoreweho ubushakashatsi .
Mugabowagahunde yavuze ko utubindi twasanzwemo , twapimwe bakagaragaza ko twari turimo inzoga zikoze mu buro .
Ibyo ashimangira ko bifite igisobanuro mu myemerere y'Abanyarwanda bo hambere .
Ati """" Ibyo bigaragaraza imyemerere y'Abanyarwanda ko umwami adapfa , ko akomeza ubuzima akanywa . """"
Mu mateka kandi bivugwa ko guhera ku bwa Yuhi III Mazimpaka , abami batari bemerewe kunywa urwagwa .
Banywaga inzoga zikoze mu binyampeke .
Kuba barasanze mu tubindi twa Cyilima inzoga zikoze mu buro , Mugabowagahunde avuga ko bihuza n'ibyo amateka avuga .
Ubushakashatsi buracyakomeje , gusa Mugabowagahunde yavuze ko hakiri imbogamizi yo kubona abahanga bahagije bo gufasha muri ubwo bushakashatsi n'ibikoresho .
Ati """" Ikibazo gihari turabura inzobere mu bushakashatsi ku bisigaramatongo ( archeologists ) .
Mu Rwanda dufite bake kandi nta laboratwari ikomeye ariko turi gusinyana n'Inzu ndangamurage yo mu Bubiligi Tervuren kugira ngo ubushakashatsi bwihute . """"
Gahunda ihari ni uko imigogo y'abo bami nimara gukorerwaho ubushakashatsi , izongera gutabarizwa .
Inkomoko ya """" Amateka Series , """" gahunda igamije kwigisha umuco urubyiruko ruba mu mahanga .
Inkomoko ya """" AMATEKA SERIES , """" gahunda igamije kwigisha umuco urubyiruko ruba mu mahanga
Ubu bukangurambaga bukubiyemo ibiganiro bizajya bitumirwamo impuguke zitandukanye mu by'umuco , inararibonye zizafasha mu kwigisha urubyiruko ibijyanye n'amateka , abahanzi mu ngeri zitandukanye n'abandi .
Linda Iriza uri mu bategura """" Amateka Series """" yabwiye IGIHE ko igitekerezo cyo gutangiza uyu mushinga bakigize muri Mutarama 2020 .
Ati """" Igitekerezo cyo gutangiza """" Amateka Series """" twakigize muri Mutarama 2020 , ubwo twateguraga ibikorwa by'urubyiruko ruba mu Mujyi wa Perth muri Australie .
Gutekereza iki gikorwa byatewe n'uko benshi muri twe tutazi byinshi , ndetse hari n'abatazi na bike , ku mateka n'umuco by'u Rwanda . """"
Yakomeje avuga ko hahise haduka icyorezo COVID - 19 biba ngombwa ko abantu batongera guterana .
Icyo gihe ubwo bari muri """" guma mu rugo """" ni bwo batangiye gutegura gahunda zose zijyanye n'iki gikorwa ndetse muri Gicurasi 2020 batangira kujya baganira bifashishije ikoranabuhanga .
Muri Kanama 2020 , amabwiriza ajyanye no kuguma mu rugo yarorohejwe ndetse hategurwa Umuganura wahujwe na """" Amateka Series . """"
Icyo gihe hatumiwemo abantu bakuru batanze ibiganiro ku bijyanye n'umuganura ndetse bababwira amateka yawo byimbitse .
Iriza avuga ko benshi mu rubyiruko baba muri Perth nibura bageze muri Australie bafite imyaka itatu ndetse abandi bakaba ari naho bavukiye bituma batagira amahirwe yo kumenya byinshi ku gihugu cyabo cy'inkomoko .
Ku bw'iyo mpamvu bashaka kwiga byinshi ku muco Nyarwanda ndetse n'amateka y'igihugu .
Yavuze ko ari ikintu cyakiriwe neza cyane , ati """" Twashimishijwe n'ibitekerezo byiza twakiriye ndetse n'ubufasha turimo kubona . """"
Iriza yakomeje ashimira Ambasade y'u Rwanda muri Singapore , Minisiteri y'Ububanyi n'Amahanga n'Ubutwererane na Minisiteri y'Urubyiruko n'Umuco y'u Rwanda bababaye hafi kandi bakabashyigikira .
Avuga ko bafite intumbero y'uko iki gikorwa kizakomeza ndetse abagitegura bagashishikariza urubyiruko gukora ubushakashatsi , bakandika , bagasangiza abandi ibyo bagezeho kandi bakarushaho kwiga byinshi ku muco wabo .
Iriza yasoje asaba urubyiruko rw'abanyarwanda aho bari hose ku Isi kuzitabira igikorwa giteganyijwe ku italiki ya 06 Gashyantare aho bazaganirizwa ku nkomoko y'u Rwanda ndetse bakanataramirwa n'umuhanzi Jules Sentore .
Ibi biganiro bizanyura ako kanya ku mbuga nkoranyambaga zose za Amateka Series ( Twitter , Facebook , Instagram na YouTube ) .
Umwaka ushize ibiganiro byakozwe byari byatumiwemo abantu batandukanye barimo Turahirwa Moses washinze inzu y'imideli Moshions ; Hope Azeda watangije Mashirika Performing Arts and Media Company ; Ambasaderi Uwihanganye Jean de Dieu uhagarariye u Rwanda muri Singapore n'abandi .
Ushaka gukomeza kumenya amakuru atandukanye ku bikorwa bitegurwa binyuze mu """" Amateka Series """" wabasura kuri uru rubuga .
Guma mu rugo , umwanya mwiza ku banditsi b'ibitabo nyarwanda .
Ibitabo bifasha abantu b'ingeri zitandukanye kwiyungura ubumenyi bubafasha gutera imbere haba mu kwihangira imirimo , kwimakaza indangagaciro na kirazira mu iterambere , ubumenyi bw'Isi n'ibindi .
Mu gihe umujyi wa Kigali uri muri gahunda ya Guma mu rugo , ni umwanya mwiza ku banditsi b'u Rwanda , kujya mu nganzo bagahanga , bakandika ibifasha igihugu nabo ubwabo kwiteza imbere .
Nta mwanditsi ukwiriye kuvuga ko yabuze icyo akora muri Guma mu rugo .
Umwanya munini w'abanditsi bawushyire mu gukora ubushakashatsi bandikire u Rwanda , bandikire Afurika bandikire Isi .
Muri Guma mu rugo yabaye umwaka ushize , hari abanditsi bayibyaje umusaruro , irangira ibitabo babigeze kure , ku buryo amezi yakurikiyeho yari ayo kubimurika , abo ni abo gushimirwa .
Ntabwo kwandika bikwiriye kuba ibya bamwe , kuko buri wese afite inkuru yo kwandika .
Ni byiza ko Abanyarwanda bose barushaho kwimakaza umuco wo kwandika no gusoma ibitabo kuko ari umuco mwiza wongera ubumenyi n'ubuhanga .
U Rwanda rudutegerejeho ubuhanga n'ubumenyi bwo kurwubaka kandi nta handi bituruka uretse mu gusoma ibitabo .
Ni umukoro kuri buri wese , mu rwego aherereyemo yakwandika kandi bikaba umusanzu ukomeye ku bariho bashaka kumenya ibyo mu rwego akoramo n'abazaza nyuma .
Wakubaka u Rwanda ute utandika cyangwa udasoma ibitabo ? Wakubaka Afurika ute utandika cyangwa udasoma ibitabo ?
Wakwandika ute ibitabo utabisoma ?
Gusoma ibitabo niwo musingi w'ibikorwa byubaka u Rwanda ndetse n'Afurika .
Mucyo duce imigozi twaziritswe na Bagashakabuhake , ngo """" Umunyafurika umuhisha mu bitabo ?
Tubyamagane .
Twimakaze umuco wo kwandika no gusoma ibitabo nkuko Nyakubahwa Perezida wa Repubulika adahwema kubidusaba kuko nibyo bizadufasha kubaka u Rwanda ndetse n'Afurika twifuza .
Ubuzima butoroshye bwa Kurawige wiciwe se mu maso muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Kuva icyo gihe yatangiye ubuzima bwo gushaka aho yerekeza , ku bw'amahirwe ahungana n'umuryango wo kwa nyirakuru ariko ntiyawutekaniyemo kuko yahahuriye n'ibibazo birimo no gufatwa ku ngufu .
Mu kubika ayo mateka no kuba umuhamya wayo , Kurawige yanditse igitabo yise """" From Bondage to Freedom """" bishatse kuvuga ugenekereje mu Kinyarwanda """" Gufatwa bunyago ukaza kwibohora """" cyashibutse ku nzira y'inzitane yanyuzemo muri Jenoside .
Mu kiganiro yagiranye na IGIHE , Kurawige yavuze ko igitabo cye yacyanditse ashaka gutanga ubuhamya bw'ibyamubayeho muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi ubwo yicirwaga se umubyara bikozwe n'Interahamwe .
Yagize ati """" Ni igitabo nanditse kugira ngo abahakana Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi , nkanjye wiciwe Data mu maso , mbibere umuhamya hatazagira ubeshya abatabizi kandi turiho .
Ni igitabo nanditse mpawe imbaraga n'ubuhamya numvise muri filime mbarankuru """" La Traverse du Génocide """" bituma nanjye numva nzasubira aho nababariye nkahakora filime mbarankuru . """"
Yavuze ko iki gitabo nacyo mu minsi iri imbere ateganya gusinya amasezerano y'uko cyakorwamo filime mbarankuru muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika .
Yakomeje agira ati """" Mu byo niyemeje rero ni ukuvuga amateka nabayemo n'abo tuyahuje kugira ngo abagenda babeshya kubera inyungu ntazi bafatwe bahanwe . """"
Umutoni avuga ko ku myaka itanu ubwo Interahamwe zicaga se Dr Kurawige Jean Baptiste , yabanje kumuhisha munsi y'intebe .
Uyu mukobwa wari ukiri umwana yarungurutse munsi abona uko bamutema , abona amaraso atemba , ariko mu bitekerezo yari afite ku myaka ye yumvaga ko umubyeyi we ari bugaruke akamukura aho yamubwiye kwihisha , ariko siko byagenze .
Umutoni avuga ko yaje kuhavanwa na nyirakuru ubyara nyina babasha guhunga bagera muri Uganda mu nkambi , bahava berekeza muri Burkina Faso , tariki ya 3 Ugushyingo 1994 .
Avuga ko bavuye muri Burkina Faso agana muri Afurika yepfo , mu mwaka wa 2011 , avuyeyo yasubiye mu Rwanda bwa mbere mu 2012 , ariko izi nzira zose ntabwo byari byoroshye , kuko guhera igihe se yicwaga kugeza 2011 yari mu bibazo bikomeye .
Umutoni avuga ko byamubabaje cyane kuko abishe se ari abo mu muryango wo kwa nyina ndetse no mu guhunga ajyana na nyirakuru ubyara nyina yakomeje kubabamo batamukunda , uretse gusa nyirakuru wahoraga amubwira ati """" Mwana wanjye ujye uhora wimenya ntibagukunda """" """"
Bageze muri Burkina Faso , nyina wabo wari warashatse muri icyo gihugu yamushumuriye umugabo we akajya amufata ku ngufu ku myaka 16 .
Ati """" Bari barabuze urubyaro bashaka ko umugabo we yambyaraho umwana , ku buryo yamfataga ku ngufu byibura gatanu mu cyumweru .
Uyu mugabo yari akomeye cyane muri kiriya gihugu kuko yari inshuti ya Perezida waho icyo gihe , ku buryo na Perezida basuranaga mu ngo , ibi bikamuha imbaraga zo gukora icyo ashaka muri iki gihugu . """"
Yakomeje avuga ko """" Byaje no kumenyekana ko mfatwa ku ngufu mu Banyarwanda batuye muri icyo gihugu ariko bagira uwo babibwira mu butegetsi bwaho bigafata ubusa . """"
Umutoni avuga kandi ko muri icyo gihugu yahagiriye amakuba y'uko umugabo witwa Athanase wishe se , yahageze babana atamuzi .
Yagize ati """" Turabana ntamuzi , nzi ko ari umuntu nyine wo mu muryango nkumva mukunze , akamperekeza ku ishuri tukaganira nk'umwana nashakaga kumenya byinshi .
Nyuma Interpol yaje kumushaka nibwo namenye ko ariwe wishe Papa , nakwibuka ukuntu nari naramugize umuntu numva nkunze ngashengukira mu mutima . """"
Igihe cyarageze nyirakuru yitaba Imana , atangira gushakisha uko yahunga ariko biramugora kuko yari yakumiriwe .
Yakomeje ati """" Nasigaye nsa nk'aho ntaho ndi , nshakisha uko nahunga birangora cyane .
Bari barashyize amatangazo ku kibuga cy'indege ku mipaka y'ibihugu byose bikikije Burkina Faso ko ntashobora gusohoka mu gihugu .
Nabiganirije umwe mu basirikare bakuru baho , ambwira ko bagiye kumfasha ariko azangira inama y'uko nzabigenza bigakunda . """" """"
Yamusabye guhindura amazina , ashaka ibindi byangombwa ndetse amufasha guhungira muri Afurika y'Epfo , aho yatangiriye ubuzima bushya .
Kurawige yize muri Kaminuza ya Pretoria mu bijyanye na Géologie , ahasoje amasomo mu 2016 , yasabye kwimenyerereza umwuga mu Rwanda aho yagarutse afite imyaka 23 .
Avuga ko yahuye n'umwe mu bafunzwe uri mu bohereje abishe umubyeyi we ariko ngo amugeze imbere aramusuzugura cyane yanga kwemera ibyo yakoze .
Akomeza ati """" Na n'ubu ntiyemera ibyo yakoze , ariko njye mu masengesho yanjye nahisemo kubabarira kugira ngo nduhuke uwo mutwaro . """" """"
Kurawige kuri ubu utuye muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , mu Mujyi wa Dallas , yavukiye i Ngoma mu Karere ka Huye mu Ntara y'Amajyepfo mu 1988 .
Ni umwe mu bayobozi b'ikigo gikomeye gikora ibijyanye n'ubucukuzi bw'amabuye y'agaciro .
Reba ikiganiro IGIHE yagiranye na Umutoni
Menya Amanda Gorman , umusizi ukiri muto waciye agahigo mu irahira rya Perezida .
Uyu mukobwa yanditse amateka ku mugoroba wo kuri uyu wa Kabiri tariki 20 Mutarama 2021 , ubwo yavugaga umuvugo mu muhango wo kurahira kwa Perezida mushya wa Leta Zunze Ubumwe z'Amerika , Joe Biden na Visi Perezida Kamala Harris .
Uyu mukobwa yavuze umuvugo yise """" The Hill We Climb """" cyangwa """" Umusozi tuzamuka """" """" mu rurimi rw'Ikinyarwanda .
Ni umuvugo yari amaze ibyumweru bibiri ari gukoraho , ugaruka ku bumwe n'ubwiyunge ku banyamerika .
Avuga ko guhimba uyu muvugo ari kimwe mu bintu by'ingirakamaro yakoze mu buzima bwe , ati """" Nari mfite ibintu byinshi , ariko mu by'ukuri ni kimwe mu bintu by'ingenzi nakoze mu buzima bwanjye bujyanye no kuvuga imivugo .
Naravugaga nti ningerageza kuzamuka uyu musozi rimwe , nzagera kure . """"
Imwe mu mirongo igize uyu muvugo yayanditse ku wa 6 Mutarama 2021 , ubwo ibihumbi by'abaturage bashyigikiye Donald Trump binjiraga mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko ya Amerika ubwo abayigize bari bateranye ngo bemeze intsinzi ya Joe Biden , bakarwana inkundura na Polisi bigateza impagarara muri Amerika .
Uyu mukobwa w'umwiraburakazi ufite inkomoko ku bacakara yarezwe na nyina gusa .
Afite inzozi zo kuzaba Perezida umunsi umwe .
Yatangiye kugaragaza impano yo kuvuga imivugo akiri muto ndetse atangira kuzamura impano ye vuba cyane .
Yakuriye mu Mujyi wa Los Angeles aho nyina yari umwarimu .
Ku myaka 16 yahize abandi mu mivugo mu marushanwa y'abakiri bato muri Los Angeles .
Imyaka mike yakurikiyeho ubwo yigaga ibijyanye na """" Sociologie """" muri Harvard yahize abasizi ku rwego rw'igihugu bakiri bato .
Nyuma yo kwigaragaza mu irahira rya Joe Biden , yashimwe na benshi barimo Barack Obama ndetse n'umugore we , Michelle Obama yagaragaje uburyo yakozwe ku mutima n'umuvugo wa Amanda Gorman .
Ati """" Hamwe n'amagambo ye akomeye kandi akora ku mutima , Amanda Gorman atwibukije imbaraga dufite mu gusigasira demokarasi .
Komeza urabagirane Amanda mfite amatsiko y'ibyo uzakora mu bihe biri imbere . """"
Abandi bantu bakomeye barimo Oprah Winfrey bose bagaragaje ko batewe ishema n'uyu mukobwa w'umwiraburakazi wanditse amateka akomeye .
Abari bari mu itsinda ryateguraga irahira rya Joe Biden bahamagaye uyu mukobwa mu mpera z'ukwezi gushize .
Yavuze ko atari yahawe amabwiriza y'ibijyanye n'umuvugo we .
Yahamagawe biturutse ku mugore wa Joe Biden , Jill Biden wabonye inyandiko ze mu isomero .
Yagize ati """" Nta mabwiriza bari bambwiye ajyanye n'ibyo ngomba kwandika .
Insanganyamatsiko y'irahira yari """" ubumwe bwa Amerika """" rero ubwo numvaga ko ariyo nsanganyamatsiko yabo byaranyoroheye kuko nanjye ni cyo kintu nashakaga kwandikaho mu muvugo wanjye , ku bumwe bwa Amerika . """"
Uyu mukobwa yabonye izuba mu 1998 avukira mu Mujyi wa Los Angeles , yakuranye n'impanga ye yitwa Gabriella na nyina w'umwarimukazi .
Mu 2015 yashyize hanze igitabo cye cya mbere cy'imivugo """" The One for Whom Food is Not enough """" gikubiyemo insanganyamatsiko zitandukanye zirimo izivuga ku burenganzira bw'abagore , ubwoko n'inkomoko n'abanyafurika baba muri Amerika .
Mu bantu afatiraho icyitegererezo harimo Winston Churchill wigeze kuba Minisitiri w'Intebe w'u Bwongereza , Martin Luther King Junior na Malala Yousafzai umukobwa w'umunya - Pakistan watsindiye igihembo cy'amahoro mu 2013 .
Amanda afite inzozi zo kuziyamamariza kuzaba Perezida wa Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika mu 2036 ubwo uzaba afite imyaka 38 .
Uretse kuvuga imivugo , ni n'impirimbanyi y'uburenganzira bwa muntu .
Silas Majoro , Umunyarwanda wa mbere wize Kaminuza """" Ababiligi bagahinda umushyitsi """"
Yigishije Milton Obote wabaye Perezida wa Uganda
Yashyizwe n'Umwami Mutara mu nama nkuru y'igihugu
Yapfuye urupfu rw'amarabira
Nta gasozi kabura intwari !
Muri ibyo bihe bikomeye aho kwiga amashuri abanza byasaga nk'inzozi ku Banyarwanda , mu 1917 i Gahini muri Kayonza havutse umuhungu akitwa Majoro Silas arenga izo nzitizi zose aba Umunyarwanda wa mbere wize Kaminuza yirwanyeho .
Mu myaka Majoro yavutsemo , mu Rwanda amashuri abanza yari mbarwa n'ahari amenshi yari mu maboko y'abihayimana ba Kiliziya Gatolika .
Majoro yavukiye mu muryango w'Abangilikani , byumvikana ko kwiga mu mashuri ya Kiliziya byasaga nk'ibidashoboka .
Ababyeyi bamurwanyeho , ashakisha ishuri , birangira abonye iryo muri Uganda rizwi nka King's College Budo .
Yahize amashuri abanza n'ayisumbuye araharangiza .
Umwarimu muri Kaminuza y'u Rwanda Ishami ry'Uburezi , Dr Evariste Karangwa , ni umwe mu bize kuri King's College Budo , ashishikazwa no kumenya amateka y'Umunyarwanda wa mbere wahize , ari we Majoro .
Dr Karangwa yabwiye IGIHE ko muri iryo shuri Majoro yari umuhanga cyane , by'umwihariko mu ishami ry'Imibare .
Majoro yiganye muri iryo shuri na Kabaka II Edward Mutesa waje kuba Umwami wa Buganda .
Yagize ati """" Icyo nabonye muri archives z'iryo shuri ryatangiye mu 1906 , bafite archives za kera , icyo bamuziho yari umuhanga cyane cyane mu mibare . """"
Mu myaka ya 1940 Majoro yari arangije amashuri yisumbuye abanza gukora muri Uganda .
Icyo gihe mu Rwanda nta Kaminuza n'imwe yari ihari , yewe nta n'umunyarwanda wari wakayize abenshi barangizaga mu mashuri yisumbuye nabo ari mbarwa .
Majoro yabanje kwigisha muri Uganda mu ishuri ryitwa Mwili College .
Muri iryo shuri yigishijemo abarimo Milton Obote waje kuba Perezida wa mbere wa Uganda .
Majoro amaze kwigisha muri iryo shuri , yaje gukomereza amasomo ye muri Kaminuza ya Makerere , yiga ibijyanye n'uburezi .
Yarangije mu 1949 .
Igitabo """" Ibitaramo ku mateka y'u Rwanda """" cya Zephrin Kagiraneza kivuga ko icyo gihe Majoro ari we wari Umunyarwanda wa mbere wize Kaminuza , akaba uwa kabiri mu Rwanda no mu Burundi .
Kigira kiti """" Muri Ruanda - Urundi , uwabonye impamyabushobozi ya kaminuza bwa mbere ni umuganwa w'Umurundi witwa Birori Joseph mwene Baranyanka .
Mu 1949 mu Rwanda habonetse Umunyarwanda Silas Majoro .
Yatsindiye impamyabushobozi y'uburezi muri Kaminuza ya Makerere muri Uganda . """"
Majoro arangije muri Kaminuza ya Makerere , yafashe icyemezo cyo gutaha mu Rwanda gufasha mu iterambere ry'uburezi .
Yanzwe n'Ababiligi , aba inshuti y'Umwami Rudahigwa
Dr Karangwa avuga ko yageze mu Rwanda abakoloni b'Ababiligi bakamwanga cyane kuko yagaragazaga amatwara y'impinduramatwara ngo uburezi bugere kuri bose .
Mu bindi bamwangiraga , ngo ni uko yari uwo muri Angilikani kandi amashuri menshi ari aya Kiliziya , hakiyongeraho ko yari yarize mu Cyongereza mu gihe amashuri yo mu Rwanda yakoreshaga Igifaransa .
Ati """" Nyuma yo gusoza amashuri , yasuzuguwe cyane n'ubuyobozi bw'abakoloni kubera idini rye n'amashuri yizemo .
Yagiye kwigisha mu ishuri ry'iwabo i Gahini .
Umwami Mutara III Rudahigwa yabibonye kare , amushyira mu nama nkuru y'Igihugu , Conseil Supérieur du Pays ariko akomeza kwangwa bikomeye n'abakoloni . """"
Bivugwa ko Majoro yari agiye kugirwa Umuyobozi Mukuru w'amashuri yose yo mu Rwanda ariko ubuyobozi bw'abakoloni na Kiliziya Gatolika bakabyitambika kuko yari umuporotestanti .
Dr Karangwa ati """" Bashakaga kumugira Umuyobozi Mukuru w'amashuri y'u Rwanda .
Ntabwo bamushyizeho ahubwo bashyizeho Kayibanda Grégoire .
Baramwangiye ngo nta Gifaransa azi ariko ubwo harimo n'ibindi by'uko ari umuporotesitanti n'ibindi . """"
Umwami Mutara III Rudahigwa amaze kumutera imboni , yabaye inshuti ye y'akadasohoka .
Dr Karangwa avuga ko Majoro ari we watangiye guhuza umwami Mutara na Kabaka Mutesa II wa Uganda kuko Majoro na Mutesa bari inshuti cyane .
Ati """" Yabaye umuyobozi w'ishuri ribanza rya Gahini ariyobora neza , akora ibishya byinshi , abakobwa batangira kwiga , Ababiligi baramwikanga ariko Rudahigwa aramukunda kubera amatwara yo gushaka abantu bazana amajyambere mu gihugu , amushyira mu nama nkuru y'Igihugu . """"
Inama Nkuru y'Igihugu muri ibyo bihe yakoraga nk'Inteko Ishinga Amategeko , cyangwa se abajyanama b'umwami .
Umusaruro ukomeye w'ubwo buhuza bwa Majoro hagati ya Rudahigwa na Mutesa , ni uruzinduko rw'amateka umwami Mutara III Rudahigwa yagiriye mu bwami bwa Buganda guhera tariki 14 Ukwakira kugeza kuwa 2 Ugushyingo 1956 .
Muri urwo ruzinduko , umwanya munini Rudahigwa yawumaze asura amashuri yo muri Buganda harimo na King's Budo College Majoro yizeho , rikaba ishuri ryamushimishije cyane .
Musenyeri Alexis Birindabagabo wahoze ayobora Diyozezi Angilikani ya Gahini , yabwiye IGIHE ko Majoro yashakaga ko u Rwanda rwihuta mu iterambere vuba .
Ati """" Yaravugaga ati Ababiligi ibyo badukorera ntitujya mbere .
Ubundi inshuti za mbere za Rudahigwa yari Majoro na Church w'Umwongereza .
Ubwo Majoro yashakaga kumuhuza n'Abongereza nibwo bavuze bati umuntu araducitse , mumwohereze ahandi . """"
Birindabagabo avuga ko Majoro yari umuntu ugendera ku mahame .
Bigaragarira mu banyeshuri yigishije i Gahini , kuko ngo hari interuro yari yaranditse ku gikuta igira iti """" Le Patriotisme c'est l'amour de la patrie """" ( Gukunda Igihugu ni ugukunda aho ukomoka ) .
Bivugwa ko iyo yabaga agiye mu nama nkuru y'Igihugu i Nyanza , yagendaga mu modoka ye bwite , yitwaye .
Mu myaka ya 1950 , amajwi yatangiye kuba menshi mu Rwanda , basaba ko Abanyarwanda bahabwa amahirwe bakajya kwiga Kaminuza mu mahanga cyangwa se hakubakwa Kaminuza mu gihugu .
Ababiligi babanje kwica amatwi ariko bikomeza kuvugwa cyane ndetse binandikwa mu binyamakuru byari biriho icyo gihe .
Igitabo """" Ibitaramo by'amateka y'u Rwanda """" kivuga ko Leta Mbiligi yageze aho ikavuga ko ntawe izarihirira .
Kinyamateka yo muri Gicurasi 1956 , ivuga ko u Bubiligi bwatangaje itegeko ribuza abategetsi bo muri Ruanda - Urundi gukora mu isanduku y'igihugu bashaka gufasha ushaka kujya kwiga mu mahanga .
Byaje kumenyekana mu nama nkuru y'Igihugu ari nabwo Rudahigwa yatangizaha ikigega cyamwitiriwe """" Fond Mutara , """" kugira ngo abana b'Abanyarwanda bajye kwiga mu mahanga .
Majoro yapfuye amarabira
Mu ba mbere barihiwe n'icyo Kigega harimo na Majoro washakaga kujya kwihugura i Burayi mu bijyanye n'Ubutegetsi n'Igifaransa dore ko mu byo Ababiligi bamwangiraga ari uko yize mu Cyongereza .
Ubwo yari amazeyo igihe gito , Majoro yafashwe n'uburwayi butunguranye aza kugwa mu maboko y'umuganga wamuvuraga i Bruxelles mu Bubiligi tariki 31 Werurwe 1958 .
Dr Karangwa avuga ko urupfu rwe rwajemo amayobera nk'urw'Umwami Mutara III Rudahigwa kuko nta ndwara ikomeye izwi yari arwaye .
Bikekwa ko na we yaba yarishwe ku kagambane k'Ababiligi batifuzaga umuntu ujijutse ugaragaza amafuti bakora cyangwa se uharanira ubwigenge n'iterambere nyabyo .
Musenyeri Birindabagabo na Dr Karangwa bahuriza ku kuba Majoro yari umuntu ukunda igihugu , wari unyotewe no guteza imbere uburezi .
Dr Karangwa ati """" Yakundaga igihugu cy'u Rwanda mu gihe gito yabayeho . """"
Ishuri ribanza rya Gahini Majoro yigishijemo riracyariho ariko inyubako zaryo zaravuguruwe .
Ahari hubatse ishuri ry'umwimerere yigishirijemo , ubu hubatse Katederali ya Diyosezi ya Gahini mu Itorero Angilikani .
Nyuma ya Majoro , abandi Banyarwanda babashije kujya muri Kaminuza mu bihe bya mbere harimo Déogratias Mbandiwimfura wagiye kuminuza mu mategeko ya Kiliziya i Roma guhera mu 1947 kugeza mu 1951 na Musenyeri Alexis Kagame wagiye kwiga mu 1952 yiga Filozofiya .
"""" Nanditse ngo ntsinde abifuje ko dushira ntihazagire ubara inkuru ye """" Ndizeye Omar .
Iki gitabo ugenekereje mu Kinyarwanda cyitwa """" Ubuzima n'urupfu i Nyamata """" cyashyizwe hanze umwaka ushize .
Ndizeye utuye muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , mu kiganiro cyihariye yagiranye na IGIHE , yagarutse ku mpamvu zatumye yandika ayo mateka nk'umwe mu bagize amahirwe bakarokoka Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi muri 1994 .
Ati """" Navuga ko igitabo kigaruka ku mateka ya Nyamata aho mvuka nakuriye , nkaharokokera .
Kiravuga ku buzima no ku rupfu muri Jenoside .
Nyamata kandi nyigarukaho nk'ahantu hari ibimenyetso by'amateka ya Jenoside ariko ahera mu 1959 , nkanagaruka uko nibuka ibyabereye aho nise mu Rusengero rwuje umwijima mu Rwanda . """"
Ndizeye avuka ahahoze ari Komine Kanzenze , ubu ni mu Murenge wa Ntarama mu Kagali ka Kanzenze .
Muri uyu murenge niho hari urusengero rwiciwemo ibihumbi by'Abatutsi , bakicanwa ubugome bukabije .
Mu gitabo cye , agaruka ku buryo Abatutsi batujwe mu Bugesera mu 1959 bakahajyanwa batabihisemo ahubwo ari amayeri y'ubutegetsi bwari buriho mu mugambi wabwo wo gutegura Jenoside .
Ati """" Mu 1959 nibwo ubutegetsi bw'Ababiligi bwahimuriye Abatutsi babakuye mu gice cy'Amajyaruguru za Gakenke na za Rulindo ndetse na za Burera by'umwihariko .
Hari n'abandi Batutsi bakuwe mu gice cy'epfo muri za Butare na Gikongoro .
Kujyanwa mu Bugesera rero ntabwo bari babisabye kuko bajyanwaga basize ibintu byabo , amatungo , inzu n'isambu , ni muri ibyo bihe rero n'abandi Batutsi benshi birukanywe mu gihugu bagana ibihugu bidukikije . """"
Iki gitabo Ndizeye agaragazamo ibyo yibaza ku buzima ababyeyi be babayemo mu nkambi zo mu Bugesera hagati ya 1959 na 1962 n'uburyo bakomeje gutoterezwa muri izo nkambi , bamwe bakicwa .
Ati """" Hari byinshi bitatumye ngoheka , aha navuga nk'amateka y'umubyeyi wa mwarimu wanjye Uwamaliya Enatha wanyigishije mu wa mbere w'amashuri abanza , waje kubura se wishwe mu 1963 mu Batutsi bishwe barasiwe aho bitaga kuri Nyabarongo ku kiraro cya Kanzenze , se wa Uwamaliya rero akaba yari Data wacu . """"
"""" Bahuye kandi n'ibindi bibazo mu Nkambi ya Nyamata kuko barwariyemo indwara nka za Tifoyide kubera isuku nke , hapfamo benshi cyane ibyo nzabigarukaho mu kindi gitabo ndimo kwandika . """"
Uretse ubwo buzima bwo mu Bugesera mu nkambi , Ndizeye agaruka ku byo yiboneye n'amaso ye birimo iyicwa ry'Abatutsi hagati ya 1990 na 1993 , mitingi z'amashyaka by'umwihariko MRND na CDR yateguye akanashyira mu bikorwa Jenoside .
Mu kindi gice , avuga by'umwihariko kuri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi , aho avuga uburyo umuryango we wishwe .
Ati """" Igice cya Jenoside nyir'izina gitangira mu 1994 , uko twahizwe , tukaza guhungira i Ntarama , nkabona uko bishe Data , muri ako kanya simbitekerezeho cyane kuko muri Jenoside , buri munota wabaga ari ubuzima , iyo wabonaga uwishwe wumvaga ko mu kanya ari wowe ukarwana no kureba ko wahanyanyaza ngo wihishe , akababaro
kaza nyuma wongeye kubitekereza no kubiha umwanya . """"
Ndizeye yavuze ko gutanga ubuhamya bw'ibyo abarokotse babayemo muri Jenoside , bifasha benshi kugabanya umutwaro w'ibyo baba bafite batavuze byibera mu mutima no mu bitekerezo byabo .
Ati """" Twari nk'inyamanswa ziba mu ishyamba zitegereje guhigwa no kwicwa isaha iyo ariyo yose buri munsi ku manywa , kuko mu ijoro nibwo twagiraga icyo nakwita agahenge . """"
Tariki 13 Gicurasi 1994 nibwo Inkotanyi zabarokoye .
Ati """" Byari ibyishimo bivanze n'umunaniro , agahinda n'inzara .
Tujya i Nyamata Inkotanyi zitangira kutwondora , baduha icyo gufungura , amazi yo koga n'ibindi , turongera tuba abantu . """"
Ndizeye yavuze ko icyakomeje gutuma abaho ari icyizere cy'ejo heza , kuko """" bitagenze bityo byaba ari Jenoside igikomeza kuko umugambi w'abayitegura bakayikora ni ukurimbura . """"
Yavuze ko kwandika ari uburyo bwo guhashya ingengabitekerezo ya Jenoside no guha agaciro abe bishwe .
Ati """" Kwandika rero kuri njye ni uburyo bw'isanamitima , kandi kugira ngo ntsinde ingengabitekerezo yo kumaraho abanjye , kuko bifuzaga ko amazina yabo asigara mu bitabo by'amateka kuko nta n'umwe wari kuzarokoka ngo avuge inkuru ye . """"
Yashishikarije abandi barokotse Jenoside kwandika amateka babayemo kugira ngo atazasibangana .
CHENO yashyizeho amarushanwa y'indirimbo n'imivugo bisingiza Intwari z'Igihugu .
CHENO mu itangazo yashyize hanze ku wa 11 Mutarama , yakanguriye Abanyarwanda babizi kandi babifitiye ubushobozi gukora imivugo n'indirimbo bisingiza Intwari z'igihugu , bikanakangurira abiganjemo urubyiruko kwimakaza umuco w'ubutwari .
Imyaka icumi y'igihirahiro kuri Sudani y'Epfo , Perezida Kiir """" arananiwe . """"
Icyizere cyari cyose kuri Aquil De Chut Deng n'abandi bagore bagenzi be babyinaga intsinzi mu mihanda ya Juba , bishimira ko noneho bagiye kubyara bagaheka , bagatunga bagatunganirwa .
Ntibyateye kabiri , icyizere cyaraje amasinde inzozi batifuzaga kurota ziba impamo .
Intambara zatangiye mu 2013 kugeza n'ubu zanze kurangira kugeza ubwo na Perezida Salva Kiir avuga ko ananiwe .
Mu 2013 , Perezida Salva Kiir wari umaze imyaka ibiri ayoboye icyo gihugu gishya ku ikarita y'Isi , yashwanye na Riek Machar wari Visi Perezida , Kiir ashinja mugenzi we gushaka kumuhirika ku butegetsi .
Salva Kiir aturuka mu bwoko bw'aba - Dinka naho Machar agaturuka mu bwoko bw'aba - Nuer .
Imirwano yahereye mu barinda Perezida , abo mu moko yombi batangira gushwana kugeza ubwo bigeze no mu baturage , imirwano ifata indi ntera .
Kuri uyu wa Gatanu tariki 9 Nyakanga 2021 , abanya - Sudani y'Epfo basaga ibihumbi 400 bamaze kugwa muri iyo ntambara mu gihe abasaga miliyoni 4 . 5 bavuye mu byabo .
Ni igihugu gikennye ariko gikungahaye kuri peteroli ari na yo ivamo 90 % by'amafaranga igihugu cyinjiza , nubwo Perezida Kiir aherutse kubwira Citizen TV yo muri Kenya ko Peteroli bafite """" yababereye umuvumo """" aho kuba isoko y'ubukire .
Kubera ko ariko gace kari gakungahaye kuri peteroli n'andi mabuye y'agaciro , Sudani y'Epfo yabonye ubwigenge ifite bimwe mu bikorwa remezo byiza , nyamara Croix Rouge ivuga ko nibura mu bitaro n'amavuriro Sudani y'Epfo yari ifite mbere y'ubwigenge , ibisigaye bikora ari 40 % .
Ishami ry'Umuryango w'Abibumbye ryita ku bana ( UNICEF ) rivuga ko nibura miliyoni 4 . 5 z'abana muri Sudani y'Epfo bakeneye ubufasha ngo bave mu mirire mibi .
Umubare w'abaturage bakeneye inkunga muri Sudani y'Epfo ugeze kuri miliyoni 8 . 5 muri miliyoni zisaga 10 zituye icyo gihugu .
Kubera imvururu , imyaka icumi ishize igihugu nta bushobozi kiragira bwo gutegura amatora , ataha akaba ateganyijwe mu 2023 ariko icyizere cy'uko azaba ni gike hashingiwe ku bibazo by'intambara , inzara n'imvururu za politiki zicyugarije igihugu .
Igitutu cy'amahanga , cyatumye abayobozi bombi bemera gusangira ubutegetsi , mu 2018 Machar yongera kugaruka mu gihugu nka Visi Perezida wa mbere , mu ba Visi Perezida batanu igihugu gifite .
Muri Gashyantare 2020 Kiir yashyizeho Guverinoma y'Ubumwe ariko ntabwo yabujije ko ubwicanyi bushingiye ku moko hirya no hino mu gihugu bukomeza .
Isabukuru y'imyaka icumi yakabaye ibirori bidasazwe ku gihugu cyabonye ubwigenge kimaze imyaka 30 kibuharanira , nyamara Perezida Salva Kiir yategetse ko nta birori bidasanzwe biba kuko ntacyo kwishimira gihari .
Aherutse kugira ati """" Ibihano Sudani y'Epfo yafatiwe byaradukenesheje nubwo mu bisanzwe dukize .
Ibihano byose baduhaye , ntabwo byatumye tuzamuka mu buryo twifuzagamo .
Niyo mpamvu tudashobora kwizihiza imyaka 10 ishize nk'uko abantu babyifuzaga .
Abantu barashonje , ubushobozi dufite ntabwo twabushyira mu birori , byarakaza abaturage bacu . """"
Ubwo Sudani yemezaga ko ibonye ubwigenge , Akanama k'umutekano ka Loni katoye kemeza ko ingabo za Loni zishinzwe kubungabunga amahoro zigomba kujya mu gihugu gishya gusubiza ibintu ku murongo .
Izo ngabo zigerageza gushyira ibintu mu buryo ariko ntabwo bibuza imvururu gukomeza .
Umuyobozi w'ingabo za Loni muri icyo gihugu , Nicholas Haysom kuri uyu munsi Sudani y'Epfo imaze imyaka icumi yigenga yagize ati """" Turasaba abanyapolitiki kubyaza umusaruro aya mahirwe kugira ngo inzozi abaturage bari bafite mu myaka icumi ishize , zibe impamo .
Baharanire amahoro arambye n'iterambere . """"
Umuryango Mpuzamahanga na Kiir bararebana ay'ingwe
Nubwo amatora yitezwe mu 2023 ngo hatorwe undi uzasimbura Salva Kiir , benshi ntibizera ko ayo matora azaba .
Hari ababona ko kugira ngo Sudani y'Epfo igire amahoro , bizasaba ko Kiir ava ku butegetsi akajyana na Riek Machar .
Ibyo byifuzo ababifite babisangiye na Loni dore ko Raporo yatanzwe muri Mata 2021 y'inzobere za Loni kuri Sudani y'Epfo , yavuze ko """" Kiir na Machar bahindutse ikibazo kuri demokarasi , iterambere ry'ubukungu n'imibereho myiza muri Sudani y'Epfo . """"
Iryo tsinda ry'impuguke ryakomeje rivuga ko abo bayobozi bombi bakwiriye kuvaho """" kugira ngo igihugu kibone undi murongo mushya wa politiki hanakumirwe izindi mvururu . """"
Nubwo Loni isanga Kiir ari we kibazo muri Sudani y'Epfo , nyir'ubwite we asanga Umuryango mpuzamahanga ari wo utuma igihugu kidatera imbere .
Mu kiganiro aherutse kugirana n'umunyamakuru wa Citizen TV Kenya , Jeff Mwaura Koinange , Perezida Kiir yagize ati """" Ndananiwe , ariko ntabwo nanijwe n'abaturage , nanijwe n'umuryango mpuzamahanga .
Niyo mpamvu mfite ba Visi Perezida batanu .
Njya kubona nkabona n'umuntu utarigeze arasa na rimwe , baramuzanye ngo ari mu masezerano y'amahoro . """"
Umunyamakuru yahise abaza Kiir impamvu bakora ibyo badashaka akabyemera , ati """" Nagira nte se ?
Ndabareka bagakora icyo bashaka . Ubu se iyo ufashe inka ukayijyana mu ibagiro , yatera amahane .
Niko bakora , bo icyo bashaka ni ukumvana ku butegetsi . """"
Kubera imvururu n'intambara , Loni yafatiye Sudani y'Epfo ibihano birimo iby'ubukungu , kutemererwa kugura intwaro , gufatira imitungo ya bamwe mu bashinjwa uruhare mu mvururu no kubabuza gukorera ingendo mu mahanga .
Ibyo byakomye mu nkokora iterambere ry'icyo gihugu .
Bishobora kuba ari nabyo bituma icyo gihugu kitagira igisirikare gikomeye cyabasha guhangana n'imitwe yitwaje intwaro .
Abaturage ntibizeye umutekano utangwa na Leta , ari yo mpamvu imbunda n'izindi ntwaro zinyanyagiye mu baturage zikanifashishwa iyo habaye imvururu zishingiye ku moko cyangwa ibindi .
Perezida Salva Kiir yavuze ko izo ntwaro bigoye kuzimara mu baturage , ngo keretse bahawe ingengo y'imari bakazibagurira .
Ati """" Niba umuntu yaragiye akagurisha inka ze akigurira imbunda ngo yirinde , ntabwo yapfa kuyitanga .
Twe twumva ko kugira ngo ibyemejwe mu masezerano bigerweho , bizasaba ko dutekereza uburyo abaturage bamburwa intwaro .
Bizakunda ari uko tubahaye amafaranga , tukazigura . """"
Hari ababona impamvu ibintu byazambye muri Sudani y'Epfo , ari uko Kiir asa n'uwaguweho n'ubutegetsi , akabufata atiteguye .
The Sudan People's Liberation Army , umutwe w'ingabo warwaniye ubwigenge bwa Sudani y'Epfo washinzwe mu 1983 na John Garang .
Garang yari afite impamyabumenyi y'ikirenga ( Phd ) mu bukungu bushingiye ku buhinzi yakuye muri Iowa State University .
Yari azi kureshya amahanga kugira ngo yemere impamvu yatumye bafata intwaro , ari nabyo byabagejeje ku bwigenge .
Mu 2005 , Garang yasinye amasezerano y'amahoro na Guverinoma ya Sudani ari nayo yabanzirizaga ubwigenge .
Yaje kugirwa Visi Perezida wa Guverinoma y'inzibacyuho ya Sudani , hashize iminsi agwa mu mpanuka ya kajugujugu .
Inyeshyamba za Garang zisanze mu ihurizo ryo gushaka umusimbura , bagena Salva Kiir wari umusirikare mukuru umenyereye ibyo kurwana , udafite amashuri menshi n'ubunararibonye muri politiki .
Mu gihe Garang yari azi kureshya amahanga no gutera ibipindi , Kiiir we yaje ari umuntu ucecetse .
Ikinyamakuru Foreign Policy giherutse gutangaza ko hari inama yigeze guhuza Kiir na George W Bush wayoboraga Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , gusobanura neza ibibazo byabo biramunanira biba ngombwa ko havuga abaminisitiri be .
Bush wakundaga cyane Garang , yabaye nk'utishimira politiki ya Kiir , gusa ibintu byarushijeho kuzamba ku ngoma ya Barrack Obama , ubwo Amerika yamenyaga ko Sudani y'Epfo yaba itera inkunga imitwe y'inyeshyamba irwanya Sudani .
Salva Kiir nubwo avuga ko ananizwa , ntatanga umuti uhamye w'icyakorwa ngo imvururu zihoshe mu gihugu cye .
Gusa yizera ko mu myaka icumi iri imbere , Sudani y'Epfo izaba imeze neza .
Ati """" Abaturage ba Sudani y'Epfo nibemera ko amahoro aganza , mu myaka icumi iri imbere kizaba ari igihugu kidasanzwe .
Nibatongera kurwana , nyuma y'imyaka icumi kizaba ari igihugu . """"
Icyakora , Kiir avuga ko hari """" Hari abantu bakinyotewe n'amaraso , bashaka kubona abantu bapfa muri Sudani y'Epfo . """"
Kuba Minisitiri w'Intebe , uko yahunze n'abamusabye kugambanira igihugu - Ikiganiro na Dr Rwigema Pierre - Célestin .
Ubu afite imyaka 68 y'amavuko .
Yabaye Minisitiri w'Intebe muri Guverinoma yari iyobowe na Pasiteri Bizimungu hagati ya 1995 na 2000 mbere yaho yabaye Minisitiri w'Uburezi mu gihe cy'umwaka umwe [ 1994 - 1995 ] .
Ni Umudepite uhagarariye u Rwanda mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko ya Afurika y'Iburasirazuba [ EALA ] . Mbere ya Jenoside yari Umuyoboke wa MDR .
Mu 2001 , yaje gushinjwa kugira uruhare muri Jenoside , hashize iminsi mike yeguye ku mwanya wa Minisitiri w'Intebe .
Byatumye ahunga ava mu Rwanda ajya muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , ashaka ubuhungiro nk'umunyapoltiki .
Muri icyo gihe yarimo akomereza amasomo ya Masters muri Bowling Green State University muri Leta ya Ohio .
Ihunga rye ryavuzweho byinshi ndetse bivugwa ko yageze iyo imahanga akareshywa n'abantu b'ingeri zitandukanye kugira ngo yiyunge ku barwanya FPR Inkotanyi .
Ibi byose ni byo yagarutseho mu kiganiro kirambuye yagiranye na IGIHE .
IGIHE : Waba wibuka uko winjiye muri Politiki n'icyabiteye ?
Dr Rwigema : Inkundura y'amashyaka ije , ntabwo nabigiyemo .
No muri MRND baje kunsaba kujyamo ndanga , gusa naje kurushwa imbaraga n'uko icyo kintu cyari gikomeye i Gitarama aho nkomoka , barantumira kugira ngo njyemo ndanga , mbanza kubaha icyo nakwita ubufasha , bageze aho bati """" amafaranga ntabwo tuyashaka ni wowe dushaka . """"
Mbura uko mbigenza , nemera kujya mu nzego zikomeye z'ishyaka rikomeye iwacu , dutangira tuvuga ko tugiye kurwanya Habyarimana , kandi akomeye ariko twe nta n'imbaraga dufite ; nta mbunda twagiraga [ . . . ] .
Ni uko ngiye iwacu muri Kigoma bahita bantora mu nzego , bigeze kuri Perefegitura ngira ngo nabaye uwa gatatu .
Ni uko ninjiye muri politiki .
Hari n'abavuga ko wigeze kwigumura kuri Habyarimana ; ni ukuri ?
Mu 1993 , Habyarimana yabonye ko opozisiyo ikomeye , ahitamo kugira ngo abikatemo kabiri , ari na bwo bamwe yabahaga icyo nakwita nk'ubushobozi cyangwa amafaranga , barabagura abandi turanga .
Ndibuka ko muri kongere yabereye i Gitarama , nafashe ijambo mbabwira ko ntashobora kubyemera , ndasohoka , ikindi gipande kinini kirankurikira .
Ni uko byacitsemo kabiri , noneho rero abantu batangira guhigana .
Ubwo icyo gihe hari abagiye ku ruhande rw'Inkotanyi . . .
Hari abashyigikiye Habyarimana abandi tuvuga rumwe n'Inkotanyi , abantu batangira guhigana hagati yabo kuko ibyo twari twaremeranyije nka Demokarasi bamwe basa nk'aho bagambaniye abandi kubera ko ubutegetsi bwabaciyemo kabiri .
Wabaye Minisitiri w'Uburezi wa mbere nyuma ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi ; usobanura ute uko izo nshingano zari zimeze ?
Kuba Minisitiri w'Uburezi nyuma ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 ni nk'inzozi kuko nanjye iyo nsubije amaso inyuma hari igihe nibaza uko nabikoze ariko narabikoze .
Mu 1994 kukubaza umubare w'abanyeshuri , abarimu bari mu gihugu noneho hagakubiraho n'uko u Rwanda rwarimo rwakira ababyeyi bazanye n'abana babo bavuye muri Kenya bize mu cyongereza , bavuye muri Tanzania bize mu Kiswahili , bavuye muri Uganda bize mu Cyongereza , abavuye muri Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo bize mu Gifaransa abavuye i Burundi
bize mu Gifaransa n'abari basanzwe mu Rwanda bize mu Kinyarwanda ntabwo byari byoroshye .
Ndakubwiye ni ikizamini kimwe n'ibindi .
Twatangije amashuri muri Nzeri mu 1994 , nakoze gahunda nyijyanye no muri guverinoma kugira ngo ize kubyemera byafashe igihe , bumvaga bidashoboka .
Ndabasobanurira hanyuma barambwira bati wabaye woroheje ?
Ndababwira nti ariko ndakeka ko dukwiye kugerageza kuko ababyeyi n'abana n'iki gihugu gikwiye kongera kugira icyizere cyo kubaho .
Ni bande bari bagushyigikiye icyo gihe mu bari muri Guverinoma ?
Perezida wa Repubulika [ Perezida Kagame ] ari mu banshyigikiye cyane , aravuga ati mumureke agerageze kuko nanjye nari maze kuvuga nti mureke ngerageze nibyanga njyane na byo mushyireho undi .
Ni iki wihutiye gukora ?
Natangije amashuri , icyo gihe hari Perefegitura , natangiriye mu Ruhengeri , icyo gihe yayoborwaga n'uwitwaga Kagiraneza Deus , nkora ku buryo tumenya ibigo byashobokaga kugira ngo bitangire , noneho aho tudafite abarimu tugashyiramo n'abanyeshuri barangizaga bashoboraga kwigisha .
Za UNICEF zirahurura , za GIZ mbese imiryango itari iya leta yose n'abanyamakuru baza kureba uburyo ibyo bintu bizahaho .
Ibigo bitandatu byose turatangira barigisha , bigenda neza .
Mwakurikijeho he ?
Umunsi wa kabiri tubikora i Byumba , hayoborwaga na Colonel Lizinde Théoneste na Musenyeri we ukinariho baradufashije cyane , tubikora kimwe n'uko twabikoze mu Ruhengeri , umunsi wa Gatatu tujya i Kibungo hari umugabo w'umukozi witwa Musoni Protais na Musenyeri Rubwejanga .
Rubwejanga yari n'inshuti yanjye na bo turakorana turabipanga birakora , umunsi wa kane tujya i Gitarama , tubikora uko twabikoze mu ntangiriro .
Ubwo byakirwaga gute hanze aha ?
Ku munsi wa Gatanu ari na ho Inama ya Guverinoma yabaga , inkuru yari yasakaye Isi yose , bati ya Guverinoma itaranamara n'amezi abiri yakoze igikorwa cy'indashyikirwa , yatangije amashuri .
Noneho ndakomeza , ni uko byagenze .
Nyuma y'umwaka umwe wahise ugirwa Minisitiri w'Intebe . . .
Ukurikije amasezerano ya Arusha , bavugaga ko Minisitiri w'Intebe azaturuka muri MDR , Twagiramungu yari yanditse muri ayo masezerano , Twagiramungu rero amaze kunanirwa inshingano , arasezera , bagombaga gushaka umuntu umusimbura .
Bashatse umuntu umusimbura rero ntabwo bari gusaba iryo shyaka ngo ribahe umuntu kanaka , byari bikomeye .
